    <div id="editHistoryModal" style="display:none;position:fixed;inset:0;z-index:10050;background:rgba(0,0,0,.55);backdrop-filter:blur(4px);align-items:center;justify-content:center;padding:24px;">

    <script>
        // ========================================
        // LOCAL DEVELOPMENT MODE CONFIGURATION
        // ========================================
        // Set to true to bypass SharePoint and use fake data
        // Set to false for production SharePoint integration
        if (typeof Chart !== 'undefined') Chart.defaults.plugins.datalabels = { display: false };
const LOCAL_DEV_MODE = false;

        // Development user profile (only used when LOCAL_DEV_MODE = true)
        const DEV_USER_PROFILE = {
            // Change this to test different roles:
            // 'Admin', 'Account Manager', 'Account Director', 'Line Manager', 'Service Manager'
            role: 'Admin',

            // User details (customize as needed)
            email: 'dev.user@duservicemanagement.com',
            name: 'Development User',

            // Optional: For LM/SM roles, specify which manager name to filter by
            // For LM: specify the Line Manager name from fake data
            // For SM: specify the Service Manager name from fake data
            managerName: 'Sarah Johnson' // Used for LM/SM filtering
        };

        // ========================================
        // EXISTING CODE CONTINUES
        // ========================================
        const SP_URL = 'http://sharedspaces:8086/sites/SM';
        const SP_LIST = 'Service Manager Request';
        const SP_ACCESS_LIST = 'Access_Control';
        const SP_MAPPING_LIST = 'Account Mapping';

        let ALL_DATA = [];
        let filtered = [];
        let SM_MAPPING_DATA = [];
        let DOJ_DATA = {}; // keyed by SM name → {doj, tenure}
        let selectedLM = null;
        let selectedSM = null;
let charts = {};

        // ══ ANALYTICS LAZY-LOAD STATE ══════════════════════════════
        window.ANALYTICS_LOADED = false;
        window.RNPS_CACHE = {};    // '_grouped_LMName' → raw grouped; 'LMName' → computed quarters
        window.ETA_LOADED  = false;

        async function loadAnalytics() {
            const btn     = document.getElementById('loadAnalyticsBtn');
            const btnText = document.getElementById('loadAnalyticsBtnText');

            // If already loaded — just refresh renders
            if (window.ANALYTICS_LOADED) {
                await renderLineManagers();
                await renderServiceManagers();
                return;
            }

            // ── Show loading state ─────────────────────────────────
            if (btn) {
                btn.disabled = true;
                btn.style.opacity = '.75';
                btn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="loader" style="width:15px;height:15px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;animation:spin 1s linear infinite;margin-right:6px;"></i><span>Loading RNPS &amp; ETA...</span>';
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
            }

            try {
                // ── 1. Collect which LMs to fetch RNPS for ────────
                let lms = [...new Set(ALL_DATA.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean);
                if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager') {
                    lms = lms.filter(l => l === USER_CONTEXT.userName);
                } else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') {
                    const myLM = ALL_DATA.find(a => a.sm === USER_CONTEXT.userName)?.lm;
                    lms = myLM ? [myLM] : [];
                } else if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) {
                    const tsmData = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE');
                    lms = [...new Set(tsmData.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean);
                }

                // ── 2. Fetch RNPS for all LMs in parallel ─────────
                await Promise.all(lms.map(async lm => {
                    try {
                        const grouped = await fetchRNPSForLM(lm);
                        window.RNPS_CACHE['_grouped_' + lm] = grouped;   // for SM drill-down
                        window.RNPS_CACHE[lm] = computeLMRNPS(grouped);  // for LM tile
                    } catch(e) { console.warn('[RNPS] Failed for', lm, e); }
                }));

                // ── 3. Load ETA data ───────────────────────────────
              if (typeof etaLoadSPData === 'function' &&
    (!window.ETA_STATE || !window.ETA_STATE.allData || !window.ETA_STATE.allData.tts)) {
    await new Promise(function(resolve) {
        var run = async function() { await etaLoadSPData(); resolve(); };
        if (typeof requestIdleCallback === 'function') {
            requestIdleCallback(function() { run(); }, { timeout: 5000 });
        } else {
            setTimeout(run, 0);
        }
    });
}
                window.ETA_LOADED = true;
                window.ANALYTICS_LOADED = true;

                // ── 4. Update button → loaded ──────────────────────
                if (btn) {
                    btn.disabled = false;
                    btn.style.opacity = '1';
                    btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#10b981,#059669)';
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="check-circle" style="width:15px;height:15px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:6px;"></i><span>Analytics Loaded — Refresh</span>';
                    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
                }

                // ── 5. Re-render with real data ────────────────────
                await renderLineManagers();
                await renderServiceManagers();

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('[loadAnalytics]', err);
                if (btn) {
                    btn.disabled = false;
                    btn.style.opacity = '1';
                    btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#dc2626)';
                    btn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="alert-triangle" style="width:15px;height:15px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:6px;"></i><span>Error — Retry</span>';
                    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
                }
            }
        }
        function toggleCharts() {
            const chartsSection = document.getElementById('chartsSection');
            const icon = document.getElementById('chartsIcon');
            const text = document.getElementById('chartsText');

            if (chartsSection.style.display === 'none') {
                chartsSection.style.display = 'grid';
                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'eye-off');
                text.textContent = 'Hide Analytics Charts';
            } else {
                chartsSection.style.display = 'none';
                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'eye');
                text.textContent = 'Show Analytics Charts';
            }

            lucide.createIcons();
        }

        function setCurrentDate() {
            const now = new Date();
            const options = {
                weekday: 'long',
                year: 'numeric',
                month: 'long',
                day: 'numeric'
            };
            document.getElementById('currentDate').textContent = now.toLocaleDateString('en-US', options);
        }

        async function fetchRevenueEnabled() {
            try {
                const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_ACCESS_LIST + "')/items?" +
                    "$select=ID,UserEmailID,RevenueEnabled&" +
                    "$filter=(UserEmailID eq 'ubaid.mir@du.ae' or UserEmailID eq 'tehleel.lone@du.ae')&$top=2";
                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });
                if (!res.ok) return;
                const data = await res.json();
                const results = data.d.results;
                window.REVENUE_ENABLED = results.some(r => {
                    const val = r.RevenueEnabled;
                    if (!val) return false;
                    if (val === true || val === 'Yes') return true;
                    if (val.results) return val.results.includes('Yes');
                    return false;
                });
                window.REVENUE_CONTROL_ITEMS = results; // store both rows for update later
                console.log('[RevenueEnabled]', window.REVENUE_ENABLED);
                updateRevenueToggleBtn();
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('fetchRevenueEnabled failed:', e);
                window.REVENUE_ENABLED = false;
            }
        }

        async function toggleRevenueEnabled() {
            try {
                const newValue = !window.REVENUE_ENABLED;
                const items = window.REVENUE_CONTROL_ITEMS || [];
                if (items.length === 0) {
                    alert('Control rows not found');
                    return;
                }

                // Get digest once
                const digestRes = await fetch(SP_URL + '/_api/contextinfo', {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });
                if (!digestRes.ok) throw new Error('Failed to get digest');
                const digest = (await digestRes.json()).d.GetContextWebInformation.FormDigestValue;

                // Update BOTH rows
                for (const item of items) {
                    const updateRes = await fetch(SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_ACCESS_LIST + "')/items(" + item.ID + ")", {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose',
                            'Content-Type': 'application/json;odata=verbose',
                            'X-RequestDigest': digest,
                            'IF-MATCH': '*',
                            'X-HTTP-Method': 'MERGE'
                        },
                        credentials: 'include',
                        body: JSON.stringify({
                            __metadata: {
                                type: 'SP.Data.Access_x005f_ControlListItem'
                            },
                            RevenueEnabled: {
                                __metadata: {
                                    type: 'Collection(Edm.String)'
                                },
                                results: newValue ? ['Yes'] : ['No']
                            }
                        })
                    });
                    if (!updateRes.ok) throw new Error('Update failed for ' + item.UserEmailID);
                }

                window.REVENUE_ENABLED = newValue;
                // Update both rows in memory too
                window.REVENUE_CONTROL_ITEMS = items.map(i => ({
                    ...i,
                    RevenueEnabled: newValue
                }));
                updateRevenueToggleBtn();
                console.log('[RevenueEnabled] updated to', newValue);
            } catch (e) {
                alert('Error updating revenue setting: ' + e.message);
            }
        }

        function updateRevenueToggleBtn() {
            const btn = document.getElementById('revenueToggleBtn');
            if (!btn) return;
            if (window.REVENUE_ENABLED) {
                btn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="unlock" style="width:14px;height:14px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:6px;"></i>Revenue: Enabled';
                btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#10b981,#059669)';
            } else {
                btn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="lock" style="width:14px;height:14px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:6px;"></i>Revenue: Disabled';
                btn.style.background = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#ef4444,#dc2626)';
            }
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        }
        async function fetchDOJData() {
            if (LOCAL_DEV_MODE) return; // skip in dev mode
            try {
                const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('DOJ')/items?$select=Title,DOJ,Status&$top=500";
                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    }
                });
                if (!res.ok) return;
                const data = await res.json();
                DOJ_DATA = {};
                (data.d.results || []).forEach(function(item) {
                    const name = (item.Title || '').trim();
                    if (!name || !item.DOJ) return;
                    const dojDate = new Date(item.DOJ);
                    const now = new Date();
                    const totalMonths = Math.floor((now - dojDate) / (1000 * 60 * 60 * 24 * 30.44));
                    const years = Math.floor(totalMonths / 12);
                    const months = totalMonths % 12;
                    const tenure = years > 0 ? (months > 0 ? years + 'y ' + months + 'm' : years + 'y') : months + 'm';
                    const dojFormatted = dojDate.toLocaleDateString('en-GB', {
                        month: 'short',
                        year: 'numeric'
                    });
                    DOJ_DATA[name] = {
                        doj: dojFormatted,
                        tenure: tenure
                    };
                });
                console.log('DOJ data loaded:', Object.keys(DOJ_DATA).length, 'records');
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('DOJ fetch failed:', e);
            }
        }

        async function fetchAccountMapping() {
            if (LOCAL_DEV_MODE) {
                const devNames = ['Ahmed Al-Mansouri', 'Fatima Hassan', 'Omar Abdullah', 'Layla Mohamed', 'Sarah Johnson', 'Michael Chen'];
                SM_MAPPING_DATA = devNames.map(function(name, idx) {
                    return {
                        name: name,
                        team: idx % 2 === 0 ? 'DSM' : 'TSM_ME',
                        email: name.toLowerCase().replace(/ /g, '.') + '@du.ae',
                        userId: String(100 + idx)
                    };
                });
                return;
            }
            try {
                const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_MAPPING_LIST + "')/items?" +
                    "$select=Service_Manager_Name,Email_ID,Team,User_ID,Status&$top=5000&$orderby=Service_Manager_Name asc";
                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });
                if (!res.ok) {
                    console.warn('Account Mapping fetch failed:', res.status);
                    return;
                }
                const data = await res.json();
                const seen = {};
                SM_MAPPING_DATA = [];
                (data.d.results || []).forEach(function(item) {
                    const name = (item.Service_Manager_Name || '').trim();
                    if (!name) return;
                    const key = name + '|' + (item.Team || '');
                    if (seen[key]) return;
                    seen[key] = true;
                    SM_MAPPING_DATA.push({
                        name: name,
                        team: item.Team || '',
                        email: item.Email_ID || '',
                        userId: item.User_ID || '',
                        status: item.Status || ''
                    });
                });
                SM_MAPPING_DATA.sort(function(a, b) { return a.name.localeCompare(b.name); });
                console.log('Account Mapping loaded:', SM_MAPPING_DATA.length, 'records');
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('Account Mapping fetch failed:', e);
            }
        }

        function smNormalizePersonName(name) {
            return (name || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
        }

        async function smResolvePersonId(name) {
            const norm = smNormalizePersonName(name);
            if (!norm) return null;

            const mapped = SM_MAPPING_DATA.find(function(a) {
                return smNormalizePersonName(a.name) === norm;
            });
            if (mapped && mapped.userId) {
                const uid = parseInt(String(mapped.userId).trim(), 10);
                if (!isNaN(uid) && uid > 0) return uid;
            }

            if (typeof getUserId === 'function') {
                const byTitle = await getUserId(name);
                if (byTitle) return byTitle;
            }

            if (mapped && mapped.email) {
                const eUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/siteusers?$filter=Email eq '" + mapped.email.replace(/'/g, "''") + "'&$select=Id&$top=1";
                const eRes = await fetch(eUrl, { headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' }, credentials: 'include' });
                if (eRes.ok) {
                    const eData = await eRes.json();
                    if (eData.d.results && eData.d.results.length > 0) return eData.d.results[0].Id;
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        async function smPatchListItem(itemId, digest, fields) {
            const updateUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items(" + itemId + ")";
            const res = await fetch(updateUrl, {
                method: 'POST',
                headers: {
                    'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose',
                    'Content-Type': 'application/json;odata=verbose',
                    'X-RequestDigest': digest,
                    'IF-MATCH': '*',
                    'X-HTTP-Method': 'MERGE'
                },
                credentials: 'include',
                body: JSON.stringify(Object.assign({
                    __metadata: { type: 'SP.Data.Service_x0020_Manager_x0020_RequestListItem' }
                }, fields))
            });
            if (!res.ok) {
                const errorText = await res.text();
                throw new Error('Update failed: ' + errorText);
            }
        }

        window.smSecondarySmSearch = function(q) {
            const dd = document.getElementById('editSecondarySMDD');
            if (!dd) return;
            const lower = (q || '').toLowerCase();
            const pool = SM_MAPPING_DATA.slice();
            const results = lower
                ? pool.filter(function(a) {
                    return a.name.toLowerCase().indexOf(lower) >= 0 ||
                        (a.team || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(lower) >= 0 ||
                        (a.email || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(lower) >= 0;
                })
                : pool.slice(0, 40);

            dd.innerHTML = '';
            if (!results.length) {
                dd.innerHTML = '<div class="sm-person-item" style="color:var(--t3);font-size:.82rem;">No service managers found</div>';
                dd.style.display = 'block';
                return;
            }
            const clearItem = document.createElement('div');
            clearItem.className = 'sm-person-item';
            clearItem.style.color = 'var(--t3)';
            clearItem.textContent = '— Clear Secondary SM —';
            clearItem.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                smClearSecondarySm();
            });
            dd.appendChild(clearItem);
            results.forEach(function(a) {
                const item = document.createElement('div');
                item.className = 'sm-person-item';
                item.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:.83rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--t1);">' + a.name + '</div>' +
                    '<div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--t3);">' + (a.team || '') + (a.email ? ' · ' + a.email : '') + '</div>';
                item.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    smSelectSecondarySm(a.name, a.team);
                });
                dd.appendChild(item);
            });
            dd.style.display = 'block';
        };

        window.smSelectSecondarySm = function(name, team) {
            const hidden = document.getElementById('editSecondarySM');
            const inp = document.getElementById('editSecondarySMInput');
            const dd = document.getElementById('editSecondarySMDD');
            const tag = document.getElementById('editSecondarySMTag');
            const normalized = smNormalizePersonName(name);
            if (hidden) hidden.value = normalized;
            if (inp) inp.value = '';
            if (dd) dd.style.display = 'none';
            if (tag) {
                if (!normalized) {
                    tag.innerHTML = '';
                    tag.style.display = 'none';
                    return;
                }
                tag.innerHTML = '<span style="display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:.35rem;background:var(--nab);border:1px solid var(--nab2);border-radius:20px;padding:.22rem .65rem;font-size:.78rem;font-weight:600;color:var(--acc);">' +
                    normalized + (team ? ' <span style="font-size:.65rem;opacity:.7;">(' + team + ')</span>' : '') +
                    '<span style="cursor:pointer;margin-left:.2rem;font-size:.95rem;" onclick="smClearSecondarySm()">×</span></span>';
                tag.style.display = 'block';
            }
        };

        window.smClearSecondarySm = function() {
            smSelectSecondarySm('', '');
        };

        function smSecondarySmEditHtml() {
            return '<div class="edit-field-card">' +
                '<div class="edit-field-label">Secondary SM</div>' +
                '<div class="sm-person-wrap">' +
                    '<input type="text" id="editSecondarySMInput" class="filter-select" placeholder="Search service manager..." style="font-size:14px;padding:10px;width:100%;cursor:text;" autocomplete="off" ' +
                    'oninput="smSecondarySmSearch(this.value)" onfocus="smSecondarySmSearch(this.value)" ' +
                    'onblur="setTimeout(function(){var d=document.getElementById(\'editSecondarySMDD\');if(d)d.style.display=\'none\';},250)">' +
                    '<div id="editSecondarySMDD" class="sm-person-dd"></div>' +
                '</div>' +
                '<div id="editSecondarySMTag" style="display:none;margin-top:.35rem;"></div>' +
                '<input type="hidden" id="editSecondarySM" value="">' +
            '</div>';
        }

async function fetchRNPSForLM(lmName) {
    try {
        const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('RNPSScores')/items?" +
            "$select=Period,ServiceManager,ResponseRate,RNPS,ResponseTarget,RNPSTarget&" +
            "$filter=LineManager eq '" + lmName.replace(/'/g, "''") + "'&" +
            "$top=500";
        const res = await fetch(url, {
            headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
            credentials: 'include'
        });
        if (!res.ok) return {};
        const data = await res.json();
        const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
        const validQuarters = ['Q1-' + currentYear, 'Q2-' + currentYear, 'Q3-' + currentYear, 'Q4-' + currentYear];

        const grouped = {};
        (data.d.results || []).forEach(row => {
            if (!validQuarters.includes(row.Period)) return;
            const sm = (row.ServiceManager || '').trim();
            if (!sm) return;
            if (!grouped[sm]) grouped[sm] = [];
            grouped[sm].push(row);
        });
        return grouped;
    } catch (e) {
        console.warn('fetchRNPSForLM failed:', e);
        return {};
    }
}

// ── ETA TILE HELPERS ──────────────────────────────────────────

function etaGetCurrentYearData(arr) {
    var currentYear = new Date().getFullYear().toString();
    return (arr || []).filter(function(r) { return r.Year === currentYear; });
}

function etaClassifyTT(r) {
    var s = r.TT_STATUS || '';
    if (['Closed','Resolved'].includes(s)) return 'completed';
    if (['Assigned','In Queue','Pending','Pending For Closure'].includes(s)) return 'assigned';
    if (['Open','In Progress'].includes(s)) return 'inprogress';
    return 'other';
}

function etaClassifyEvent(r) {
    var s = r.STATUS || '';
    if (['Completed','Closed'].includes(s)) return 'completed';
    if (['Open','In Queue'].includes(s)) return 'assigned';
    if (['In Progress','Escalated','Pending'].includes(s)) return 'inprogress';
    return 'other';
}

function etaClassifyActivity(r) {
    var s = r.ACTIVITY_STATUS || '';
    if (s === 'Done') return 'completed';
    if (['Assigned','Unassigned'].includes(s)) return 'assigned';
    if (['In Progress','Open'].includes(s)) return 'inprogress';
    return 'other';
}

function etaGetManagerStats(filterFn) {
    if (!ETA_STATE.allData) return null;

    var tts        = etaGetCurrentYearData(ETA_STATE.allData.tts).filter(filterFn);
    var events     = etaGetCurrentYearData(ETA_STATE.allData.events).filter(filterFn);
    var activities = etaGetCurrentYearData(ETA_STATE.allData.activities).filter(filterFn);

    function countBy(arr, classifyFn) {
        var counts = { assigned: 0, inprogress: 0, completed: 0, other: 0, total: 0 };
        arr.forEach(function(r) {
            var c = classifyFn(r);
            counts[c]++;
            counts.total++;
        });
        return counts;
    }

    // Detailed breakdown for (i) popup
    function detailBy(arr, statusField) {
        var map = {};
        arr.forEach(function(r) {
            var s = r[statusField] || 'Unknown';
            map[s] = (map[s] || 0) + 1;
        });
        return map;
    }

    return {
        tt:         countBy(tts, etaClassifyTT),
        events:     countBy(events, etaClassifyEvent),
        activities: countBy(activities, etaClassifyActivity),
        ttDetail:   detailBy(tts, 'TT_STATUS'),
        evDetail:   detailBy(events, 'STATUS'),
        actDetail:  detailBy(activities, 'ACTIVITY_STATUS')
    };
}

function etaStatsTileHtml(stats, title) {
    if (!stats) {
        return `<div class="lm-tile" style="cursor:default;opacity:.7;">
            <div class="lm-header"><h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">${title}</h3>
            <div class="lm-meta">ETA data loading...</div></div>
        </div>`;
    }

    var currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();

    function statRow(label, s) {
        return `
        <div style="margin-bottom:6px;">
            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:3px;">
                <span style="font-size:.65rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--t2);">${label}</span>
                <span style="font-size:.65rem;color:var(--t3);">Total: ${s.total}</span>
            </div>
            <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:3px;">
                <div style="background:rgba(245,158,11,.12);border:1px solid rgba(245,158,11,.3);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                    <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#b45309;font-weight:600;">Assigned</div>
                    <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#f59e0b;">${s.assigned}</div>
                </div>
                <div style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.12);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.3);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                    <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#1d4ed8;font-weight:600;">In Prog</div>
                    <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#3b82f6;">${s.inprogress}</div>
                </div>
                <div style="background:rgba(16,185,129,.12);border:1px solid rgba(16,185,129,.3);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                    <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#065f46;font-weight:600;">Done</div>
                    <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#10b981;">${s.completed}</div>
                </div>
                <div style="background:rgba(107,114,128,.12);border:1px solid rgba(107,114,128,.3);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                    <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:var(--t3);font-weight:600;">Other</div>
                    <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--t3);">${s.other}</div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>`;
    }

    return `
    <div class="lm-tile" style="cursor:default;border-color:var(--border-s);min-width:220px;">
        <div class="lm-header" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;">
                <h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">${title}</h3>
                <span style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--t3);font-weight:500;">${currentYear}</span>
                <div style="position:relative;display:inline-block;">
                    <span id="etaInfoBtn_${title.replace(/\s/g,'_')}"
                        onclick="etaShowInfoPopup(event,'${title.replace(/\s/g,'_')}')"
                        style="cursor:pointer;width:18px;height:18px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--bg-secondary);border:1px solid var(--border);display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:.65rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--acc);">i</span>
                    <div id="etaInfoPopup_${title.replace(/\s/g,'_')}" 
                        style="display:none;position:absolute;right:0;top:24px;z-index:999;background:var(--bg-card);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.2);padding:10px 12px;min-width:220px;max-width:260px;">
                        <div style="font-size:.7rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--t1);margin-bottom:6px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);padding-bottom:4px;">Detailed Breakdown</div>
                        ${etaDetailHtml('TTs', stats.ttDetail)}
                        ${etaDetailHtml('Events', stats.evDetail)}
                        ${etaDetailHtml('Activities', stats.actDetail)}
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
            <div class="lm-meta">ETA Data — Current Year</div>
        </div>
        ${statRow('Trouble Tickets', stats.tt)}
        ${statRow('Events', stats.events)}
        ${statRow('Activities', stats.activities)}
    </div>`;
}

function etaDetailHtml(label, detailMap) {
    var entries = Object.entries(detailMap).sort(function(a,b){ return b[1]-a[1]; });
    if (!entries.length) return `<div style="font-size:.68rem;color:var(--t3);margin-bottom:6px;">${label}: No data</div>`;
    return `
    <div style="margin-bottom:8px;">
        <div style="font-size:.65rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--acc);margin-bottom:3px;">${label}</div>
        ${entries.map(function(e) {
            return `<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:.65rem;padding:1px 0;">
                <span style="color:var(--t2);">${e[0]}</span>
                <span style="font-weight:700;color:var(--t1);">${e[1]}</span>
            </div>`;
        }).join('')}
    </div>`;
}

// Close info popups when clicking outside
document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (!e.target.closest('[id^="etaInfoBtn_"]') && !e.target.closest('[id^="etaInfoPopup_"]')) {
        document.querySelectorAll('[id^="etaInfoPopup_"]').forEach(function(p) {
            p.style.display = 'none';
        });
    }
});

window.etaShowInfoPopup = function(e, key) {
    e.stopPropagation();
    // Close all other popups first
    document.querySelectorAll('[id^="etaInfoPopup_"]').forEach(function(p) {
        p.style.display = 'none';
    });
    var popup = document.getElementById('etaInfoPopup_' + key);
    if (popup) popup.style.display = popup.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
};
function computeLMRNPS(rnpsGrouped) {
    // rnpsGrouped is { smName: [rows], ... } — flatten and average by period
    const byPeriod = {};
    Object.values(rnpsGrouped).forEach(rows => {
        rows.forEach(row => {
            if (!byPeriod[row.Period]) byPeriod[row.Period] = [];
            byPeriod[row.Period].push(row);
        });
    });

    const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
    const validQuarters = ['Q1-' + currentYear, 'Q2-' + currentYear, 'Q3-' + currentYear, 'Q4-' + currentYear];

    const result = [];
    validQuarters.forEach(q => {
        if (!byPeriod[q] || byPeriod[q].length === 0) return;
        const rows = byPeriod[q];
        const count = rows.length;
        result.push({
            Period: q,
            ResponseRate: parseFloat((rows.reduce((s, r) => s + (r.ResponseRate || 0), 0) / count).toFixed(1)),
            RNPS: parseFloat((rows.reduce((s, r) => s + (r.RNPS || 0), 0) / count).toFixed(1)),
            ResponseTarget: rows[0].ResponseTarget,
            RNPSTarget: rows[0].RNPSTarget
        });
    });
    return result;
}
        function parseChoiceField(raw) {
            if (raw === null || raw === undefined) return '';
            if (typeof raw === 'object') {
                if (Array.isArray(raw)) return raw.length ? parseChoiceField(raw[0]) : '';
                return raw.Label || raw.Value || raw.Title || '';
            }
            return String(raw).replace(/\u00a0/g, ' ').trim();
        }

        async function fetchData() {
            // ===== LOCAL DEV MODE: Return fake data =====
            if (LOCAL_DEV_MODE) {
                console.log('🎭 LOCAL DEV MODE: Using fake data');
                return generateFakeData();
            }

            // ===== EXISTING SHAREPOINT DATA FETCH =====
            const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                "$select=ID,Title,Parent_x0020_Code,Customer_x0020_Name,Team," +
                "Proposed_x0020_Team,Transfer_Request_Date," +
                "Line_x0020_Manager/Title,Line_x0020_Manager/EMail," +
                "Service_x0020_Manager/Title,Service_x0020_Manager/EMail," +
                "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma/Title,Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma/EMail," +
                "Account_x0020_Manager/Title,Account_x0020_Manager/EMail," +
                "Account_x0020_Director/Title,Account_x0020_Director/EMail," +
                "POC_x0020_Name,POC_x0020_Email_x0020_ID,POC_x0020_Contact_x0020_No," +
                "Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Name,Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Email,Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Contac," +
                "Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Name,Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Email,Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Contac," +
                "AccountType,RNPS_Eligibility," +
                // 2025 months
                "Oct_x002d_25,Nov_x002d_25,Dec_x002d_25," +
                // 2026 months
                "Jan_x002d_26,Feb_x002d_26,Mar_x002d_26,Apr_x002d_26,May_x002d_26,Jun_x002d_26," +
                "Jul_x002d_26,Aug_x002d_26,Sep_x002d_26,Oct_x002d_26,Nov_x002d_26,Dec_x002d_26," +
                "Request_x0020_Status,Request_x0020_Type,Reject_New_Account_Reason&" +
                "$expand=Line_x0020_Manager,Service_x0020_Manager,Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma,Account_x0020_Manager,Account_x0020_Director&" +
                "$top=10000";

            const res = await fetch(url, {
                headers: {
                    'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                },
                credentials: 'include'
            });

            if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed: ' + res.statusText);

            const data = await res.json();
            return data.d.results.map(item => {
                const isApproved = item.Request_x0020_Status === 'OnBoarded' || item.Request_x0020_Status === 'AM_Approved';

                // [NEW] Get last 3 completed months dynamically
                const lastThreeMonths = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();
                const monthRevenues = [];

                lastThreeMonths.forEach(month => {
                    const value = parseFloat(item[month.field]) || 0;
                    monthRevenues.push(value);
                });

                // Calculate average from last 3 months
                const avgRevenue = monthRevenues.length > 0 ?
                    monthRevenues.reduce((sum, val) => sum + val, 0) / monthRevenues.length :
                    0;

                const team = item.Team || '';
                const lastMonthValue = monthRevenues[2] || 0; // Most recent month

                // Calculate if revenue drop or upgrade (only for approved PARENT accounts)
                let isRevDrop = false;
                let isRevUpgrade = false;
                const isGroup = (item.Title === item.Parent_x0020_Code) || !item.Parent_x0020_Code;
                // NOTE: isRevDrop/isRevUpgrade will be recalculated after ALL data loads
                // using combined parent+children revenue. Set placeholder here.
                if (isApproved && isGroup) {
                    // Placeholder - real check done in recalculateRevFlags() after full load
                }
                const result = {
                    spItemId: item.ID || item.Id || null,
                    code: item.Title || '',
                    parent: item.Parent_x0020_Code || null,
                    customer: item.Customer_x0020_Name || '',
                    team: team,
                    lm: item.Line_x0020_Manager ? item.Line_x0020_Manager.Title : '',
                    sm: item.Service_x0020_Manager ? item.Service_x0020_Manager.Title : '',
                    secondarySm: item.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma ? item.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma.Title : '',
                    secondarySmEmail: item.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma ? (item.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma.EMail || '') : '',
                    am: item.Account_x0020_Manager ? item.Account_x0020_Manager.Title : '',
                    ad: item.Account_x0020_Director ? item.Account_x0020_Director.Title : '',
                    lmEmail: item.Line_x0020_Manager ? (item.Line_x0020_Manager.EMail || '') : '',
                    smEmail: item.Service_x0020_Manager ? (item.Service_x0020_Manager.EMail || '') : '',
                    amEmail: item.Account_x0020_Manager ? (item.Account_x0020_Manager.EMail || '') : '',
                    adEmail: item.Account_x0020_Director ? (item.Account_x0020_Director.EMail || '') : '',
                    proposedTeam: item.Proposed_x0020_Team || '',
                    transferRequestDate: item.Transfer_Request_Date ? new Date(item.Transfer_Request_Date) : null,
                    pocName: item.POC_x0020_Name || '',
                    pocEmail: item.POC_x0020_Email_x0020_ID || '',
                    pocPhone: item.POC_x0020_Contact_x0020_No || '',
                    secondaryPocName: item.Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Name || '',
                    secondaryPocEmail: item.Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Email || '',
                    secondaryPocPhone: item.Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Contac || '',
                    technicalPocName: item.Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Name || '',
                    technicalPocEmail: item.Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Email || '',
                    technicalPocPhone: item.Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Contac || '',
                    accountType: parseChoiceField(item.AccountType) || '',
                    rnpsEligibility: parseChoiceField(item.RNPS_Eligibility) || '',

                    // [NEW] Store last 3 months values with keys
                    [lastThreeMonths[0].key]: monthRevenues[0] || 0, // e.g., 'oct25'
                    [lastThreeMonths[1].key]: monthRevenues[1] || 0,
                    [lastThreeMonths[2].key]: monthRevenues[2] || 0,

                    avg: avgRevenue,
                    type: (item.Title === item.Parent_x0020_Code) ? 'Group' : 'Child',
                    isRevDrop: isRevDrop,
                    requestStatus: item.Request_x0020_Status || 'Not Onboarded',
                    requestType: item.Request_x0020_Type || 'New Account',
                    isApproved: isApproved,
                    isRevUpgrade: isRevUpgrade,
                    rejectReason: item.Reject_New_Account_Reason || '',
                    transferDaysPassed: item.Transfer_Request_Date ? Math.floor((new Date() - new Date(item.Transfer_Request_Date)) / 86400000) : null,

                    // [NEW] Store ALL month values for edit view
                    allMonths: {
                        'Oct_x002d_25': parseFloat(item.Oct_x002d_25) || 0,
                        'Nov_x002d_25': parseFloat(item.Nov_x002d_25) || 0,
                        'Dec_x002d_25': parseFloat(item.Dec_x002d_25) || 0,
                        'Jan_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Jan_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Feb_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Feb_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Mar_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Mar_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Apr_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Apr_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'May_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.May_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Jun_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Jun_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Jul_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Jul_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Aug_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Aug_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Sep_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Sep_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Oct_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Oct_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Nov_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Nov_x002d_26) || 0,
                        'Dec_x002d_26': parseFloat(item.Dec_x002d_26) || 0
                    }
                };

                return result;
            });
        }

        function recalculateRevFlags() {
            // For each Group account, sum its own revenue + all children's revenue
            ALL_DATA.forEach(account => {
                if (account.type !== 'Group') return;

                const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();
                const latestKey = lastThree[2].key;

                // Find all children
                const children = ALL_DATA.filter(a =>
                    a.type === 'Child' &&
                    a.parent === account.code &&
                    a.code !== account.code
                );

                // Combined latest month revenue
                const combinedLatest = (account[latestKey] || 0) +
                    children.reduce((sum, c) => sum + (c[latestKey] || 0), 0);

                account.isRevDrop = false;
                account.isRevUpgrade = false;

                if (!account.isApproved) return;

                const team = account.team;
                if (team === 'DSM' && combinedLatest < 50000) account.isRevDrop = true;
                if (team === 'TSM_ME' && combinedLatest < 10000) account.isRevDrop = true;
                if (team === 'TSM_SE' && combinedLatest >= 10000) account.isRevUpgrade = true;
                if (team === 'TSM_ME' && combinedLatest >= 50000) account.isRevUpgrade = true;

                // Store combined revenue for use in transfer form
                account.combinedLatestRev = combinedLatest;
            });
        }
        // ========================================
        // DYNAMIC REVENUE MONTH FUNCTIONS
        // ========================================

        /**
         * Get the last 3 COMPLETED months
         * Example: If today is Feb 15, 2026 → Returns [Nov-25, Dec-25, Jan-26]
         */
        function getLastThreeCompletedMonths() {
            const today = new Date();
            const months = [];

            for (let i = 3; i >= 1; i--) {
                const date = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() - i, 1);
                months.push(getMonthInfo(date));
            }

            return months;
        }

        /**
         * Get the PREVIOUS month (editable month)
         * Example: If today is Feb 15, 2026 → Returns Jan-26
         */
        function getPreviousMonth() {
            const today = new Date();
            const date = new Date(today.getFullYear(), today.getMonth() - 1, 1);
            return getMonthInfo(date);
        }

        /**
         * Get the CURRENT month
         */
        function getCurrentMonth() {
            const today = new Date();
            return getMonthInfo(today);
        }

        /**
         * Convert a Date object to month info
         */
        function getMonthInfo(date) {
            const monthNames = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun',
                'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'
            ];

            const monthName = monthNames[date.getMonth()];
            const year = date.getFullYear().toString().slice(-2); // "26"

            return {
                label: `${monthName}-${year}`, // "Jan-26"
                field: `${monthName}_x002d_${year}`, // "Jan_x002d_26"
                key: `${monthName.toLowerCase()}${year}`, // "jan26" (for storing in result object)
                date: date,
                month: date.getMonth(),
                year: date.getFullYear()
            };
        }

        /**
         * Check if deadline has passed for a given month
         * Deadline = Last day of the NEXT month
         * Example: Jan-26 deadline = Feb 28/29, 2026 23:59:59
         */
        function isDeadlinePassed(monthInfo) {
            const today = new Date();

            // Deadline = Last day of next month
            const deadlineMonth = monthInfo.month + 1; // Next month
            const deadlineYear = monthInfo.year;

            // Get last day of next month
            const lastDay = new Date(deadlineYear, deadlineMonth + 1, 0); // Day 0 = last day of previous month
            lastDay.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);

            return today > lastDay;
        }

        /**
         * Check if a month is locked (cannot edit)
         * Locked if: value > 0 OR deadline passed
         */
        function isMonthLocked(value, monthInfo) {
            if (window.REVENUE_ENABLED) return false; // override — always unlocked
            if (value > 0) return true;
            if (isDeadlinePassed(monthInfo)) return true;
            return false;
        }

        /**
         * Get revenue months for display/edit
         */
        function getRevenueMonthsForEdit() {
            const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();
            const previous = getPreviousMonth();
            const current = getCurrentMonth();

            // Check if previous month is still editable
            const canEditPrevious = !isDeadlinePassed(previous);

            return {
                lastThree: lastThree, // Array of 3 months (disabled)
                editable: canEditPrevious ? previous : null, // Single month or null
                current: current // For reference
            };
        }

        function normalizeSmRole(role) {
            if (!role) return 'none';
            var r = String(role).trim();
            if (r === 'PSD Admin') return 'PSD_Admin';
            if (r === 'PSD Agent') return 'PSD_Agent';
            return r;
        }
        function isPsdRole(role) {
            return role === 'PSD_Admin' || role === 'PSD_Agent';
        }
        function applyPsdNavRestrictions() {
            var psdAllowedLabels = [
                'Newsletter',
                'Events / TT / Activity',
                'Project Management',
                'Synergy 360',
                'Suggestion Box',
                'Process Documents',
                'Contact Us',
                'PSD Assignment'
            ];
            document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(function(item) {
                var labelEl = item.querySelector('.nav-label');
                var label = labelEl ? labelEl.textContent.trim() : '';
                item.style.display = (psdAllowedLabels.indexOf(label) >= 0) ? 'flex' : 'none';
            });
            document.querySelectorAll('.nav-section-label').forEach(function(lbl) {
                lbl.style.display = 'none';
            });
        }

        // ===== VISIT TRACKING =====
        function getVisitCount() {
            try {
                const visitCount = localStorage.getItem('sm_visit_count_' + USER_CONTEXT.userEmail);
                return visitCount ? parseInt(visitCount, 10) : 0;
            } catch (e) {
                return 0;
            }
        }

        function incrementVisitCount() {
            try {
                const currentCount = getVisitCount();
                const newCount = currentCount + 1;
                localStorage.setItem('sm_visit_count_' + USER_CONTEXT.userEmail, newCount.toString());
                return newCount;
            } catch (e) {
                return 1;
            }
        }

        function getLastVisit() {
            try {
                const lastVisit = localStorage.getItem('sm_last_visit_' + USER_CONTEXT.userEmail);
                if (lastVisit) {
                    const date = new Date(lastVisit);
                    const now = new Date();
                    const diffMs = now - date;
                    const diffMins = Math.floor(diffMs / 60000);
                    const diffHours = Math.floor(diffMs / 3600000);
                    const diffDays = Math.floor(diffMs / 86400000);

                    if (diffMins < 60) return diffMins + ' min ago';
                    else if (diffHours < 24) return diffHours + ' hr ago';
                    else if (diffDays < 7) return diffDays + ' days ago';
                    else return date.toLocaleDateString();
                }
                return 'First visit';
            } catch (e) {
                return 'First visit';
            }
        }

        function saveLastVisit() {
            try {
                localStorage.setItem('sm_last_visit_' + USER_CONTEXT.userEmail, new Date().toISOString());
            } catch (e) {}
        }

        function getUserInitials(name) {
            if (!name) return '?';
            const parts = name.split(' ');
            if (parts.length >= 2) {
                return (parts[0][0] + parts[parts.length - 1][0]).toUpperCase();
            }
            return name[0].toUpperCase();
        }

USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager = (DEV_USER_PROFILE.role === 'TSM Manager');
USER_CONTEXT.isTSMSEViewer = (DEV_USER_PROFILE.role === 'TSM_SE_Viewer');
            // For LM/SM roles, use manager name from config
            if (USER_CONTEXT.isLM || USER_CONTEXT.isSM) {

            }

            // Show admin-only nav items immediately
            if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) {
           ['portalAnalyticsNavItem', 'transferRequestsNavItem', 'pendingRequestsNavItem'].forEach(function(id) {
                    var el = document.getElementById(id);
                    if (el) el.style.display = 'flex';
                });
                var lbl = document.getElementById('intelligenceNavLabel');
                if (lbl) lbl.style.display = 'block';
            }

            console.log('[✓] Mock user:', USER_CONTEXT.userName, '| Role:', USER_CONTEXT.role);
            return true;
        }

        // ===== ACCESS CONTROL =====
        function loadUserAccess(callback) {
            // ===== LOCAL DEV MODE: Skip SharePoint authentication =====
            if (LOCAL_DEV_MODE) {
                mockAuthentication();
                callback(true);
                return;
            }

            // ===== EXISTING SHAREPOINT AUTHENTICATION (UNCHANGED) =====
            const siteUrl = 'http://sharedspaces:8086/sites/SM';

            const xhrUser = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhrUser.open('GET', siteUrl + '/_api/web/currentuser?$select=Title,Email', true);
            xhrUser.setRequestHeader('Accept', 'application/json;odata=verbose');
            xhrUser.onreadystatechange = function() {
                if (xhrUser.readyState !== 4) return;
                if (xhrUser.status >= 200 && xhrUser.status < 300) {
                    const currentUser = JSON.parse(xhrUser.responseText).d;
                    const userEmail = currentUser.Email;
                    const userName = currentUser.Title;

                    USER_CONTEXT.userEmail = userEmail;
                    USER_CONTEXT.userName = userName;

                    fetchAccessControl(userEmail, userName, callback);
                } else {
                    console.error('Error loading current user');
                    callback(false);
                }
            };
            xhrUser.send();
        }

        function fetchAccessControl(userEmail, userName, callback) {
            const siteUrl = 'http://sharedspaces:8086/sites/SM';
            const accessListTitle = 'Access_Control';

            const url = siteUrl +
                "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + accessListTitle + "')/items" +
                "?$select=UserEmailID,Role&$top=5000";

            const xhr = new XMLHttpRequest();
            xhr.open('GET', url, true);
            xhr.setRequestHeader('Accept', 'application/json;odata=verbose');
            xhr.onreadystatechange = function() {
                if (xhr.readyState !== 4) return;
                if (xhr.status >= 200 && xhr.status < 300) {
                    const json = JSON.parse(xhr.responseText);
                    const allResults = (json.d && json.d.results) ? json.d.results : [];
                    const emailLower = (userEmail || '').toLowerCase();
                    const accessRecord = allResults.find(function(r) {
                        return (r.UserEmailID || '').toLowerCase() === emailLower;
                    });

                    if (accessRecord) {
                        // [OK] Found in Access_Control list
                        USER_CONTEXT.role = normalizeSmRole(accessRecord.Role || 'none');
                        USER_CONTEXT.isAM = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Account Manager');
                        USER_CONTEXT.isAD = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Account Director');
                        USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Admin');
USER_CONTEXT.isReadOnly = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Read Only');
USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'TSM Manager');
USER_CONTEXT.isTSMSEViewer = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'TSM_SE_Viewer');
USER_CONTEXT.isPsdAdmin = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'PSD_Admin');
USER_CONTEXT.isPsdAgent = (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'PSD_Agent');
USER_CONTEXT.isActive = true;

                        localStorage.setItem('sm_user_email', userEmail);
                        localStorage.setItem('sm_user_name', userName);
                        localStorage.setItem('sm_user_role', USER_CONTEXT.role);

                        // Show admin-only nav items immediately
                        if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) {
                         ['portalAnalyticsNavItem', 'transferRequestsNavItem', 'pendingRequestsNavItem'].forEach(function(id) {
                                var el = document.getElementById(id);
                                if (el) el.style.display = 'flex';
                            });
                            var lbl = document.getElementById('intelligenceNavLabel');
                            if (lbl) lbl.style.display = 'block';
                        }

                        console.log('[✓] Access granted:', userEmail, '| Role:', USER_CONTEXT.role);
                        callback(true);
                    } else {
                        // [NOT] NOT in Access_Control - Check if they're LM or SM in accounts
                        console.log('Not in Access_Control, checking if LM/SM...');
                        checkIfLineOrServiceManager(userName, callback);
                    }
                } else {
                    console.error('Error loading access control:', xhr.status, xhr.statusText);
                    callback(false);
                }
            };
            xhr.send();
        }
        async function checkIfLineOrServiceManager(userName, callback) {
            try {
                // Fetch all accounts and check if userName is LM or SM
                const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                    "$select=Line_x0020_Manager/Title,Service_x0020_Manager/Title&" +
                    "$expand=Line_x0020_Manager,Service_x0020_Manager&" +
                    "$filter=(Request_x0020_Status eq 'OnBoarded')&" +
                    "$top=10000";

                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });

                if (!res.ok) {
                    console.error('Failed to check LM/SM status');
                    callback(false);
                    return;
                }

                const data = await res.json();
                const accounts = data.d.results;

                // Check if userName appears as Line Manager
                const isLM = accounts.some(a =>
                    a.Line_x0020_Manager && a.Line_x0020_Manager.Title === userName
                );

                // Check if userName appears as Service Manager
                const isSM = accounts.some(a =>
                    a.Service_x0020_Manager && a.Service_x0020_Manager.Title === userName
                );

                if (isLM || isSM) {
                    // [OK] They are LM or SM - give them access
               USER_CONTEXT.role = isLM ? 'Line Manager' : 'Service Manager';
USER_CONTEXT.isLM = isLM;
USER_CONTEXT.isSM = isSM;
USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin = false;
USER_CONTEXT.isAM = false;
USER_CONTEXT.isAD = false;
USER_CONTEXT.isReadOnly = false;
USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager = false;
USER_CONTEXT.isActive = true;

                    localStorage.setItem('sm_user_email', USER_CONTEXT.userEmail);
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_user_name', userName);
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_user_role', USER_CONTEXT.role);

                    console.log('[✓] Access granted:', userName, '| Role:', USER_CONTEXT.role);
                    callback(true);
                } else {
                    // [NOT] Not LM/SM either - no access
                    console.log('[✗] User not found as LM/SM:', userName);
                    USER_CONTEXT.role = 'none';
                    USER_CONTEXT.isActive = false;
                    callback(false);
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Error checking LM/SM:', err);
                callback(false);
            }
        }

        }

        function showDashboard() {
            const landing = document.getElementById('landingPage');
            if (landing) {
                landing.style.display = 'none';
                landing.style.visibility = 'hidden';
                landing.style.position = 'absolute';
                landing.style.zIndex = '-9999';
            }

            document.getElementById('dashboardContent').style.display = 'block';

            // Auditor: jump straight to QA view
            if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Auditor') {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    switchDashboardSection('qaView');
                    if (typeof qaInit === 'function') qaInit();
                }, 150);
            }

            // PSD roles: jump straight to PSD Assignment
            if (isPsdRole(USER_CONTEXT.role)) {
                setTimeout(function() {
                    switchDashboardSection('psdView');
                }, 150);
            }

            const loading = document.getElementById('loading');
            const content = document.getElementById('content');
            if (loading) loading.style.display = 'none';
            if (content) content.style.display = 'block';
            // Re-initialize icons and ensure nav is visible
            setTimeout(() => {
                // Only show nav items appropriate to role
                // Pending/Transfer nav items are hidden by default (style="display:none") 
                // and only shown for Admin in init()
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                    lucide.createIcons();
                }
            }, 100);
            incrementVisitCount();
            saveLastVisit();
        }

        function initPsdShell() {
            try {
                setCurrentDate();
                var loading = document.getElementById('loading');
                var content = document.getElementById('content');
                if (loading) loading.style.display = 'none';
                if (content) content.style.display = 'block';

                var psdNav = document.getElementById('psdNavItem');
                if (psdNav) psdNav.style.display = 'flex';
                applyPsdNavRestrictions();

                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
                if (typeof analyticsStartSession === 'function') analyticsStartSession();
                if (typeof nlCheckOnLoad === 'function') nlCheckOnLoad();
            } catch (err) {
                console.error('PSD shell init error:', err);
            }
        }

        async function init() {
            try {
                console.log('Loading SharePoint...');
                await fetchDOJData();
                await fetchAccountMapping();
                await fetchRevenueEnabled();
          ALL_DATA = await fetchData();
window.ALL_DATA = ALL_DATA;
recalculateRevFlags();

                // Filter data by role on initial load
                if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager') {
                    // ✅ STEP 1: Get ALL accounts first (groups + children)
                    window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.lm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);
                    // ✅ STEP 2: Then filter to groups only for stats
                    filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
                } else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') {
                    // ✅ STEP 1: Get ALL accounts first (groups + children)
                    window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.sm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);
                    // ✅ STEP 2: Then filter to groups only for stats
                    filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
                } else if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) {
    window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE');
    filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
} else {
    // Admin
    window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.slice();
    filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
}

              setCurrentDate();
populateFilters({ preserve: false });
updateServiceManagerFilter();
applyFilters();
if (!window._smMsDropdownClickBound) {
    window._smMsDropdownClickBound = true;
    document.addEventListener('click', function (event) {
        document.querySelectorAll('.custom-multiselect').forEach(function (ms) {
            if (!ms.contains(event.target)) {
                var dd = ms.querySelector('.multiselect-dropdown');
                if (dd) dd.style.display = 'none';
            }
        });
    });
}

         if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Director' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Auditor' || USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') {

}

var rnpsNav = document.getElementById('rnpsNavItem');
if (rnpsNav) rnpsNav.style.display = 'flex';

                // PSD Assignment: visible to SM Admin, PSD_Admin and PSD_Agent only
                if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'PSD_Admin' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'PSD_Agent') {
                    var psdNav = document.getElementById('psdNavItem');
                    if (psdNav) psdNav.style.display = 'flex';
                }
                // PSD_Admin / PSD_Agent: restrict the sidebar to an allowed set of menus
                if (isPsdRole(USER_CONTEXT.role)) {
                    applyPsdNavRestrictions();
                }

                // Auditor: hide all nav items except allowed ones
                if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Auditor') {
                    var allowedSections = ['qaView', 'suggestionsView', 'processDocsView', 'contactUsView'];
                    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(function(item) {
                        var section = item.getAttribute('data-section');
                        var labelEl = item.querySelector('.nav-label');
                        var isNewsletter = labelEl && labelEl.textContent.trim() === 'Newsletter';
                        if (!allowedSections.includes(section) && !isNewsletter) {
                            item.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    });
                    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-section-label').forEach(function(lbl) {
                        lbl.style.display = 'none';
                    });
                }
 // TSM Manager: hide Project Management
                if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) {
                    var projNav = document.getElementById('projectMgmtNavItem');
                    if (projNav) projNav.style.display = 'none';
                }

                // TSM SE Viewer: no export
                if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMSEViewer) {
                    var exportBtn = document.getElementById('smExportExcelBtn');
                    if (exportBtn) exportBtn.style.display = 'none';
                }

                // Start session tracking
                if (typeof analyticsStartSession === 'function') {
                    analyticsStartSession();
                }

                if (typeof nlCheckOnLoad === 'function') {
                    nlCheckOnLoad();
                }
            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Error:', err);
                document.getElementById('loading').innerHTML = '<div style="color:#ef4444;">Error: ' + err.message + '</div>';
            }


        }

  const SM_MS_FILTER_CFG = {
            LM: { dropdown: 'filterLMDropdown', text: 'filterLMSelectedText', label: 'Line Managers' },
            SM: { dropdown: 'filterSMDropdown', text: 'filterSMSelectedText', label: 'Service Managers' },
            Team: { dropdown: 'filterTeamDropdown', text: 'filterTeamSelectedText', label: 'Teams' },
            RevDrop: { dropdown: 'filterRevDropDropdown', text: 'filterRevDropSelectedText', label: 'Accounts' },
            Structure: { dropdown: 'filterStructureDropdown', text: 'filterStructureSelectedText', label: 'Accounts' }
        };

        function smGetMsFilterValues(key) {
            const cfg = SM_MS_FILTER_CFG[key];
            if (!cfg) return [];
            return Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('#' + cfg.dropdown + ' input[type="checkbox"]:checked')).map(function (cb) { return cb.value; });
        }

        function smToggleMsDropdown(dropdownId) {
            document.querySelectorAll('.multiselect-dropdown').forEach(function (d) {
                if (d.id !== dropdownId) d.style.display = 'none';
            });
            const dropdown = document.getElementById(dropdownId);
            if (dropdown) dropdown.style.display = dropdown.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        }
        window.smToggleMsDropdown = smToggleMsDropdown;

        function smUpdateMsFilterDisplay(key, label) {
            const cfg = SM_MS_FILTER_CFG[key];
            if (!cfg) return;
            const selected = smGetMsFilterValues(key);
            const displayText = selected.length === 0 ? 'All ' + label :
                selected.length === 1 ? selected[0] :
                selected.length + ' selected';
            const textEl = document.getElementById(cfg.text);
            if (textEl) textEl.textContent = displayText;
        }

        function smUpdateLegacySelect(selectId, values, selectedValues) {
            var el = document.getElementById(selectId);
            if (!el) return;
            el.innerHTML = '<option value=""></option>';
            values.forEach(function (v) {
                var opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = v;
                opt.textContent = v;
                el.appendChild(opt);
            });
            if (selectedValues && selectedValues.length === 1) el.value = selectedValues[0];
            else el.value = '';
        }

        function smSyncLegacyFilterSelects(fireTeamChange) {
            var teamSel = smGetMsFilterValues('Team');
            var lmSel = smGetMsFilterValues('LM');
            var smSel = smGetMsFilterValues('SM');
            var teamEl = document.getElementById('filterTeam');
            var lmEl = document.getElementById('filterLM');
            var smEl = document.getElementById('filterSM');
            if (lmEl) lmEl.value = lmSel.length === 1 ? lmSel[0] : '';
            if (smEl) smEl.value = smSel.length === 1 ? smSel[0] : '';
            if (!teamEl) return;
            var newTeam = teamSel.length === 1 ? teamSel[0] : '';
            var teamChanged = teamEl.value !== newTeam;
            teamEl.value = newTeam;
            if (!fireTeamChange || window._smSyncingLegacyTeam) return;
            window._smSyncingLegacyTeam = true;
            try {
                // tsm-se.js listens to the native #filterTeam change event — dispatch it
                if (teamChanged) {
                    teamEl.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                } else {
                    onTeamFilterChanged();
                }
            } finally {
                window._smSyncingLegacyTeam = false;
            }
        }

        function smOnMsFilterChange(key, label, applyNow) {
            smUpdateMsFilterDisplay(key, label);
            if (key === 'Team') {
                selectedLM = null;
                selectedSM = null;
                var perfSec = document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection');
                if (perfSec) perfSec.style.display = 'none';
                smSyncLegacyFilterSelects(true);
                return;
            }
            if (applyNow !== false) applyFilters();
        }
        window.smOnMsFilterChange = smOnMsFilterChange;

        function smBuildMsDropdown(key, values, savedValues) {
            const cfg = SM_MS_FILTER_CFG[key];
            if (!cfg) return;
            const dropdown = document.getElementById(cfg.dropdown);
            if (!dropdown) return;
            dropdown.innerHTML = '';
            values.forEach(function (val) {
                const div = document.createElement('div');
                div.className = 'multiselect-option';
                const safeId = key + '_' + String(val).replace(/\s+/g, '_').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '');
                const checked = savedValues && savedValues.includes(val) ? ' checked' : '';
                div.innerHTML = '<input type="checkbox" id="' + safeId + '" value="' + String(val).replace(/"/g, '&quot;') + '"' + checked + ' onchange="smOnMsFilterChange(\'' + key + '\',\'' + cfg.label + '\',true)">' +
                    '<label for="' + safeId + '">' + val + '</label>';
                dropdown.appendChild(div);
            });
            smUpdateMsFilterDisplay(key, cfg.label);
        }

        function smClearMsDropdown(key) {
            const cfg = SM_MS_FILTER_CFG[key];
            if (!cfg) return;
            document.querySelectorAll('#' + cfg.dropdown + ' input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function (cb) { cb.checked = false; });
            smUpdateMsFilterDisplay(key, cfg.label);
        }

        function smSetMsDropdownDisabled(key, disabled) {
            const cfg = SM_MS_FILTER_CFG[key];
            if (!cfg) return;
            document.querySelectorAll('#' + cfg.dropdown + ' input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function (cb) { cb.disabled = disabled; });
            const wrap = document.getElementById(cfg.dropdown);
            if (wrap && wrap.parentElement) {
                const sel = wrap.parentElement.querySelector('.multiselect-selected');
                if (sel) {
                    sel.style.opacity = disabled ? '0.6' : '1';
                    sel.style.pointerEvents = disabled ? 'none' : 'auto';
                }
            }
        }

  function populateFilters(options) {
    options = options || {};
    const preserve = options.preserve !== false;
    const savedLM = preserve ? smGetMsFilterValues('LM') : [];
    const savedSM = preserve ? smGetMsFilterValues('SM') : [];
    const savedTeam = preserve ? smGetMsFilterValues('Team') : [];
console.log('[populateFilters] role:', USER_CONTEXT.role, '| isTSMManager:', USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager);
    const role = USER_CONTEXT.role;
            const userName = USER_CONTEXT.userName;

           let filteredData = ALL_DATA;

// Role-based data filtering
if (role === 'Line Manager') {
    filteredData = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.lm === userName);
} else if (role === 'Service Manager') {
    filteredData = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.sm === userName);
} else if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) {
    filteredData = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE');
}
            if (role === 'Line Manager') {
                smBuildMsDropdown('LM', [userName], [userName]);
                smSetMsDropdownDisabled('LM', true);
            } else if (role === 'Service Manager') {
                const myLM = ALL_DATA.find(a => a.sm === userName)?.lm;
                smBuildMsDropdown('LM', myLM ? [myLM] : [], myLM ? [myLM] : []);
                smSetMsDropdownDisabled('LM', true);
            } else {
    const sourceData = USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager
        ? ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE')
        : ALL_DATA;
    const lms = [...new Set(sourceData.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
    smBuildMsDropdown('LM', lms, preserve ? savedLM.filter(v => lms.includes(v)) : []);
    smSetMsDropdownDisabled('LM', false);
}

            if (role === 'Service Manager') {
                smBuildMsDropdown('SM', [userName], [userName]);
                smSetMsDropdownDisabled('SM', true);
            } else if (role === 'Line Manager') {
                const mySMs = [...new Set(filteredData.map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
                smBuildMsDropdown('SM', mySMs, preserve ? savedSM.filter(v => mySMs.includes(v)) : []);
                smSetMsDropdownDisabled('SM', false);
            } else {
    const sourceData = USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager
        ? ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE')
        : ALL_DATA;
    const sms = [...new Set(sourceData.map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
    smBuildMsDropdown('SM', sms, preserve ? savedSM.filter(v => sms.includes(v)) : []);
    smSetMsDropdownDisabled('SM', false);
}
            const teams = [...new Set(filteredData.map(a => a.team))].filter(Boolean).sort();
            smBuildMsDropdown('Team', teams, preserve ? savedTeam.filter(v => teams.includes(v)) : []);
            smSetMsDropdownDisabled('Team', false);
            smUpdateLegacySelect('filterLM', role === 'Line Manager' ? [userName] : (role === 'Service Manager' ? (ALL_DATA.find(a => a.sm === userName)?.lm ? [ALL_DATA.find(a => a.sm === userName).lm] : []) : [...new Set((USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager ? ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE') : ALL_DATA).map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean).sort()), smGetMsFilterValues('LM'));
            smUpdateLegacySelect('filterSM', role === 'Service Manager' ? [userName] : [...new Set(filteredData.map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort(), smGetMsFilterValues('SM'));
            smUpdateLegacySelect('filterTeam', teams, smGetMsFilterValues('Team'));
            smSyncLegacyFilterSelects(false);
        }

        function updateServiceManagerFilter() {
            const role = USER_CONTEXT.role;
            const userName = USER_CONTEXT.userName;

            if (role === 'Line Manager' || role === 'Service Manager') {
                return;
            }

            const lmFilter = smGetMsFilterValues('LM');
            const teamFilter = smGetMsFilterValues('Team');
            let sms, lms;

            if (teamFilter.length) {
                const teamData = ALL_DATA.filter(a => teamFilter.includes(a.team));
                lms = [...new Set(teamData.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean).sort();

                if (lmFilter.length) {
                    sms = [...new Set(teamData.filter(a => lmFilter.includes(a.lm)).map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
                } else {
                    sms = [...new Set(teamData.map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
                }
            } else {
    const baseData = USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager
        ? ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE')
        : ALL_DATA;

    lms = [...new Set(baseData.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean).sort();

    if (lmFilter.length) {
        sms = [...new Set(baseData.filter(a => lmFilter.includes(a.lm)).map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
    } else {
        sms = [...new Set(baseData.map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean).sort();
    }
}

            const currentLM = smGetMsFilterValues('LM');
            if (!document.querySelector('#filterLMDropdown input[disabled]')) {
                smBuildMsDropdown('LM', lms, currentLM.filter(v => lms.includes(v)));
            }

            const currentSM = smGetMsFilterValues('SM');
            if (!document.querySelector('#filterSMDropdown input[disabled]')) {
                smBuildMsDropdown('SM', sms, currentSM.filter(v => sms.includes(v)));
            }
        }

        function onTeamFilterChanged() {
            selectedLM = null;
            selectedSM = null;
            var teamEl = document.getElementById('filterTeam');
            var wasTsmSe = !!window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE;
            window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE = !!(teamEl && teamEl.value === 'TSM_SE');
            if (wasTsmSe && !window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE) {
                smExitTsmSeMode();
            }
            var perfSec = document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection');
            if (perfSec) perfSec.style.display = 'none';
            applyFilters();
        }

        function smDestroyTsmSeGridOnly() {
            ['tsmSeDestroy', 'tsmSeReset', 'tsmSeClear', 'tsmSeRestoreMainGrid', 'tsmSeHide'].forEach(function (name) {
                if (typeof window[name] === 'function') {
                    try { window[name](); } catch (e) { console.warn('[smDestroyTsmSeGridOnly]', name, e); }
                }
            });
            if (window.tsmSeGridApi) {
                try { window.tsmSeGridApi.destroy(); } catch (e) {}
                window.tsmSeGridApi = null;
            }
            var gridDiv = document.getElementById('myGrid');
            if (gridDiv) gridDiv.innerHTML = '';
            if (agGridApi) {
                try {
                    agGridApi.setFilterModel(null);
                    agGridApi.setGridOption('quickFilterText', '');
                    agGridApi.destroy();
                } catch (e) {}
                agGridApi = null;
            }
        }

        function smExitTsmSeMode() {
            window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE = false;
            smDestroyTsmSeGridOnly();
            window.PARENT_ROWS = null;
            window.CURRENT_TABLE_DATA = null;
        }

        function resetFilters() {
