            smClearMsDropdown('LM');
            smClearMsDropdown('SM');
            smClearMsDropdown('Team');
            smClearMsDropdown('RevDrop');
            smClearMsDropdown('Structure');
            var tfEl = document.getElementById('transferStatusFilterMain');
            if (tfEl) tfEl.value = '';
            var searchEl = document.getElementById('agGridSearch');
            if (searchEl) searchEl.value = '';
            window._TRANSFER_FILTER_VAL = '';
            selectedLM = null;
            selectedSM = null;
            document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection').style.display = 'none';

            smExitTsmSeMode();
            populateFilters({ preserve: false });

            var teamEl = document.getElementById('filterTeam');
            var lmEl = document.getElementById('filterLM');
            var smEl = document.getElementById('filterSM');
            if (lmEl) lmEl.value = '';
            if (smEl) smEl.value = '';
            if (teamEl) {
                teamEl.value = '';
                try {
                    teamEl.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', { bubbles: true }));
                } catch (e) {
                    onTeamFilterChanged();
                }
            } else {
                applyFilters();
            }
        }

        function applyFilters() {
            smSyncLegacyFilterSelects(false);
            updateServiceManagerFilter();
            const lmSel = smGetMsFilterValues('LM');
            const smSel = smGetMsFilterValues('SM');
            const teamSel = smGetMsFilterValues('Team');
            const revDropSel = smGetMsFilterValues('RevDrop');
            const structureSel = smGetMsFilterValues('Structure');

            window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE = teamSel.length === 1 && teamSel[0] === 'TSM_SE';

            // First filter ALL data based on criteria
           const allFiltered = ALL_DATA.filter(a => {
    if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager') {
        if (a.lm !== USER_CONTEXT.userName) return false;
    } else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') {
        if (a.sm !== USER_CONTEXT.userName) return false;
    } else if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) {
        if (a.team !== 'TSM_ME' && a.team !== 'TSM_SE') return false;
    }
                if (selectedLM && a.lm !== selectedLM) return false;
                if (selectedSM && a.sm !== selectedSM) return false;
                if (lmSel.length && !lmSel.includes(a.lm)) return false;
                if (smSel.length && !smSel.includes(a.sm)) return false;
                if (teamSel.length && !teamSel.includes(a.team)) return false;
                if (revDropSel.length) {
                    const revMatch = (revDropSel.includes('drop') && a.isRevDrop) ||
                        (revDropSel.includes('upgrade') && a.isRevUpgrade);
                    if (!revMatch) return false;
                }
                return true;
            });

            // PARENTS ONLY for stats, charts, tiles
            filtered = allFiltered.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');

            // ✅ NEW: Apply structure filter (Groups with/without children)
            if (structureSel.length) {
                filtered = filtered.filter(parent => {
                    const hasChildren = allFiltered.some(child =>
                        child.type === 'Child' &&
                        child.parent === parent.code &&
                        child.code !== parent.code
                    );
                    const wantWith = structureSel.includes('with-children');
                    const wantStandalone = structureSel.includes('standalone');
                    if (wantWith && wantStandalone) return true;
                    if (wantWith) return hasChildren;
                    if (wantStandalone) return !hasChildren;
                    return true;
                });
            }

            // Store all filtered (including children) for table expand
            window.ALL_FILTERED = allFiltered;
            // ✅ ADD THIS
            console.log('[applyFilters] window.ALL_FILTERED now has:', window.ALL_FILTERED.length, 'accounts');
            console.log('[applyFilters] Groups:', window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group').length);
            console.log('[applyFilters] Children:', window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Child').length);
            updateStats();
            renderLineManagers();
            renderServiceManagers();
            renderCharts();
            if (window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE && typeof window.tsmSeRenderTable === 'function') {
                window.tsmSeRenderTable();
            } else {
                renderTable();
            }
        }

     async function selectLM(name) {
    selectedLM = selectedLM === name ? null : name;
    selectedSM = null;

    if (selectedLM) {
        document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection').style.display = 'block';
    } else {
        document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection').style.display = 'none';
    }

    updateServiceManagerFilter();
    applyFilters();
    await renderServiceManagers(); // ← add this
}

        function selectSM(name) {
            selectedSM = selectedSM === name ? null : name;
            applyFilters();
        }

        function formatCurrency(v) {
            if (v === null || v === undefined || isNaN(v)) return '0';
            if (v >= 1000000) return (v / 1000000).toFixed(2) + 'M';
            if (v >= 1000) return (v / 1000).toFixed(1) + 'K';
            return v.toFixed(0);
        }

        function updateStats() {
            const total = filtered.length;
            const totalRev = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);
            const groups = filtered.filter(a => a.type === 'Group').length;

            // ✅ FIX: Count children from ALL_FILTERED (not filtered which only has Groups)
            const allFiltered = window.ALL_FILTERED || [];
            const children = allFiltered.filter(a => a.type === 'Child').length;

            // ✅ FIX: Display total as Groups + Children
            const displayTotal = groups + children;

            // [NEW] Get dynamic last 3 months
            const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();
            const month1Key = lastThree[0].key;
            const month2Key = lastThree[1].key;
            const month3Key = lastThree[2].key;

            const month1 = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[month1Key] || 0), 0);
            const month2 = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[month2Key] || 0), 0);
            const month3 = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[month3Key] || 0), 0);

            const growth = month2 > 0 ? ((month3 - month2) / month2 * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;

            document.getElementById('stats').innerHTML = `
    <div class="stat-card">
        <div class="stat-label">Total Accounts</div>
        <div class="stat-value">${displayTotal}</div>
        <div class="stat-subtitle">Active Accounts</div>
        <div class="stat-breakdown">
            <div class="breakdown-item">
                <div class="breakdown-label">Groups</div>
                <div class="breakdown-value">${groups}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="breakdown-item">
                <div class="breakdown-label">Children</div>
                <div class="breakdown-value">${children}</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
        <div class="stat-label">Total Revenue</div>
        <div class="stat-value">${formatCurrency(totalRev)}</div>
        <div class="stat-subtitle">Monthly Average</div>
        <div class="stat-breakdown">
            <div class="breakdown-item">
                <div class="breakdown-label">Growth</div>
                <div class="breakdown-value" style="color:${growth >= 0 ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444'}">${growth}%</div>
            </div>
            <div class="breakdown-item">
                <div class="breakdown-label">Per Account</div>
                <div class="breakdown-value">${total > 0 ? formatCurrency(totalRev/total) : 0}</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="stat-card">
        <div class="stat-label">${lastThree[2].label} Revenue</div>
        <div class="stat-value">${formatCurrency(month3)}</div>
        <div class="stat-subtitle">Latest Month</div>
        <div class="stat-breakdown">
            <div class="breakdown-item">
                <div class="breakdown-label">${lastThree[1].label}</div>
                <div class="breakdown-value">${formatCurrency(month2)}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="breakdown-item">
                <div class="breakdown-label">${lastThree[0].label}</div>
                <div class="breakdown-value">${formatCurrency(month1)}</div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
                <div class="stat-card">
                    <div class="stat-label">Line Managers</div>
                    <div class="stat-value">${new Set(filtered.map(a => a.lm).filter(Boolean)).size}</div>
                    <div class="stat-subtitle">Active Managers</div>
                </div>
                <div class="stat-card">
                    <div class="stat-label">Service Managers</div>
                    <div class="stat-value">${new Set(filtered.map(a => a.sm).filter(Boolean)).size}</div>
                    <div class="stat-subtitle">Active Managers</div>
                </div>
            `;
        }

async function renderLineManagers() {
    const scopeGroups = filtered.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
    let lms = [...new Set(scopeGroups.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean);

    if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager') {
        lms = lms.filter(lm => lm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);
    } else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') {
        const myLM = ALL_DATA.find(a => a.sm === USER_CONTEXT.userName)?.lm;
        if (myLM) lms = [myLM];
        else lms = [];
    }

    const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();

    // Use cached RNPS — populated only when loadAnalytics() is called
    const rnpsMap = window.RNPS_CACHE || {};

    const stats = lms.map(lm => {
        const accs = filtered.filter(a => a.lm === lm);
        const totalR = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);

        const month1 = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[lastThree[0].key] || 0), 0);
        const month2 = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[lastThree[1].key] || 0), 0);
        const month3 = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[lastThree[2].key] || 0), 0);

        const growth = month2 > 0 ? ((month3 - month2) / month2 * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;

        const totalC = filtered.length;
        const totalRev = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);
        const cShare = totalC > 0 ? (accs.length / totalC * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;
        const rShare = totalRev > 0 ? (totalR / totalRev * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;

        return { name: lm, count: accs.length, totalR, month1, month2, month3, growth, cShare, rShare };
    })
    .filter(m => m.count > 0)
    .sort((a, b) => b.totalR - a.totalR);

    const grid = document.getElementById('lineManagersGrid');

    if (stats.length === 0) {
        grid.innerHTML = `
            <div style="grid-column: 1 / -1; text-align: center; padding: 60px 20px; color: var(--text-secondary);">
                <div style="font-size: 48px; margin-bottom: 16px;">📭</div>
                <div style="font-size: 18px; font-weight: 600; margin-bottom: 8px;">No Accounts Found</div>
                <div style="font-size: 14px;">No accounts match the current filters</div>
            </div>`;
        return;
    }

    grid.innerHTML = stats.map(m => {
        const isSelected = selectedLM === m.name;
        const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();
        const key = m.name.replace(/\s/g, '_');

const lmQuarters = rnpsMap[m.name] || [];
let rnpsTileHtml = '';
if (isSelected && !window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE) {
            if (!window.ANALYTICS_LOADED) {
                rnpsTileHtml = `
                <div class="lm-tile" style="cursor:default;opacity:.85;min-width:200px;">
                    <div class="lm-header">
                        <h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">RNPS Performance</h3>
                        <div class="lm-meta" style="margin-top:6px;line-height:1.5;">
                            <i data-lucide="bar-chart-2" style="width:12px;height:12px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:3px;"></i>
                            Click <strong style="color:var(--acc);">Load RNPS &amp; ETA Analytics</strong> above to view
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            } else if (lmQuarters.length > 0) {
                rnpsTileHtml = `
            <div class="lm-tile" style="border-color:var(--border-s);cursor:default;">
                <div class="lm-header">
                    <h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">RNPS Performance</h3>
                    <div class="lm-meta">Avg across all SMs</div>
                </div>
                <div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px;margin-top:4px;">
                    ${lmQuarters.map(row => {
                        const rnpsColor = row.RNPS >= row.RNPSTarget ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444';
                        const rrColor = row.ResponseRate >= row.ResponseTarget ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444';
                        return `
                        <div style="background:var(--bg-secondary);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:8px 10px;">
                            <div style="font-size:.68rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--acc);margin-bottom:5px;">${row.Period}</div>
                            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:3px;">
                                <span style="font-size:.63rem;color:var(--t3);">Avg Response Rate</span>
                                <span style="font-size:.7rem;font-weight:700;color:${rrColor};">
                                    ${row.ResponseRate}%
                                    <span style="color:var(--t3);font-weight:400;">/ ${row.ResponseTarget}%</span>
                                </span>
                            </div>
                            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">
                                <span style="font-size:.63rem;color:var(--t3);">Avg RNPS Score</span>
                                <span style="font-size:.7rem;font-weight:700;color:${rnpsColor};">
                                    ${row.RNPS}
                                    <span style="color:var(--t3);font-weight:400;">/ ${row.RNPSTarget}</span>
                                </span>
                            </div>
                        </div>`;
                    }).join('')}
                </div>
            </div>`;
            } else {
                rnpsTileHtml = `
                <div class="lm-tile" style="cursor:default;opacity:.75;min-width:200px;">
                    <div class="lm-header">
                        <h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">RNPS Performance</h3>
                        <div class="lm-meta" style="margin-top:6px;">No RNPS data found for this period.</div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            }
        }

       // ── ETA tile (only when selected) ────────────────────
    let etaTileHtml = '';
if (isSelected && !window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE) {
            if (!window.ETA_LOADED) {
                etaTileHtml = `
                <div class="lm-tile" style="cursor:default;opacity:.85;min-width:200px;">
                    <div class="lm-header">
                        <h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">ETA Overview</h3>
                        <div class="lm-meta" style="margin-top:6px;line-height:1.5;">
                            <i data-lucide="layers" style="width:12px;height:12px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:3px;"></i>
                            Click <strong style="color:var(--acc);">Load RNPS &amp; ETA Analytics</strong> above to view
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            } else {
                const etaStats = etaGetManagerStats(function(r) { return r.LM === m.name; });
                const hasData = etaStats && (etaStats.tt.total > 0 || etaStats.events.total > 0 || etaStats.activities.total > 0);

                function lmMiniRow(label, s) {
                    if (!s || s.total === 0) return '';
                    return `
                    <div style="margin-bottom:6px;">
                        <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:2px;">
                            <span style="font-size:.62rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--t2);">${label}</span>
                            <span style="font-size:.6rem;color:var(--t3);">Total: ${s.total}</span>
                        </div>
                        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:3px;">
                            <div style="background:rgba(245,158,11,.12);border:1px solid rgba(245,158,11,.25);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                                <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#b45309;font-weight:600;">Assigned</div>
                                <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#f59e0b;">${s.assigned}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.12);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.25);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                                <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#1d4ed8;font-weight:600;">In Prog</div>
                                <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#3b82f6;">${s.inprogress}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div style="background:rgba(16,185,129,.12);border:1px solid rgba(16,185,129,.25);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                                <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:#065f46;font-weight:600;">Done</div>
                                <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:#10b981;">${s.completed}</div>
                            </div>
                            <div style="background:rgba(107,114,128,.12);border:1px solid rgba(107,114,128,.25);border-radius:5px;padding:3px 4px;text-align:center;">
                                <div style="font-size:.58rem;color:var(--t3);font-weight:600;">Other</div>
                                <div style="font-size:.78rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--t3);">${s.other}</div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>`;
                }

                etaTileHtml = `
                <div class="lm-tile" style="border-color:var(--border-s);cursor:default;min-width:220px;">
                    <div class="lm-header" style="margin-bottom:8px;">
                        <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;gap:6px;">
                            <h3 style="font-size:.85rem;">${m.name}</h3>
                            <span style="font-size:.7rem;color:var(--t3);font-weight:500;">${currentYear}</span>
                            <div style="position:relative;display:inline-block;">
                                <span id="etaInfoBtn_lm_${key}"
                                    onclick="etaShowInfoPopup(event,'lm_${key}')"
                                    style="cursor:pointer;width:18px;height:18px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--bg-secondary);border:1px solid var(--border);display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:.65rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--acc);">i</span>
                                <div id="etaInfoPopup_lm_${key}"
                                    style="display:none;position:absolute;right:0;top:24px;z-index:999;background:var(--bg-card);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.2);padding:10px 12px;min-width:220px;max-width:260px;">
                                    <div style="font-size:.7rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--t1);margin-bottom:6px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);padding-bottom:4px;">Detailed Breakdown</div>
                                    ${hasData
                                        ? etaDetailHtml('TTs', etaStats.ttDetail) + etaDetailHtml('Events', etaStats.evDetail) + etaDetailHtml('Activities', etaStats.actDetail)
                                        : '<div style="font-size:.72rem;color:var(--t3);">No ETA data found</div>'
                                    }
                                </div>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="lm-meta">ETA Data — Current Year</div>
                    </div>
                    ${hasData ? `
                        ${lmMiniRow('Trouble Tickets', etaStats.tt)}
                        ${lmMiniRow('Events', etaStats.events)}
                        ${lmMiniRow('Activities', etaStats.activities)}
                    ` : `
                        <div style="font-size:.75rem;color:var(--t3);text-align:center;padding:1rem 0;">No ETA data found for this LM.</div>
                    `}
                </div>`;
            }
        }

        // ── Main LM tile ──────────────────────────────────────
        return `
        <div class="lm-tile ${isSelected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="selectLM('${m.name}')">
            <div class="lm-header">
                <h3>${m.name}</h3>
            </div>

            <div class="lm-stats-grid">
                <div class="lm-stat-box">
                    <div class="lm-stat-label">Count</div>
                    <div class="lm-stat-value">${m.count}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="lm-stat-box">
                    <div class="lm-stat-label">Revenue</div>
                    <div class="lm-stat-value">${formatCurrency(m.totalR)}</div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="lm-revenue">
                <div class="lm-revenue-label">${lastThree[2].label} Revenue</div>
                <div class="lm-revenue-count">${formatCurrency(m.month3)}</div>
                <div class="lm-revenue-breakdown">
                    <div class="lm-revenue-item">
                        <div class="lm-revenue-item-label">Growth</div>
                        <div class="lm-revenue-item-value" style="color:${m.growth >= 0 ? '#34d399' : '#fca5a5'};">${m.growth >= 0 ? '+' : ''}${m.growth}%</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="lm-revenue-item">
                        <div class="lm-revenue-item-label">${lastThree[1].label}</div>
                        <div class="lm-revenue-item-value">${formatCurrency(m.month2)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="lm-revenue-item">
                        <div class="lm-revenue-item-label">${lastThree[0].label}</div>
                        <div class="lm-revenue-item-value">${formatCurrency(m.month1)}</div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>

            <div class="lm-progress-section">
                <div class="lm-progress-row">
                    <span class="lm-progress-label">Account Share</span>
                    <span class="lm-progress-value">${m.cShare}%</span>
                </div>
                <div class="progress-bar">
                    <div class="progress-fill" style="width:${m.cShare}%"></div>
                </div>
                <div class="lm-progress-row">
                    <span class="lm-progress-label">Revenue Share</span>
                    <span class="lm-progress-value">${m.rShare}%</span>
                </div>
                <div class="progress-bar">
                    <div class="progress-fill" style="width:${m.rShare}%"></div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
        ${rnpsTileHtml}
        ${etaTileHtml}`;
    }).join('');
}
async function renderServiceManagers() {
    if (!selectedLM) {
        document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection').style.display = 'none';
        return;
    }

    document.getElementById('smPerformanceSection').style.display = 'block';

    const sms = [...new Set(filtered.map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean);
    const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();
    const currentYear = new Date().getFullYear();

    // Fetch RNPS data for selected LM
    const rnpsData = await fetchRNPSForLM(selectedLM);

    const stats = sms.map(sm => {
        const accs = filtered.filter(a => a.sm === sm);
        const totalR = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);

        const month1 = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[lastThree[0].key] || 0), 0);
        const month2 = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[lastThree[1].key] || 0), 0);
        const month3 = accs.reduce((sum, a) => sum + (a[lastThree[2].key] || 0), 0);

        const growth = month2 > 0 ? ((month3 - month2) / month2 * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;

        const totalC = filtered.length;
        const totalRev = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);
        const cShare = totalC > 0 ? (accs.length / totalC * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;
        const rShare = totalRev > 0 ? (totalR / totalRev * 100).toFixed(1) : 0;

        return { name: sm, count: accs.length, totalR, month1, month2, month3, growth, cShare, rShare };
    }).sort((a, b) => b.totalR - a.totalR);

    document.getElementById('serviceManagersList').innerHTML = stats.map((m, i) => {
        const rankClass = i === 0 ? 'rank-1' : i === 1 ? 'rank-2' : i === 2 ? 'rank-3' : 'rank-other';
        const isSelected = selectedSM === m.name;
        const tag = i === 0 ? 'Top Performer' : i === 1 ? 'High Achiever' : 'Key Contributor';
        const key = m.name.replace(/\s/g, '_');

      // ── RNPS block ────────────────────────────────────────
    const smRnps = rnpsData[m.name] || [];
let rnpsHtml = '';
if (window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE) {
    rnpsHtml = '';
} else if (!window.ANALYTICS_LOADED) {
            rnpsHtml = `
                <div style="margin-top:8px;padding-top:8px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);font-size:.72rem;color:var(--t3);">
                    <i data-lucide="bar-chart-2" style="width:11px;height:11px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:3px;"></i>
                    Click <strong style="color:var(--acc);">Load RNPS &amp; ETA Analytics</strong> above to view RNPS data
                </div>`;
        } else if (smRnps.length > 0) {
            const sorted = smRnps.slice().sort((a, b) => {
                const qa = parseInt(a.Period.replace('Q', '').split('-')[0]);
                const qb = parseInt(b.Period.replace('Q', '').split('-')[0]);
                return qa - qb;
            });
            rnpsHtml = `
                <div style="margin-top:8px;padding-top:8px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:6px;">
                    <div style="width:100%;font-size:.62rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--t3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;margin-bottom:2px;">RNPS Performance</div>
                    ${sorted.map(row => {
                        const rnpsColor = row.RNPS >= row.RNPSTarget ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444';
                        const rrColor = row.ResponseRate >= row.ResponseTarget ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444';
                        return `
                        <div style="background:var(--bg-secondary);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;padding:6px 10px;min-width:120px;flex:1;">
                            <div style="font-size:.65rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--acc);margin-bottom:4px;">${row.Period}</div>
                            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:2px;">
                                <span style="font-size:.62rem;color:var(--t3);">Response Rate</span>
                                <span style="font-size:.68rem;font-weight:700;color:${rrColor};">${row.ResponseRate != null ? row.ResponseRate + '%' : 'N/A'} <span style="color:var(--t3);font-weight:400;">/ ${row.ResponseTarget != null ? row.ResponseTarget + '%' : 'N/A'}</span></span>
                            </div>
                            <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;">
                                <span style="font-size:.62rem;color:var(--t3);">RNPS Score</span>
                                <span style="font-size:.68rem;font-weight:700;color:${rnpsColor};">${row.RNPS != null ? row.RNPS : 'N/A'} <span style="color:var(--t3);font-weight:400;">/ ${row.RNPSTarget != null ? row.RNPSTarget : 'N/A'}</span></span>
                            </div>
                        </div>`;
                    }).join('')}
                </div>`;
        }

    // ── ETA block ─────────────────────────────────────────
    const etaStats = window.ETA_LOADED ? etaGetManagerStats(function(r) { return r.SM === m.name; }) : null;
let etaHtml = '';
if (window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE) {
    etaHtml = '';
} else if (!window.ANALYTICS_LOADED || !window.ETA_LOADED) {
            etaHtml = `
                <div style="margin-top:8px;padding-top:8px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);font-size:.72rem;color:var(--t3);">
                    <i data-lucide="layers" style="width:11px;height:11px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:3px;"></i>
                    Click <strong style="color:var(--acc);">Load RNPS &amp; ETA Analytics</strong> above to view ETA data
                </div>`;
        } else if (etaStats && (etaStats.tt.total > 0 || etaStats.events.total > 0 || etaStats.activities.total > 0)) {
            function miniRow(label, s) {
                if (s.total === 0) return '';
                return `
                <div style="margin-bottom:5px;">
                    <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:2px;">
                        <span style="font-size:.62rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--t2);">${label}</span>
                        <span style="font-size:.6rem;color:var(--t3);">Total: ${s.total}</span>
                    </div>
                    <div style="display:flex;gap:3px;">
                        <span style="flex:1;background:rgba(245,158,11,.12);border:1px solid rgba(245,158,11,.25);border-radius:4px;padding:2px 3px;text-align:center;font-size:.6rem;font-weight:700;color:#f59e0b;" title="Assigned">${s.assigned}</span>
                        <span style="flex:1;background:rgba(59,130,246,.12);border:1px solid rgba(59,130,246,.25);border-radius:4px;padding:2px 3px;text-align:center;font-size:.6rem;font-weight:700;color:#3b82f6;" title="In Progress">${s.inprogress}</span>
                        <span style="flex:1;background:rgba(16,185,129,.12);border:1px solid rgba(16,185,129,.25);border-radius:4px;padding:2px 3px;text-align:center;font-size:.6rem;font-weight:700;color:#10b981;" title="Completed">${s.completed}</span>
                        <span style="flex:1;background:rgba(107,114,128,.12);border:1px solid rgba(107,114,128,.25);border-radius:4px;padding:2px 3px;text-align:center;font-size:.6rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--t3);" title="Other">${s.other}</span>
                    </div>
                </div>`;
            }

            etaHtml = `
            <div style="margin-top:8px;padding-top:8px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);">
                <div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center;margin-bottom:5px;">
                    <div style="font-size:.62rem;font-weight:700;color:var(--t3);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.05em;">ETA — ${currentYear}</div>
                    <div style="display:flex;gap:4px;font-size:.55rem;color:var(--t3);">
                        <span style="background:rgba(245,158,11,.15);border-radius:3px;padding:1px 4px;">🟡 Assigned</span>
                        <span style="background:rgba(59,130,246,.15);border-radius:3px;padding:1px 4px;">🔵 In Prog</span>
                        <span style="background:rgba(16,185,129,.15);border-radius:3px;padding:1px 4px;">🟢 Done</span>
                        <span style="background:rgba(107,114,128,.15);border-radius:3px;padding:1px 4px;">⚫ Other</span>
                    </div>
                    <div style="position:relative;display:inline-block;">
                        <span id="etaInfoBtn_sm_${key}"
                            onclick="etaShowInfoPopup(event,'sm_${key}')"
                            style="cursor:pointer;width:16px;height:16px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--bg-secondary);border:1px solid var(--border);display:inline-flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:.6rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--acc);">i</span>
                        <div id="etaInfoPopup_sm_${key}"
                            style="display:none;position:absolute;right:0;top:20px;z-index:999;background:var(--bg-card);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:10px;box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.2);padding:10px 12px;min-width:200px;">
                            <div style="font-size:.7rem;font-weight:800;color:var(--t1);margin-bottom:6px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);padding-bottom:4px;">Detailed Breakdown</div>
                            ${etaDetailHtml('TTs', etaStats.ttDetail)}
                            ${etaDetailHtml('Events', etaStats.evDetail)}
                            ${etaDetailHtml('Activities', etaStats.actDetail)}
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                ${miniRow('Trouble Tickets', etaStats.tt)}
                ${miniRow('Events', etaStats.events)}
                ${miniRow('Activities', etaStats.activities)}
            </div>`;
        }

        return `
            <div class="manager-row ${isSelected ? 'selected' : ''}" onclick="selectSM('${m.name}')">
                <div class="rank-badge ${rankClass}">${i + 1}</div>
                <div class="manager-name-col">
                    <div class="manager-name">${m.name}</div>
                    <div class="manager-tag">${tag}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="stat-col">
                    <div class="stat-label">Accounts</div>
                    <div class="stat-value">${m.count}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="stat-col">
                    <div class="stat-label">Revenue</div>
                    <div class="stat-value">${formatCurrency(m.totalR)}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="stat-col">
                    <div class="stat-label">${lastThree[2].label}</div>
                    <div class="stat-value">${formatCurrency(m.month3)}</div>
                </div>
                <div class="stat-col">
                    <div class="stat-label">Growth</div>
                    <div class="stat-value" style="color: ${m.growth >= 0 ? '#10b981' : '#ef4444'}">${m.growth}%</div>
                </div>
                <div class="progress-bar-col">
                    <div class="progress-label">Account Share: ${m.cShare}%</div>
                    <div class="progress-bar">
                        <div class="progress-fill" style="width: ${m.cShare}%"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                <div class="progress-bar-col">
                    <div class="progress-label">Revenue Share: ${m.rShare}%</div>
                    <div class="progress-bar">
                        <div class="progress-fill" style="width: ${m.rShare}%"></div>
                    </div>
                </div>
                ${DOJ_DATA[m.name] ? `<div class="sm-doj-col"><div class="stat-label">Joined</div><div class="stat-value">${DOJ_DATA[m.name].doj}</div><div class="stat-sub">${DOJ_DATA[m.name].tenure} exp</div></div>` : ''}
                ${rnpsHtml}
                ${etaHtml}
            </div>`;
    }).join('');
}        function getColors() {
            const theme = document.body.getAttribute('data-theme');
            const isDuralux = theme === 'duralux' || theme === 'duralux-dark';
            const isDark = theme === 'dark' || theme === 'duralux-dark';
            return {
                text: isDark ? '#f3e8ff' : (isDuralux ? '#0f1a3e' : '#1e1133'),
                secondary: isDark ? '#c4b5fd' : (isDuralux ? '#3d4f8a' : '#4b3f6b'),
                grid: isDark ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.08)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.06)',
                primary: isDuralux ? '#4c6fff' : (isDark ? '#c084fc' : '#a855f7'),
                accent: isDuralux ? '#818cf8' : (isDark ? '#c084fc' : '#a855f7'),
                teamBlue: isDuralux ? '#60a5fa' : '#a855f7',
                teamPurple: isDuralux ? '#3b82f6' : '#c724b1'
            };
        }

        function renderCharts() {
            const colors = getColors();

            // ✅ Calculate totals for percentages
            const totalRevenue = filtered.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);

            // ✅ Get managers based on current selection
            let managers = [];
            let revenueData = [];
            let accountsData = [];
            let revenueShareData = [];

            // 🔥 SCALING FACTOR: Make accounts visible on chart (multiply by 100)
            const ACCOUNT_SCALE = 100;

            if (selectedLM) {
                // Show Service Managers under selected Line Manager
                const sms = [...new Set(filtered.filter(a => a.lm === selectedLM).map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean);
                managers = sms;

                sms.forEach(sm => {
                    const smAccounts = filtered.filter(a => a.sm === sm);
                    const smRevenue = smAccounts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);

                    revenueData.push(smRevenue / 1000); // in K
                    accountsData.push(smAccounts.length * ACCOUNT_SCALE); // 🔥 SCALED
                    revenueShareData.push(totalRevenue > 0 ? (smRevenue / totalRevenue * 100) : 0);
                });
            } else if (selectedSM) {
                // Show only selected Service Manager
                managers = [selectedSM];
                const smAccounts = filtered.filter(a => a.sm === selectedSM);
                const smRevenue = smAccounts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);

                revenueData.push(smRevenue / 1000);
                accountsData.push(smAccounts.length * ACCOUNT_SCALE); // 🔥 SCALED
                revenueShareData.push(totalRevenue > 0 ? (smRevenue / totalRevenue * 100) : 0);
            } else {
                // Show all Line Managers
                const lms = [...new Set(filtered.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean);
                managers = lms;

                lms.forEach(lm => {
                    const lmAccounts = filtered.filter(a => a.lm === lm);
                    const lmRevenue = lmAccounts.reduce((sum, a) => sum + a.avg, 0);

                    revenueData.push(lmRevenue / 1000);
                    accountsData.push(lmAccounts.length * ACCOUNT_SCALE); // 🔥 SCALED
                    revenueShareData.push(totalRevenue > 0 ? (lmRevenue / totalRevenue * 100) : 0);
                });
            }

            // ✅ WORKLOAD & REVENUE CHART (Bars + Lines) - ENHANCED
            // ✅ WORKLOAD & REVENUE CHART (Bars + Lines) - ENHANCED WITH LABELS
            if (charts.trend) charts.trend.destroy();

            // 🔧 Calculate account share percentages
            const totalAccounts = filtered.length;
            const accountShareData = [];

            if (selectedLM) {
                const sms = [...new Set(filtered.filter(a => a.lm === selectedLM).map(a => a.sm))].filter(Boolean);
                sms.forEach(sm => {
                    const smAccounts = filtered.filter(a => a.sm === sm);
                    const accountShare = totalAccounts > 0 ? (smAccounts.length / totalAccounts * 100) : 0;
                    accountShareData.push(accountShare);
                });
            } else if (selectedSM) {
                const smAccounts = filtered.filter(a => a.sm === selectedSM);
                const accountShare = totalAccounts > 0 ? (smAccounts.length / totalAccounts * 100) : 0;
                accountShareData.push(accountShare);
            } else {
                const lms = [...new Set(filtered.map(a => a.lm))].filter(Boolean);
                lms.forEach(lm => {
                    const lmAccounts = filtered.filter(a => a.lm === lm);
                    const accountShare = totalAccounts > 0 ? (lmAccounts.length / totalAccounts * 100) : 0;
                    accountShareData.push(accountShare);
                });
            }

            charts.trend = new Chart(document.getElementById('trendChart'), {
                type: 'bar',
                data: {
                    labels: managers,
                    datasets: [{
                            label: 'Revenue (K AED)',
                            data: revenueData,
                            backgroundColor: colors.teamBlue,
                            borderColor: colors.teamBlue,
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            borderRadius: 8,
                            maxBarThickness: 30,
                            yAxisID: 'y',
                            order: 3
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Total Accounts',
                            data: accountsData,
                            backgroundColor: colors.teamPurple,
                            borderColor: colors.teamPurple,
                            borderWidth: 2,
                            borderRadius: 8,
                            maxBarThickness: 30,
                            yAxisID: 'y',
                            order: 4
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Revenue Share (%)',
                            data: revenueShareData,
                            type: 'line',
                            borderColor: '#f97316',
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(249, 115, 22, 0.1)',
                            borderWidth: 3,
                            borderDash: [8, 4],
                            pointRadius: 6,
                            pointBackgroundColor: '#f97316',
                            pointBorderColor: '#fff',
                            pointBorderWidth: 2,
                            pointHoverRadius: 8,
                            tension: 0.3,
                            yAxisID: 'y1',
                            order: 1
                        },
                        {
                            label: 'Account Share (%)',
                            data: accountShareData,
                            type: 'line',
                            borderColor: '#10b981',
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.1)',
                            borderWidth: 3,
                            borderDash: [8, 4],
                            pointRadius: 6,
                            pointBackgroundColor: '#10b981',
                            pointBorderColor: '#fff',
                            pointBorderWidth: 2,
                            pointHoverRadius: 8,
                            tension: 0.3,
                            yAxisID: 'y1',
                            order: 2
                        }
                    ]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: {
                            display: true,
                            position: 'bottom',
                            labels: {
                                color: colors.text,
                                font: {
                                    size: 11,
                                    weight: '600'
                                },
                                padding: 8,
                                usePointStyle: true,
                                pointStyle: 'circle'
                            }
                        },
                        tooltip: {
                            backgroundColor: 'rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.8)',
                            titleFont: {
                                size: 14,
                                weight: 'bold'
                            },
                            bodyFont: {
                                size: 13
                            },
                            padding: 12,
                            callbacks: {
                                label: (context) => {
                                    const label = context.dataset.label;
                                    const value = context.parsed.y;
                                    const managerName = context.label;

                                    if (label.includes('Revenue (K')) {
                                        return `💰 Revenue: ${formatCurrency(value * 1000)}`;
                                    } else if (label.includes('Total Accounts')) {
                                        // ✅ Show both parent and child counts
                                        const allFiltered = window.ALL_FILTERED || [];
                                        let parentCount = 0;
                                        let childCount = 0;

                                        if (selectedLM) {
                                            const accounts = allFiltered.filter(a => a.sm === managerName);
                                            parentCount = accounts.filter(a => a.type === 'Group').length;
                                            childCount = accounts.filter(a => a.type === 'Child').length;
                                        } else {
                                            const accounts = allFiltered.filter(a => a.lm === managerName);
                                            parentCount = accounts.filter(a => a.type === 'Group').length;
                                            childCount = accounts.filter(a => a.type === 'Child').length;
                                        }

                                        return `📊 Groups: ${parentCount} | Children: ${childCount} | Total: ${parentCount + childCount}`;
                                    } else if (label.includes('Revenue Share')) {
                                        return `📈 Revenue Share: ${value.toFixed(1)}%`;
                                    } else if (label.includes('Account Share')) {
                                        return `🎯 Account Share: ${value.toFixed(1)}%`;
                                    }
                                    return `${label}: ${value}`;
                                }
                            }
                        },
                    },
                    scales: {
                        x: {
                            ticks: {
                                color: colors.secondary,
                                font: {
                                    size: 10,
                                    weight: '600'
                                },
                                maxRotation: 35,
                                minRotation: 0
                            },
                            grid: {
                                display: false
                            }
                        },
                        y: {
                            type: 'linear',
                            display: false,
                            position: 'left',
                            beginAtZero: true,
                            grid: {
                                color: colors.grid,
                                lineWidth: 1
                            }
                        },
                        y1: {
                            type: 'linear',
                            display: true,
                            position: 'right',
                            beginAtZero: true,
                            max: 100,
                            ticks: {
                                color: colors.secondary,
                                font: {
                                    size: 10,
                                    weight: '700'
                                },
                                callback: function(value) {
                                    return value + '%';
                                }
                            },
                            grid: {
                                display: false
                            },
                            title: {
                                display: true,
                                text: 'Share (%)',
                                color: colors.text,
                                font: {
                                    size: 14,
                                    weight: '700'
                                },
                                padding: {
                                    top: 10
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    },
                    interaction: {
                        mode: 'index',
                        intersect: false
                    }
                },
                plugins: [{
                    id: 'barLabels',
                    afterDatasetsDraw: function(chart) {
                        const ctx = chart.ctx;

                        chart.data.datasets.forEach((dataset, datasetIndex) => {
                            // Only show labels on bar datasets (not lines)
                            if (dataset.type === 'line') return;

                            const meta = chart.getDatasetMeta(datasetIndex);

                            meta.data.forEach((bar, index) => {
                                const value = dataset.data[index];

                                // Get the corresponding percentage from lines
                                let percentage = '';
                                if (dataset.label.includes('Revenue')) {
                                    const revenueShareDataset = chart.data.datasets.find(d => d.label === 'Revenue Share (%)');
                                    if (revenueShareDataset) {
                                        percentage = revenueShareDataset.data[index].toFixed(1) + '%';
                                    }
                                } else if (dataset.label.includes('Accounts')) {
                                    const accountShareDataset = chart.data.datasets.find(d => d.label === 'Account Share (%)');
                                    if (accountShareDataset) {
                                        percentage = accountShareDataset.data[index].toFixed(1) + '%';
                                    }
                                }

                                // Format the main value
                                let mainLabel;
                                if (dataset.label.includes('Revenue')) {
                                    mainLabel = formatCurrency(value * 1000);
                                } else if (dataset.label.includes('Accounts')) {
                                    mainLabel = Math.round(value / 100).toString();
                                }

                                // Position - MORE space above bars
                                const x = bar.x;
                                let y;
                                if (dataset.label.includes('Revenue')) {
                                    y = bar.y - 26;
                                } else {
                                    y = bar.y - 14;
                                }

                                // Draw text with stroke for visibility
                                ctx.save();
                                ctx.textAlign = 'center';
                                ctx.textBaseline = 'bottom';
                                ctx.font = 'bold 9px Arial';

                                // White stroke (outline) for better visibility
                                ctx.strokeStyle = 'rgba(255, 255, 255, 0.8)';
                                ctx.lineWidth = 3;

                                // Use bright, contrasting colors
                                const textColor = dataset.label.includes('Revenue') ? '#1e40af' : '#7c3aed';
                                ctx.fillStyle = textColor;

                                // Line 1: Main value (with stroke)
                                ctx.strokeText(mainLabel, x, y);
                                ctx.fillText(mainLabel, x, y);

                                // Line 2: Percentage (with stroke)
                                if (percentage) {
                                    ctx.strokeText(percentage, x, y + 15);
                                    ctx.fillText(percentage, x, y + 15);
                                }

                                ctx.restore();
                            });
                        });
                    }
                }]
            });

            // TYPE CHART (unchanged)
            if (charts.type) charts.type.destroy();
            const allFiltered = window.ALL_FILTERED || [];
            const groupC = allFiltered.filter(a => a.type === 'Group').length;
            const childC = allFiltered.filter(a => a.type === 'Child').length;

            charts.type = new Chart(document.getElementById('typeChart'), {
                type: 'doughnut',
                data: {
                    labels: ['Group', 'Child'],
                    datasets: [{
                        data: [groupC, childC],
                        backgroundColor: [colors.teamBlue, colors.teamPurple],
                        borderWidth: 0
                    }]
                },
                options: {
                    responsive: true,
                    maintainAspectRatio: false,
                    plugins: {
                        legend: {
                            position: 'bottom',
                            labels: {
                                color: colors.secondary,
                                font: {
                                    size: 13,
                                    weight: '600'
                                },
                                padding: 15
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            });
        }
        let agGridApi = null;

        function SmSetColumnFilter() {}
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.init = function (params) {
            this.params = params;
            this.selected = new Set();
            this.gui = document.createElement('div');
            this.gui.className = 'sm-ag-set-filter';
            this._buildGui();
        };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype._cellValue = function (data) {
            var field = this.params.colDef.field;
            var v = data[field];
            if (v === null || v === undefined || v === '') return '—';
            if (this.params.colDef.type === 'numericColumn' || typeof v === 'number') {
                return typeof formatCurrency === 'function' ? formatCurrency(v) : String(v);
            }
            return String(v);
        };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype._allValues = function () {
            var values = new Set(), self = this;
            this.params.api.forEachNode(function (node) {
                if (node.data) values.add(self._cellValue(node.data));
            });
            return Array.from(values).sort(function (a, b) { return a.localeCompare(b); });
        };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype._buildGui = function () {
            var self = this, all = this._allValues();
            this.gui.innerHTML = '';
            var search = document.createElement('input');
            search.type = 'text';
            search.placeholder = 'Search...';
            search.className = 'sm-ag-set-search';
            this.gui.appendChild(search);
            var list = document.createElement('div');
            list.className = 'sm-ag-set-list';
            this.gui.appendChild(list);
            var render = function (term) {
                list.innerHTML = '';
                all.filter(function (v) { return !term || v.toLowerCase().indexOf(term.toLowerCase()) >= 0; }).forEach(function (v) {
                    var row = document.createElement('label');
                    row.className = 'sm-ag-set-option';
                    var cb = document.createElement('input');
                    cb.type = 'checkbox';
                    cb.checked = self.selected.has(v);
                    cb.onchange = function () {
                        if (cb.checked) self.selected.add(v); else self.selected.delete(v);
                        self.params.filterChangedCallback();
                    };
                    row.appendChild(cb);
                    row.appendChild(document.createTextNode(' ' + v));
                    list.appendChild(row);
                });
            };
            render('');
            search.oninput = function () { render(search.value); };
            var actions = document.createElement('div');
            actions.className = 'sm-ag-set-actions';
            var btnAll = document.createElement('button');
            btnAll.type = 'button';
            btnAll.textContent = 'Select all';
            btnAll.onclick = function () { all.forEach(function (v) { self.selected.add(v); }); render(search.value); self.params.filterChangedCallback(); };
            var btnClear = document.createElement('button');
            btnClear.type = 'button';
            btnClear.textContent = 'Clear';
            btnClear.onclick = function () { self.selected.clear(); render(search.value); self.params.filterChangedCallback(); };
            actions.appendChild(btnAll);
            actions.appendChild(btnClear);
            this.gui.appendChild(actions);
        };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.getGui = function () { return this.gui; };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.isFilterActive = function () { return this.selected.size > 0; };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.doesFilterPass = function (params) {
            if (!this.selected.size) return true;
            return this.selected.has(this._cellValue(params.data));
        };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.getModel = function () { return this.selected.size ? { values: Array.from(this.selected) } : null; };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.setModel = function (model) {
            this.selected = new Set(model && model.values ? model.values : []);
            this._buildGui();
        };
        SmSetColumnFilter.prototype.destroy = function () {};

        function smEnhanceColDef(col) {
            if (col.field === 'actions') return col;
            col.filter = SmSetColumnFilter;
            return col;
        }

        function renderTable() {
            if (window.TSM_SE_ACTIVE && typeof window.tsmSeRenderTable === 'function') {
                return window.tsmSeRenderTable();
            }

            smDestroyTsmSeGridOnly();

            const gridDiv = document.getElementById('myGrid');
            if (!gridDiv) return;
            const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();

            // Build parent rows with children nested
            const parentRows = filtered.map(parent => {
                const children = (window.ALL_FILTERED || []).filter(a =>
                    a.type === 'Child' && a.parent === parent.code && a.code !== parent.code
                );

          
                return {
                    ...parent,
                    _children: children,
                    _hasChildren: children.length > 0,
                    _isParent: true
                };
            });

         
            const columnDefs = [{
                    field: 'code',
                    headerName: 'Account Code',
                    pinned: 'left',
                    width: 180,
                    cellRenderer: params => {
                        const data = params.data;
                        if (data._isParent && data._hasChildren) {
                            const expanded = data._expanded ? true : false;
                            const icon = expanded ? '▼' : '▶';
                            const count = data._children ? data._children.length : 0;
                            return `<span style="cursor:pointer; font-weight:700;" onclick="toggleChildren('${data.code}')">
                <span style="display:inline-block; width:24px; color:var(--accent); font-size:16px; font-weight:900;">${icon}</span>
                ${data.code} <span style="font-size:10px; color:var(--text-secondary); font-weight:500;">(${count})</span>
            </span>`;
                        } else if (data._isChild) {
                            return `<span style="padding-left:28px; color:var(--text-secondary); font-weight:500;">↳ ${data.code}</span>`;
                        }
                        return `<span style="font-weight:700;">${data.code}</span>`;
                    }
                },
                {
                    field: 'parent',
                    headerName: 'Parent Code',
                    width: 140
                },
                {
                    field: 'customer',
                    headerName: 'Customer Name',
                    width: 200
                },
                {
                    field: 'type',
                    headerName: 'Type',
                    width: 100,
                    cellRenderer: params => {
                        if (params.data._isChild) {
                            return `<span class="status-badge badge-warning" style="opacity:0.7;">Child</span>`;
                        }
                        const badge = params.value === 'Group' ? 'badge-success' : 'badge-warning';
                        return `<span class="status-badge ${badge}">${params.value}</span>`;
                    }
                },
                {
                    field: 'team',
                    headerName: 'Team',
                    width: 110
                },
                {
                    field: 'lm',
                    headerName: 'Line Manager',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'sm',
                    headerName: 'Service Manager',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'secondarySm',
                    headerName: 'Secondary SM',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'am',
                    headerName: 'Account Manager',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'ad',
                    headerName: 'Account Director',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'pocName',
                    headerName: 'POC Name',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'pocEmail',
                    headerName: 'POC Email',
                    width: 180
                },
                {
                    field: 'pocPhone',
                    headerName: 'POC Phone',
                    width: 140
                },
                {
                    field: 'accountType',
                    headerName: 'Account Type',
                    width: 150
                },
                {
                    field: 'rnpsEligibility',
                    headerName: 'RNPS Eligibility',
                    width: 150
                },
                ...lastThree.map((month, index) => ({
                    field: month.key,
                    headerName: month.label,
                    width: 150,
                    type: 'numericColumn',
                    autoHeight: true, // ✅ Let row expand for 2 lines
                    cellRenderer: params => {
                        const value = params.value || 0;
                        const data = params.data;

                        // ✅ CHILD rows - simple display
                        if (data._isChild) {
                            return `<div style="opacity: 0.6; text-align: right; padding: 8px 0;">${formatCurrency(value)}</div>`;
                        }

                        // ✅ PARENT rows WITH children - show parent + sum
                        if (data._isParent && data._hasChildren && data._children && data._children.length > 0) {
                            const childrenSum = data._children.reduce((sum, child) => {
                                return sum + (child[month.key] || 0);
                            }, 0);

                            return `
                <div style="text-align: right; padding: 8px 0;">
                    <div style="font-weight: 700; font-size: 14px;">${formatCurrency(value)}</div>
                    <div style="font-size: 10px; color: var(--text-secondary); font-weight: 500; margin-top: 4px;">Child Sum: ${formatCurrency(childrenSum)}</div>
                </div>
            `;
                        }

                        // ✅ PARENT rows WITHOUT children - simple display
                        return `<div style="font-weight: 700; text-align: right; padding: 8px 0;">${formatCurrency(value)}</div>`;
                    },
                    cellStyle: params => {
                        if (index === 2 && params.data.isRevDrop && params.data._isParent) {
                            return {
                                color: '#ef4444'
                            };
                        }
                        return null;
                    }
                })),
                {
                    field: 'avg',
                    headerName: 'Avg Revenue',
                    width: 130,
                    valueFormatter: params => formatCurrency(params.value),
                    type: 'numericColumn',
                    cellStyle: params => {
                        if (params.data._isChild) return {
                            opacity: '0.6'
                        };
                        return {
                            fontWeight: '700'
                        };
                    }
                },
                {
                    field: 'actions',
                    headerName: 'Actions',
                    width: 120,
                    pinned: 'right',
                    sortable: false,
                    filter: false,
                    autoHeight: true,
                   cellRenderer: params => {
    const a = params.data;

    // Read Only — no actions at all
if (USER_CONTEXT.isReadOnly || USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) return '<div></div>';
    // Children only get Edit button
    if (a._isChild) {
                            let childHtml = '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:3px;padding:4px 2px;">';
                            let canEdit = false;
                            if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) canEdit = true;
                            else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager') canEdit = (a.lm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);
                            else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') canEdit = (a.sm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);

                            if (canEdit) {
                                childHtml += `<button type="button" class="export-btn" style="padding:3px 7px;font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;" onclick="openEditRequest('${a.code}')">
                    <i data-lucide="pencil" style="width: 12px; height: 12px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 4px;"></i>Edit
                </button>`;
                            }
                            childHtml += '</div>';
                            return childHtml;
                        }

                        let canEdit = false;
                        if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) canEdit = true;
                        else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager') canEdit = (a.lm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);
                        else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') canEdit = (a.sm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);

                        const canTransfer = USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin || (a.lm === USER_CONTEXT.userName) || (a.sm === USER_CONTEXT.userName);

                        const hasTransfer = (a.isRevDrop || a.isRevUpgrade) && canTransfer && a._isParent;

                  const transferAlreadyRaised = a._isParent && a.requestType === 'Transfer' &&
                            (a.requestStatus === 'Not Onboarded' || a.requestStatus === 'AM_Approved' || a.requestStatus === 'Transfer_Pending');
                        let html = `<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:3px;padding:4px 2px;">`;
if (transferAlreadyRaised) {
                            var tStatus = a.requestStatus;
                            var tLabel, tColor, tIcon;
                            if (tStatus === 'AM_Approved') {
                                tLabel = 'Transfer: AM Approved';
                                tColor = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#10b981,#059669)';
                                tIcon = 'check-circle';
                            } else {
                                tLabel = 'Pending AM Approval';
                                tColor = 'linear-gradient(135deg,#f97316,#ea580c)';
                                tIcon = 'hourglass';
                            }
                            html += '<button type="button" class="export-btn" style="padding:3px 7px;font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;background:' + tColor + ';color:#fff;cursor:default;opacity:0.85;" disabled>' +
                                '<i data-lucide="' + tIcon + '" style="width:12px;height:12px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:4px;"></i>' + tLabel + '</button>';

                            // Send reminder button: 3+ days pending AM action (Transfer_Pending / Not Onboarded)
                            const isPendingAM = (a.requestStatus === 'Transfer_Pending' || a.requestStatus === 'Not Onboarded');
                            const overdue = (a.transferDaysPassed !== null && a.transferDaysPassed !== undefined && a.transferDaysPassed >= 3);
                            if (isPendingAM && overdue) {
                                const esc = (v) => String(v || '').replace(/\\/g, '\\\\').replace(/'/g, "\\'");
                                html += `<button type="button" class="reset-btn" style="padding:3px 7px;font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;"
onclick="sendTransferReminderEmailMain('${esc(a.amEmail)}','${esc(a.adEmail)}','${esc(a.smEmail)}','${esc(a.lmEmail)}','${esc(a.code)}','${esc(a.customer)}','${esc(a.team)}','${esc(a.proposedTeam)}',${a.transferDaysPassed || 0})">
<i data-lucide="mail" style="width:12px;height:12px;display:inline-block;vertical-align:middle;margin-right:4px;"></i>Send Reminder</button>`;
                            }
                        } else if (hasTransfer) {
                            html += `<button type="button" class="export-btn" style="padding:3px 7px;font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#f97316,#ea580c);color:#fff;"
            onclick="openTransferRequest('${a.code}', '${a.customer.replace(/'/g, "\\'")}', '${a.team}', '${a.lm}', '${a.sm}', '${a.am}', '${a.ad}')">
                <i data-lucide="repeat" style="width: 12px; height: 12px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 4px;"></i>Transfer
            </button>`;
                        }
                        if (canEdit) {
                            html += `<button type="button" class="export-btn" style="padding:3px 7px;font-size:10px;white-space:nowrap;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;" onclick="openEditRequest('${a.code}')">
                <i data-lucide="pencil" style="width: 12px; height: 12px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 4px;"></i>Edit
            </button>`;
                        }

                        html += '</div>';
                        return html;
                    },
                    onCellClicked: params => {
                        setTimeout(() => lucide.createIcons(), 100);
                    }
                }
            ];

            // Store parent data globally for expand/collapse
            window.PARENT_ROWS = parentRows;
            window.CURRENT_TABLE_DATA = [...parentRows];

            const gridOptions = {
                columnDefs: columnDefs.map(function (col) {
                    if (!col.field || col.field === 'actions') return col;
                    return smEnhanceColDef(Object.assign({}, col));
                }),
                rowData: parentRows,
                defaultColDef: {
                    sortable: true,
                    filter: true,
                    resizable: true,
                    minWidth: 100
                },
                pagination: true,
                paginationPageSize: 50,
                paginationPageSizeSelector: [25, 50, 100, 200],
                rowHeight: 60,
                headerHeight: 50,
                animateRows: true,
                enableCellTextSelection: true,
                suppressMenuHide: false,
               onGridReady: params => {
                    agGridApi = params.api;
                },
                isExternalFilterPresent: () => {
                    return !!window._TRANSFER_FILTER_VAL;
                },
                doesExternalFilterPass: node => {
                    var val = window._TRANSFER_FILTER_VAL;
                    if (!val) return true;
                    var d = node.data;
                    if (val === 'Transfer_Pending') {
                        return d.requestType === 'Transfer' && (d.requestStatus === 'Transfer_Pending' || d.requestStatus === 'Not Onboarded');
                    }
                    if (val === 'Transfer_Overdue_3D') {
                        return d.requestType === 'Transfer' &&
                            (d.requestStatus === 'Transfer_Pending' || d.requestStatus === 'Not Onboarded') &&
                            (d.transferDaysPassed !== null && d.transferDaysPassed !== undefined && d.transferDaysPassed >= 3);
                    }
                    if (val === 'AM_Approved') {
                        return d.requestType === 'Transfer' && d.requestStatus === 'AM_Approved';
                    }
                    return true;
                },
                getRowStyle: params => {
                    if (params.data._isChild) {
                        return {
                            background: 'rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.06)',
                            borderLeft: '3px solid var(--accent)'
                        };
                    }
                    if (params.data.isRevDrop) {
                        return {
                            background: 'rgba(239, 68, 68, 0.2)'
                        };
                    }
                    if (params.data.isRevUpgrade) {
                        return {
                            background: 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.2)'
                        };
                    }
                    return null;
                },
                getRowId: params => params.data._isChild ? 'child_' + params.data.code : 'parent_' + params.data.code
            };

            if (agGridApi) {
                agGridApi.destroy();
            }

            gridDiv.innerHTML = '';
            agGrid.createGrid(gridDiv, gridOptions);
        }

        function toggleChildren(parentCode) {
            if (!agGridApi) return;

            const parentRow = window.PARENT_ROWS.find(p => p.code === parentCode);
            if (!parentRow || !parentRow._hasChildren) return;

            // Toggle expanded state
            parentRow._expanded = !parentRow._expanded;

            // Rebuild row data
            const newRowData = [];
            window.PARENT_ROWS.forEach(parent => {
                newRowData.push(parent);
                if (parent._expanded && parent._children) {
                    parent._children.forEach(child => {
                        newRowData.push({
                            ...child,
                            _isChild: true,
                            _isParent: false,
                            _hasChildren: false
                        });
                    });
                }
            });

            agGridApi.setGridOption('rowData', newRowData);

            // ✅ FORCE REFRESH to update the icon
            agGridApi.refreshCells({
                force: true
            });

            setTimeout(() => {
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
            }, 100);
        }

       function searchAGGrid(searchText) {
            if (!agGridApi) return;
            agGridApi.setGridOption('quickFilterText', searchText);
        }

        function applyTransferFilter() {
            var val = document.getElementById('transferStatusFilterMain').value;
            if (!agGridApi) return;
            if (!val) {
                // IMPORTANT: this grid uses an external filter via window._TRANSFER_FILTER_VAL.
                // If we don't clear it, "All accounts" stays filtered even after resetting.
                window._TRANSFER_FILTER_VAL = '';
                agGridApi.setFilterModel(null);
                agGridApi.onFilterChanged();
                return;
            }
            // Use external filter
            window._TRANSFER_FILTER_VAL = val;
            agGridApi.onFilterChanged();
        }

        function sendTransferReminderEmailMain(amEmail, adEmail, smEmail, lmEmail, code, customer, oldTeam, newTeam, daysPassed) {
            const safeDays = (daysPassed === null || daysPassed === undefined) ? '3+' : String(daysPassed);
            const subj = encodeURIComponent(`[REMINDER] Transfer Request Pending AM Action - ACC# ${code} | ${customer}`);
            const body = encodeURIComponent(
                `Dear AM / AD,

This is a reminder that the following transfer request has been pending AM action for ${safeDays} day(s).

Account: ${code} - ${customer}
Current Team: ${oldTeam}
Proposed Team: ${newTeam}

Please log in to the Service Management Dashboard and approve or reject the request.

Note: If no action is taken, the transfer request will be auto-approved.

Best regards,
${USER_CONTEXT.userName}`
            );

            const to = [amEmail, adEmail].filter(Boolean).join(';');
            const cc = [smEmail, lmEmail].filter(Boolean).join(';');
            window.location.href = `mailto:${encodeURIComponent(to)}?subject=${subj}&body=${body}` + (cc ? `&cc=${encodeURIComponent(cc)}` : '');
        }

        function searchTable() {
            const search = document.getElementById('searchBox').value.toLowerCase();
            const tbody = document.getElementById('tbody');
            if (!tbody) return;

            const rows = tbody.getElementsByTagName('tr');
            Array.from(rows).forEach(row => {
                // Get only td elements, exclude buttons
                const cells = row.getElementsByTagName('td');
                let rowText = '';
                for (let cell of cells) {
