                    // Skip the last cell (Actions column with buttons)
                    if (cell !== cells[cells.length - 1]) {
                        rowText += cell.textContent.toLowerCase() + ' ';
                    }
                }
                row.style.display = rowText.includes(search) ? '' : 'none';
            });
        }

        function smGetExportColumns() {
            if (!agGridApi) return [];
            return agGridApi.getColumns().filter(function (col) {
                return col.getColId() !== 'actions';
            });
        }

        function smFormatExportCellValue(col, row) {
            const colDef = col.getColDef();
            const field = colDef.field;
            let raw = field ? row[field] : '';

            if (field === 'code') {
                return row._isExportChild ? '  ↳ ' + (row.code || '') : (row.code || '');
            }
            if (field === 'type') {
                return row._isExportChild ? 'Child' : (row.type || '');
            }
            if (field === 'parent') {
                return row.parent || '-';
            }
            if (colDef.type === 'numericColumn' || field === 'avg') {
                return formatCurrency(raw || 0);
            }
            if (field === 'accountType' || field === 'rnpsEligibility') {
                return raw || '';
            }
            return raw != null && raw !== '' ? raw : '';
        }

        function exportToExcel() {
            if (!agGridApi) return;

            const today = new Date();
            const dateStr = today.toLocaleDateString('en-GB') + " " + today.toLocaleTimeString('en-GB', {
                hour: '2-digit',
                minute: '2-digit'
            });

            const exportColumns = smGetExportColumns();
            const colCount = exportColumns.length || 1;
            const thStyle = 'background-color:#a855f7;color:white;font-weight:bold;padding:10px;';

            // Build export data: parents with their children underneath
            const exportData = [];
            const parentAccounts = filtered; // Parents only
            const allAccounts = window.ALL_FILTERED || [];

            parentAccounts.forEach(parent => {
                exportData.push({
                    ...parent,
                    _isExportParent: true
                });
                // Find and add children
                const children = allAccounts.filter(a =>
                    a.type === 'Child' && a.parent === parent.code && a.code !== parent.code
                );
                children.forEach(child => {
                    exportData.push({
                        ...child,
                        _isExportChild: true
                    });
                });
            });

            let html = '<html><head><meta charset="utf-8"></head><body>';
            html += '<table border="1" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="4">';

            html += '<tr><td colspan="' + colCount + '" style="background-color:#a855f7;color:white;font-size:16px;font-weight:bold;text-align:center;padding:12px;">';
            html += 'Service Management Dashboard - Export</td></tr>';

            html += '<tr><td colspan="' + colCount + '" style="background-color:#e9d5ff;font-size:12px;padding:8px;text-align:center;">';
            html += '<b>Generated:</b> ' + dateStr + ' | <b>Parents:</b> ' + parentAccounts.length + ' | <b>Total (with children):</b> ' + exportData.length + '</td></tr>';

            html += '<tr><td colspan="' + colCount + '" style="height:10px;"></td></tr>';

            html += '<tr>';
            exportColumns.forEach(function (col) {
                const headerName = col.getColDef().headerName || col.getColId();
                html += '<th style="' + thStyle + '">' + headerName + '</th>';
            });
            html += '</tr>';

            exportData.forEach((a, i) => {
                let rowColor;
                if (a._isExportChild) {
                    rowColor = '#fef3c7'; // Light yellow for children
                } else {
                    rowColor = (i % 2 === 0) ? '#f3e8ff' : '#ffffff';
                }

                html += '<tr>';
                exportColumns.forEach(function (col) {
                    const field = col.getColDef().field;
                    const isNumeric = col.getColDef().type === 'numericColumn' || field === 'avg';
                    const cellValue = smFormatExportCellValue(col, a);
                    const fontWeight = field === 'code' ? ';font-weight:' + (a._isExportChild ? '400' : '700') : '';
                    const align = isNumeric ? ';text-align:right' : '';
                    html += '<td style="background-color:' + rowColor + ';padding:8px' + fontWeight + align + ';">' + cellValue + '</td>';
                });
                html += '</tr>';
            });

            html += '<tr><td colspan="' + colCount + '" style="background-color:#e9d5ff;font-weight:bold;padding:10px;text-align:center;">';
            html += 'Parent Accounts: ' + parentAccounts.length + ' | Total Records (with children): ' + exportData.length + '</td></tr>';
            html += '</table></body></html>';

            const blob = new Blob([html], {
                type: "application/vnd.ms-excel"
            });
            const link = document.createElement("a");
            const url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
            const filename = "SM_Dashboard_" + today.toISOString().split("T")[0] + ".xls";
            link.setAttribute("href", url);
            link.setAttribute("download", filename);
            link.style.visibility = "hidden";
            document.body.appendChild(link);
            link.click();
            document.body.removeChild(link);
        }

        function changeTheme(event) {
            const selectedTheme = event.target.value;
            const body = document.body;
            const wrapper = document.querySelector('.sm-dashboard-container');
            const icon = document.getElementById('themeIcon');
            const currentTheme = (wrapper || body).getAttribute('data-theme');

            // Check if we're currently in dark mode
            const isDarkMode = currentTheme === 'dark' || currentTheme === 'duralux-dark';

            // Switch to the selected theme, maintaining dark mode state if applicable
            if (selectedTheme === 'magenta') {
                if (isDarkMode) {
                    body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                    if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                    icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                } else {
                    body.removeAttribute('data-theme');
                    if (wrapper) wrapper.removeAttribute('data-theme');
                    icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                }
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_base_theme', 'magenta');
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_dark_mode', isDarkMode ? 'true' : 'false');
                } catch (e) {}
            } else if (selectedTheme === 'duralux') {
                if (isDarkMode) {
                    body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux-dark');
                    if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux-dark');
                    icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                } else {
                    body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux');
                    if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux');
                    icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                }
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_base_theme', 'duralux');
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_dark_mode', isDarkMode ? 'true' : 'false');
                } catch (e) {}
            }

            lucide.createIcons();

            setTimeout(() => {
                if (typeof renderCharts === 'function' && charts.trend) {
                    renderCharts();
                }
                if (typeof renderAMCharts === 'function' && amCharts.revenue) {
                    renderAMCharts();
                }
            }, 100);
        }

        function toggleSidebar() {
            var sb = document.getElementById('sidebar');
            var icon = document.getElementById('sidebarToggleIcon');
            if (!sb) return;
            sb.classList.toggle('collapsed');
            var collapsed = sb.classList.contains('collapsed');
            icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', collapsed ? 'chevrons-right' : 'chevrons-left');
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        }

        function toggleTheme() {
            const body = document.body;
            const wrapper = document.querySelector('.sm-dashboard-container');
            const icon = document.getElementById('themeIcon');
            const amIcon = document.getElementById('amThemeIcon');
            const currentTheme = (wrapper || body).getAttribute('data-theme');

            // Toggle between light and dark of the CURRENT base theme
            if (!currentTheme || currentTheme === 'default') {
                // Currently on Magenta light → switch to Magenta dark
                body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                if (amIcon) amIcon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_dark_mode', 'true');
                } catch (e) {}
            } else if (currentTheme === 'dark') {
                // Currently on Magenta dark → switch to Magenta light
                body.removeAttribute('data-theme');
                if (wrapper) wrapper.removeAttribute('data-theme');
                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                if (amIcon) amIcon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_dark_mode', 'false');
                } catch (e) {}
            } else if (currentTheme === 'duralux') {
                // Currently on Duralux light → switch to Duralux dark
                body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux-dark');
                if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux-dark');
                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                if (amIcon) amIcon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_dark_mode', 'true');
                } catch (e) {}
            } else if (currentTheme === 'duralux-dark') {
                // Currently on Duralux dark → switch to Duralux light
                body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux');
                if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux');
                icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                if (amIcon) amIcon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                try {
                    localStorage.setItem('sm_dark_mode', 'false');
                } catch (e) {}
            }

            lucide.createIcons();

            setTimeout(() => {
                if (typeof renderCharts === 'function' && charts.trend) {
                    renderCharts();
                }
                if (typeof renderAMCharts === 'function' && amCharts.revenue) {
                    renderAMCharts();
                }
            }, 100);
        }

        function switchColorScheme() {
            const scheme = document.getElementById('colorSchemeSelector').value;

            if (scheme === 'cyan') {
                document.body.classList.add('cyan-theme');
            } else {
                document.body.classList.remove('cyan-theme');
            }

            try {
                localStorage.setItem('sm_color_scheme', scheme);
            } catch (e) {}

            setTimeout(() => {
                if (typeof renderCharts === 'function' && charts.trend) {
                    renderCharts();
                }
                if (typeof renderAMCharts === 'function' && amCharts.revenue) {
                    renderAMCharts();
                }
            }, 100);
        }


        function switchDashboardSection(sectionId) {
            // Track page view
            if (typeof analyticsTrackPage === 'function') {
                const pageNames = {
                    'dashboard-view': 'Dashboard',
                    'pending-requests': 'Pending Requests',
                    'transfer-requests': 'Transfer Requests'
                };
                analyticsTrackPage(pageNames[sectionId] || sectionId);
            }

            // ── RESET ALL OVERLAY/FULL-PAGE VIEWS FIRST ──────────────────
            const overlayViews = [
                'reviewRequestView',
                'sdReviewTransferView',
                'transferRequestView'
            ];
            overlayViews.forEach(function(id) {
                var el = document.getElementById(id);
                if (el) el.style.display = 'none';
            });

            // Reset pending requests internal state
            CURRENT_REQUEST_ITEM = null;
            if (typeof pendingGridApi !== 'undefined' && pendingGridApi) {
                // grid stays, just reset the review state
            }

            // ── RESET section-mode on content div ────────────────────────
            var contentDiv = document.querySelector('.content');
            if (contentDiv) {
                contentDiv.classList.remove('section-mode');
                contentDiv.classList.remove('psd-full-mode');
            }
            var portalShell = document.querySelector('.portal-shell');
            if (portalShell) portalShell.classList.remove('psd-full-shell');

            // ── HIDE ALL SECTIONS ─────────────────────────────────────────
            document.querySelectorAll('.dashboard-section').forEach(function(section) {
                section.style.display = 'none';
            });

            // ── REMOVE ACTIVE FROM ALL NAV ITEMS ─────────────────────────
            document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(function(item) {
                item.classList.remove('active');
            });

            // ── SHOW TARGET SECTION ───────────────────────────────────────
            var targetSection = document.getElementById(sectionId);
            if (targetSection) {
                targetSection.style.display = 'block';
            }

            // ── SET ACTIVE NAV ITEM ───────────────────────────────────────
            var activeNav = document.querySelector('[data-section="' + sectionId + '"]');
            if (activeNav) {
                activeNav.classList.add('active');
            }

            // ── SECTION-MODE for pending/transfer ────────────────────────
            if (contentDiv) {
                if (sectionId === 'pending-requests' || sectionId === 'transfer-requests') {
                    contentDiv.classList.add('section-mode');
                }
                if (sectionId === 'psdView') {
                    contentDiv.classList.add('psd-full-mode');
                    if (portalShell) portalShell.classList.add('psd-full-shell');
                }
            }

            // ── LOAD DATA FOR SPECIFIC SECTIONS ──────────────────────────
            if (sectionId === 'pending-requests') {
                if (typeof loadAccountRequests === 'function') loadAccountRequests();
            } 
            else if (sectionId === 'transfer-requests') {
                if (typeof loadAdminTransferRequests === 'function') loadAdminTransferRequests();
            } 
           
        else if (sectionId === 'processDocsView') {
    if (typeof pdLoadDocs === 'function') pdLoadDocs();
}
else if (sectionId === 'qaView') {
    if (typeof qaInit === 'function') qaInit();
}
else if (sectionId === 'rnpsView') {
    if (typeof rnpsInit === 'function') rnpsInit();
}
else if (sectionId === 'contactUsView') {
    if (typeof cuLoadContacts === 'function') cuLoadContacts();
}
          else if (sectionId === 'seMailboxView') {
    if (typeof SEMailbox !== 'undefined') SEMailbox.init();
}
else if (sectionId === 'psdView') {
    if (typeof psdInit === 'function') psdInit();
    else {
        var psdLoading = document.getElementById('psdLoading');
        if (psdLoading) {
            psdLoading.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;color:#ef4444;font-weight:700;">PSD script failed to load. Re-upload psd-assignment.js to SharePoint and hard-refresh (Ctrl+F5).</div>';
        }
    }
}

        }

        function getVisibleDashboardSectionId() {
            var sections = document.querySelectorAll('.dashboard-section');
            for (var i = 0; i < sections.length; i++) {
                var section = sections[i];
                if (section.style.display !== 'none' && section.offsetParent !== null && section.id) {
                    return section.id;
                }
            }
            return 'dashboard-view';
        }

        window.refreshCurrentTab = function() {
            var activeNav = document.querySelector('.nav-item.active[data-section]');
            var sectionId = activeNav ? activeNav.getAttribute('data-section') : getVisibleDashboardSectionId();
            refreshTabData(sectionId || 'dashboard-view');
        };

        window.refreshTabData = async function(sectionId) {
            var btn = document.querySelector('.tab-refresh-btn[data-section="' + sectionId + '"]') || document.getElementById('headerRefreshBtn');
            if (btn) {
                btn.disabled = true;
                btn.classList.add('refreshing');
            }
            try {
                switch (sectionId) {
                    case 'dashboard-view':
                        await init();
                        break;
                    case 'pending-requests':
                        if (typeof loadAccountRequests === 'function') await loadAccountRequests();
                        break;
                    case 'transfer-requests':
                        if (typeof loadAdminTransferRequests === 'function') await loadAdminTransferRequests();
                        break;
                    case 'processDocsView':
                        if (typeof pdLoadDocs === 'function') pdLoadDocs();
                        break;
                    case 'qaView':
                        if (typeof qaInit === 'function') qaInit();
                        break;
                    case 'rnpsView':
                        if (typeof rnpsInit === 'function') rnpsInit();
                        break;
                    case 'contactUsView':
                        if (typeof cuLoadContacts === 'function') cuLoadContacts();
                        break;
                    case 'suggestionsView':
                        if (typeof sgLoadSuggestions === 'function') sgLoadSuggestions();
                        break;
                    case 'seMailboxView':
                        if (typeof SEMailbox !== 'undefined' && SEMailbox.init) SEMailbox.init();
                        break;
                    case 'psdView':
                        if (typeof psdInit === 'function') psdInit();
                        break;
                    case 'customerServiceView':
                        if (typeof csFetchSharePointData === 'function') {
                            var csLoading = document.getElementById('csLoadingScreen');
                            var csMain = document.getElementById('csMainContent');
                            if (csLoading) csLoading.style.display = 'block';
                            if (csMain) csMain.style.display = 'none';
                            await csFetchSharePointData();
                        }
                        break;
                    default:
                        await init();
                        break;
                }
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Tab refresh failed:', err);
                alert('Refresh failed: ' + err.message);
            } finally {
                if (btn) {
                    btn.disabled = false;
                    btn.classList.remove('refreshing');
                }
            }
        };

        // Load user access first, then initialize
        // ===== MAIN INITIALIZATION =====
        function initAll() {
            injectAGGridThemeStyles();
            initLandingPage();

            loadUserAccess(function(hasAccess) {
                populateLandingPage();
                try {
                    const savedBaseTheme = localStorage.getItem('sm_base_theme') || 'magenta'; // ✅ DEFAULT TO MAGENTA
                    const savedDarkMode = localStorage.getItem('sm_dark_mode') === 'true'; // ✅ DEFAULT TO LIGHT (false)
                    const selector = document.getElementById('colorSchemeSelector');
                    const icon = document.getElementById('themeIcon');
                    const wrapper = document.querySelector('.sm-dashboard-container');

                    // Set the dropdown to the saved base theme
                    if (selector) {
                        selector.value = savedBaseTheme;
                    }

                    // Apply the appropriate theme based on base theme + dark mode
                    if (savedBaseTheme === 'duralux') {
                        if (savedDarkMode) {
                            document.body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux-dark');
                            if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux-dark');
                            if (icon) icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                        } else {
                            document.body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux');
                            if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'duralux');
                            if (icon) icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                        }
                    } else {
                        // Magenta theme
                        if (savedDarkMode) {
                            document.body.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                            if (wrapper) wrapper.setAttribute('data-theme', 'dark');
                            if (icon) icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                        } else {
                            document.body.removeAttribute('data-theme');
                            if (wrapper) wrapper.removeAttribute('data-theme');
                            if (icon) icon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                        }
                    }
                } catch (e) {}

                // Initialize Lucide icons
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                    lucide.createIcons();
                }
                // Show revenue toggle only to authorised users
                const userEmail = (USER_CONTEXT.userEmail || '').toLowerCase();
                if (userEmail === 'ubaid.mir@du.ae' || userEmail === 'tehleel.lone@du.ae') {
                    const btn = document.getElementById('revenueToggleBtn');
                    if (btn) btn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
                }
                // ✅ ALWAYS show landing page for ALL users (even without access)
                console.log('[INFO] User:', USER_CONTEXT.userName, '| Role:', USER_CONTEXT.role);

                // Show landing page ALWAYS
                document.getElementById('landingPage').style.display = 'grid';

                // Load dashboard data ONLY if user has access
              if (hasAccess) {
    console.log('[✓] Access granted - Loading dashboard data');

    if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Admin' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Read Only' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'TSM Manager' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Auditor' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'TSM_SE_Viewer') {
        init();
    } else if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Account Manager' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Account Director') {
        initAMView();
    } else if (isPsdRole(USER_CONTEXT.role)) {
        initPsdShell();
    }
    // TSM_SE data loader
    if (typeof tsmSeInit === 'function') tsmSeInit();
                } else {
                    console.log('[!] No dashboard access - Account Search only');
                }
            });
        }
        // Start the app
        if (document.readyState === 'complete') {
            initAll();
        } else {
            window.addEventListener('load', initAll);
        }
// ===== OWNER: VIEW AS USER =====
async function ownerFetchUserRole(email) {
            // Step 1: Check Access_Control list
            const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_ACCESS_LIST + "')/items?" +
                "$select=UserEmailID,Role&" +
                "$filter=UserEmailID eq '" + email + "'&$top=1";
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });
            if (res.ok) {
                const data = await res.json();
                const results = data.d.results;
                if (results.length > 0) return { role: results[0].Role, name: null };
            }

            // Step 2: Get their display name from the main SP list directly
            // Search by email in Line_Manager or Service_Manager expanded fields
            const spListUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                "$select=Line_x0020_Manager/Title,Line_x0020_Manager/EMail," +
                "Service_x0020_Manager/Title,Service_x0020_Manager/EMail&" +
                "$expand=Line_x0020_Manager,Service_x0020_Manager&" +
                "$filter=(Line_x0020_Manager/EMail eq '" + email + "') or " +
                "(Service_x0020_Manager/EMail eq '" + email + "')&$top=1";

            const spRes = await fetch(spListUrl, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });

            if (spRes.ok) {
                const spData = await spRes.json();
                const spResults = spData.d.results;
                if (spResults.length > 0) {
                    const item = spResults[0];
                    if (item.Line_x0020_Manager && 
                        item.Line_x0020_Manager.EMail && 
                        item.Line_x0020_Manager.EMail.toLowerCase() === email) {
                        return { role: 'Line Manager', name: item.Line_x0020_Manager.Title };
                    }
                    if (item.Service_x0020_Manager && 
                        item.Service_x0020_Manager.EMail && 
                        item.Service_x0020_Manager.EMail.toLowerCase() === email) {
                        return { role: 'Service Manager', name: item.Service_x0020_Manager.Title };
                    }
                }
            }

            return null;
        }        async function ownerFetchUserName(email) {
            const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/siteusers?$filter=Email eq '" + email + "'&$select=Title,Email&$top=1";
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });
            if (!res.ok) return null;
            const data = await res.json();
            const results = data.d.results;
            if (results.length > 0) return results[0].Title;
            return null;
        }

        window.ownerSwitchView = async function() {
            const email = document.getElementById('ownerViewAsEmail').value.trim().toLowerCase();
            const msgEl = document.getElementById('ownerViewAsMsg');

            if (!email) {
                msgEl.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#ef4444;">Please enter an email.</span>';
                return;
            }

            msgEl.innerHTML = '<span style="color:var(--t3);">Checking access...</span>';

          const result = await ownerFetchUserRole(email);
            if (!result) {
                msgEl.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#ef4444;">No access found for this email.</span>';
                return;
            }

            const role = result.role;
            let displayName = result.name;

            // If name not returned (Admin/AM/AD roles), fetch from siteusers
            if (!displayName) {
                displayName = await ownerFetchUserName(email);
            }
            if (!displayName) displayName = email.split('@')[0];
            msgEl.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#10b981;">Found: ' + role + ' — loading view...</span>';

            msgEl.innerHTML = '<span style="color:#10b981;">Found: ' + role + ' — loading view...</span>';

            USER_CONTEXT.userEmail    = email;
            USER_CONTEXT.userName     = displayName;
            USER_CONTEXT.role         = role;
            USER_CONTEXT.isActive     = true;
            USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin      = role === 'Admin';
            USER_CONTEXT.isAM         = role === 'Account Manager';
            USER_CONTEXT.isAD         = role === 'Account Director';
            USER_CONTEXT.isLM         = role === 'Line Manager';
            USER_CONTEXT.isSM         = role === 'Service Manager';
            USER_CONTEXT.isReadOnly   = role === 'Read Only';
            USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager = role === 'TSM Manager';
            window.USER_CONTEXT       = USER_CONTEXT;

            document.getElementById('ownerViewAsPanel').style.display = 'none';

            setTimeout(async function() {
                if (role === 'Account Manager' || role === 'Account Director') {
                    showAMDashboard();
                } else {
                    if (role === 'Line Manager') {
                        window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.lm === displayName);
                        filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
                    } else if (role === 'Service Manager') {
                        window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.sm === displayName);
                        filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
                    } else if (role === 'TSM Manager') {
                        window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.filter(a => a.team === 'TSM_ME' || a.team === 'TSM_SE');
                        filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
                   } else {
                        window.ALL_FILTERED = ALL_DATA.slice();
                        filtered = window.ALL_FILTERED.filter(a => a.type === 'Group');
                    }

                    populateLandingPage();
                    showDashboard();
                    populateFilters({ preserve: false });
                    updateServiceManagerFilter();
                    applyFilters();

                    // Reset all nav items first
                    ['portalAnalyticsNavItem','transferRequestsNavItem','pendingRequestsNavItem',
                     'intelligenceNavLabel','executiveHubNavItem','qaNavItem','rnpsNavItem',
                     'projectMgmtNavItem'].forEach(function(id) {
                        var el = document.getElementById(id);
                        if (el) el.style.display = 'none';
                    });

                    // Show nav items for the impersonated role
                    if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) {
                        ['portalAnalyticsNavItem','transferRequestsNavItem','pendingRequestsNavItem',
                         'executiveHubNavItem','qaNavItem','projectMgmtNavItem'].forEach(function(id) {
                            var el = document.getElementById(id);
                            if (el) el.style.display = 'flex';
                        });
                        var lbl = document.getElementById('intelligenceNavLabel');
                        if (lbl) lbl.style.display = 'block';
                    }

                    if (USER_CONTEXT.isTSMManager) {
                        var ehNav = document.getElementById('executiveHubNavItem');
                        if (ehNav) ehNav.style.display = 'flex';
                        var qaNav = document.getElementById('qaNavItem');
                        if (qaNav) qaNav.style.display = 'flex';
                    }

                    if (USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Line Manager' || USER_CONTEXT.role === 'Service Manager') {
                        var qaNavLmSm = document.getElementById('qaNavItem');
                        if (qaNavLmSm) qaNavLmSm.style.display = 'flex';
                    }

                    var rnpsNav = document.getElementById('rnpsNavItem');
                    if (rnpsNav) rnpsNav.style.display = 'flex';

                    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
                }
            }, 300);
        };

        let CURRENT_REQUEST_ITEM = null;

            'Oct_x002d_26': 'Oct-26', 'Nov_x002d_26': 'Nov-26', 'Dec_x002d_26': 'Dec-26'
        };

        function smHistoryFmtDate(iso) {
            if (!iso) return 'N/A';
            const d = new Date(iso);
            if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(iso);
            return d.toLocaleString('en-GB', {
                day: '2-digit', month: 'short', year: 'numeric',
                hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit'
            });
        }

        function smHistoryNorm(val) {
            if (val === null || val === undefined) return '';
            return String(val).replace(/\u00a0/g, ' ').trim();
        }

        function smCleanSpValue(val) {
            val = smHistoryNorm(val);
            if (val.indexOf(';#') >= 0) val = val.split(';#').pop();
            return val;
        }

        function smParseVersionFields(data) {
            if (!data || !data.d) return {};
            var d = data.d;
            if (d.FieldValuesAsText && typeof d.FieldValuesAsText === 'object' && !d.FieldValuesAsText.__deferred) {
                return d.FieldValuesAsText;
            }
            var copy = Object.assign({}, d);
            delete copy.__metadata;
            if (copy.FieldValuesAsText && copy.FieldValuesAsText.__deferred) delete copy.FieldValuesAsText;
            return copy;
        }

        function smEditorFromFields(fields) {
            return smCleanSpValue(fields.Editor || fields['Modified By'] || fields.Author || '');
        }

        async function smFetchListItemId(accountCode) {
            const safeCode = String(accountCode || '').replace(/'/g, "''");
            const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                "$select=ID&$filter=Title eq '" + safeCode + "'&$top=1";
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Could not find list item');
            const data = await res.json();
            if (!data.d.results.length) throw new Error('Account not found in SharePoint list');
            return data.d.results[0].ID;
        }

        async function smFetchItemVersions(itemId) {
            const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items(" + itemId + ")/versions";
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load version history (' + res.status + ')');
            const data = await res.json();
            var versions = data.d.results || [];
            versions.sort(function (a, b) { return new Date(b.Created) - new Date(a.Created); });
            return versions;
        }

        async function smFetchVersionsPageHtml(itemId) {
            const listGuid = await smGetListGuid();
            const url = SP_URL + '/_layouts/15/Versions.aspx?list=' + encodeURIComponent(listGuid) + '&ID=' + itemId;
            const res = await fetch(url, { credentials: 'include' });
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load version history page (' + res.status + ')');
            return res.text();
        }

        function smHistoryFieldLabel(raw) {
            var key = String(raw || '').trim();
            if (!key) return key;
            if (SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key]) return SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key];
            if (SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP[key]) return SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP[key];
            return key.replace(/_x0020_/g, ' ').replace(/_x002d_/g, '-').replace(/_/g, ' ').trim();
        }

        var SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP = {};
        Object.keys(SM_HISTORY_FIELDS).forEach(function (k) {
            SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP[SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[k]] = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[k];
            SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP[k] = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[k];
        });
        ['Service_Required', 'Parent Code', 'Parent_x0020_Code', 'Customer Name'].forEach(function (k) {
            if (!SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP[k]) SM_HISTORY_LABEL_LOOKUP[k] = smHistoryFieldLabel(k);
        });

        function smLooksLikeDate(text) {
            return /^\d{1,2}\/\d{1,2}\/\d{4}/.test(String(text || '').trim()) ||
                /^\d{1,2}\s+[A-Za-z]{3}\s+\d{4}/.test(String(text || '').trim());
        }

        function smStripHtml(html) {
            var tmp = document.createElement('div');
            tmp.innerHTML = html || '';
            return (tmp.textContent || tmp.innerText || '').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
        }

        function smCellTextNoNestedTables(cell) {
            if (!cell) return '';
            var clone = cell.cloneNode(true);
            clone.querySelectorAll('table').forEach(function (t) { t.remove(); });
            return smStripHtml(clone.innerHTML);
        }

        function smParseVersionsPageHtml(html) {
            const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
            const entries = [];
            const versionTable = doc.querySelector('table.ms-settingsframe') ||
                doc.querySelector('table[id*="versions"]') ||
                doc.querySelector('table.ms-formtable');

            if (!versionTable) {
                console.warn('[smParseVersionsPageHtml] ms-settingsframe not found, using fallback scan');
                return smParseVersionsPageHtmlFallback(doc);
            }

            const rows = versionTable.querySelectorAll('tbody > tr, tr');
            var dataStart = 0;
            for (var h = 0; h < Math.min(rows.length, 6); h++) {
                var ht = (rows[h].textContent || '').toLowerCase();
                if (ht.indexOf('modified') >= 0 && ht.indexOf('no') >= 0) {
                    dataStart = h + 1;
                    break;
                }
            }

            var current = null;
            for (let i = dataStart; i < rows.length; i++) {
                const row = rows[i];
                const cells = row.querySelectorAll(':scope > td');
                if (!cells.length) continue;

                const versionRaw = smStripHtml(cells[0].innerHTML).replace(/\s*View\s*$/i, '').trim();
                const verMatch = versionRaw.match(/^(\d+\.\d+)/);

                if (verMatch && cells.length >= 2) {
                    if (current) entries.push(current);
                    let modified = '';
                    let editor = '';
                    const dateEl = row.querySelector('table[ctxname="ctxVer"] a, table[ctxname="ctxVer"] td, .ms-vb-time');
                    if (dateEl) modified = smStripHtml(dateEl.innerHTML);
                    const userEl = row.querySelector('.ms-imnSpan a:nth-child(2), .ms-imnSpan a, .ms-subtleLink');
                    if (userEl) editor = smStripHtml(userEl.innerHTML);
                    if (!modified && cells[1]) modified = smCellTextNoNestedTables(cells[1]);
                    if (!editor && cells[2]) editor = smCellTextNoNestedTables(cells[2]);

                    current = {
                        versionLabel: verMatch[1],
                        versionNo: smExtractVersionNoFromRow(row) || smVersionLabelToNo(verMatch[1]),
                        viewUrl: smExtractVersionViewUrl(row),
                        created: modified,
                        editor: editor,
                        changes: []
                    };
                    smCollectVersionChanges(row, current.changes, {});
                    continue;
                }

                if (current) {
                    smCollectVersionChanges(row, current.changes, {});
                }
            }
            if (current) entries.push(current);

            entries.sort(function (a, b) {
                return parseFloat(b.versionLabel) - parseFloat(a.versionLabel);
            });
            entries.forEach(function (e, idx) { e.isCurrent = idx === 0; });
            return entries;
        }

        function smVersionLabelToNo(label) {
            return Math.round(parseFloat(String(label)) * 512);
        }

        function smExtractVersionNoFromRow(verRow) {
            if (!verRow) return null;
            const html = verRow.innerHTML || '';
            var m = html.match(/VersionNo=(\d+)/i);
            if (m) return parseInt(m[1], 10);
            m = html.match(/VersionNo['"%3D\s:=]+(\d{3,6})/i);
            if (m) return parseInt(m[1], 10);
            return null;
        }

        function smResolveSpUrl(href) {
            if (!href) return null;
            if (href.indexOf('http') === 0) return href;
            try {
                return new URL(href, SP_URL + '/').href;
            } catch (e) {
                return SP_URL + (href.charAt(0) === '/' ? href : '/' + href);
            }
        }

        function smExtractVersionViewUrl(verRow) {
            if (!verRow) return null;
            var links = verRow.querySelectorAll('a[href]');
            for (var i = 0; i < links.length; i++) {
                var href = links[i].getAttribute('href') || '';
                if (/VersionNo=|listform\.aspx|DispForm\.aspx|displayifs\.aspx/i.test(href)) {
                    return smResolveSpUrl(href);
                }
            }
            return null;
        }

        function smCollectVersionChanges(root, changes, seen) {
            if (!root) return;
            seen = seen || {};

            root.querySelectorAll('tr[id^="SPField"]').forEach(function (tr) {
                if (tr.closest('table[ctxname="ctxVer"]')) return;
                var rowId = tr.getAttribute('id') || '';
                var idMatch = rowId.match(/SPField(?:\w+?)_(.+)$/i);
                var label = idMatch ? smHistoryFieldLabel(idMatch[1]) : '';
                var body = tr.querySelector('.ms-formbody');
                var tds = tr.querySelectorAll('td');
                var newVal = '';
                if (body) newVal = smStripHtml(body.innerHTML);
                else if (tds.length >= 2) newVal = smStripHtml(tds[tds.length - 1].innerHTML);
                else if (tds.length === 1) newVal = smStripHtml(tds[0].innerHTML);
                if (!label && tds.length >= 1) label = smHistoryFieldLabel(smStripHtml(tds[0].innerHTML));
                if (!label || smLooksLikeDate(label) || seen[label]) return;
                seen[label] = true;
                changes.push({ label: label, oldVal: '—', newVal: newVal || '—' });
            });

            root.querySelectorAll('.ms-formlabel').forEach(function (lab) {
                var tr = lab.closest('tr');
                if (!tr || tr.closest('table[ctxname="ctxVer"]')) return;
                var body = tr.querySelector('.ms-formbody');
                if (!body) return;
                var label = smHistoryFieldLabel(smStripHtml(lab.innerHTML));
                var newVal = smStripHtml(body.innerHTML);
                if (!label || smLooksLikeDate(label) || seen[label]) return;
                seen[label] = true;
                changes.push({ label: label, oldVal: '—', newVal: newVal || '—' });
            });

            root.querySelectorAll('tr').forEach(function (tr) {
                if (tr.id && tr.id.indexOf('SPField') === 0) return;
                if (tr.closest('table[ctxname="ctxVer"]')) return;
                var tds = tr.querySelectorAll(':scope > td');
                if (tds.length < 2) return;
                var label = smHistoryFieldLabel(smStripHtml(tds[0].innerHTML));
                var newVal = smStripHtml(tds[1].innerHTML);
                if (!label || smLooksLikeDate(label) || /^no\.?$/i.test(label) || /^modified/i.test(label)) return;
                if (seen[label]) return;
                seen[label] = true;
                changes.push({ label: label, oldVal: '—', newVal: newVal || '—' });
            });

            root.querySelectorAll('td[colspan]').forEach(function (td) {
                if (td.querySelector('table')) {
                    td.querySelectorAll('table tr').forEach(function (tr) {
                        var tds = tr.querySelectorAll('td');
                        if (tds.length >= 2) {
                            var label = smHistoryFieldLabel(smStripHtml(tds[0].innerHTML));
                            var newVal = smStripHtml(tds[1].innerHTML);
                            if (label && !smLooksLikeDate(label) && !seen[label]) {
                                seen[label] = true;
                                changes.push({ label: label, oldVal: '—', newVal: newVal || '—' });
                            }
                        }
                    });
                } else {
                    smParsePlainVersionChangeText(smStripHtml(td.innerHTML), changes, seen);
                }
            });

            if (!changes.length && root.innerHTML) {
                smParseChangesFromRawFragment(root.innerHTML, changes, seen);
            }
        }

        function smParseChangesFromRawFragment(html, changes, seen) {
            seen = seen || {};
            Object.keys(SM_HISTORY_FIELDS).forEach(function (key) {
                var label = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key];
                if (seen[label]) return;
                var re = new RegExp('SPField\\w+_' + key.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g, '\\$&') + '[\\s\\S]{0,400}?ms-formbody[^>]*>([\\s\\S]*?)<', 'i');
                var m = html.match(re);
                if (m) {
                    seen[label] = true;
                    changes.push({ label: label, oldVal: '—', newVal: smStripHtml(m[1]) || '—' });
                }
            });
            var monthRe = /(Jan|Feb|Mar|Apr|May|Jun|Jul|Aug|Sep|Oct|Nov|Dec)-(\d{2})[\s\S]{0,160}?([\d,\.]+)/gi;
            var mm;
            while ((mm = monthRe.exec(html)) !== null) {
                var mLabel = mm[1] + '-' + mm[2];
                if (!seen[mLabel]) {
                    seen[mLabel] = true;
                    changes.push({ label: mLabel, oldVal: '—', newVal: mm[3].trim() });
                }
            }
        }

        function smParsePlainVersionChangeText(text, changes, seen) {
            if (!text) return;
            seen = seen || {};
            Object.keys(SM_HISTORY_FIELDS).forEach(function (key) {
                if (text.indexOf(key) === 0) {
                    var label = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key];
                    if (seen[label]) return;
                    seen[label] = true;
                    changes.push({
                        label: label,
                        oldVal: '—',
                        newVal: text.slice(key.length).trim() || '—'
                    });
                }
            });
            var monthMatch = text.match(/^(Jan|Feb|Mar|Apr|May|Jun|Jul|Aug|Sep|Oct|Nov|Dec)-\d{2}\s+(.+)$/i);
            if (monthMatch && !seen[monthMatch[0].split(/\s/)[0]]) {
                var mLabel = monthMatch[0].split(/\s/)[0];
                seen[mLabel] = true;
                changes.push({ label: mLabel, oldVal: '—', newVal: monthMatch[2].trim() });
            }
        }

        function smParseDispFormFields(html) {
            const doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(html, 'text/html');
            const fields = {};
            function addField(key, val) {
                if (!key) return;
                val = smCleanSpValue(val);
                if (val) fields[key] = val;
            }
            doc.querySelectorAll('tr[id^="SPField"], [id^="SPField"]').forEach(function (el) {
                var idMatch = (el.getAttribute('id') || '').match(/SPField(?:\w+?)_(.+)$/i);
                if (!idMatch) return;
                var key = idMatch[1];
                var body = el.querySelector('.ms-formbody');
                if (body) { addField(key, smStripHtml(body.innerHTML)); return; }
                var tds = el.querySelectorAll('td');
                if (tds.length >= 2) addField(key, smStripHtml(tds[tds.length - 1].innerHTML));
                else addField(key, smStripHtml(el.innerHTML));
            });
            doc.querySelectorAll('.ms-formlabel').forEach(function (lab) {
                var tr = lab.closest('tr');
                if (!tr) return;
                var body = tr.querySelector('.ms-formbody');
                if (!body) return;
                var labelText = smStripHtml(lab.innerHTML);
                Object.keys(SM_HISTORY_FIELDS).forEach(function (key) {
                    if (SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key] === labelText || key === labelText) {
                        addField(key, smStripHtml(body.innerHTML));
                    }
                });
            });
            return fields;
        }

        function smDecodeSoapInnerXml(text) {
            if (!text) return '';
            return String(text)
                .replace(/&lt;/g, '<').replace(/&gt;/g, '>')
                .replace(/&amp;/g, '&').replace(/&quot;/g, '"')
                .replace(/<!\[CDATA\[([\s\S]*?)\]\]>/g, '$1');
        }

        function smParseSoapVersionCollection(xmlText, fieldName) {
            const versions = [];
            var innerMatch = xmlText.match(/<GetVersionCollectionResult[^>]*>([\s\S]*?)<\/GetVersionCollectionResult>/i);
            if (!innerMatch) return versions;
            var inner = smDecodeSoapInnerXml(innerMatch[1].trim());
            if (!inner) return versions;

            var doc;
            try {
                doc = new DOMParser().parseFromString(inner, 'text/xml');
            } catch (e) {
                return versions;
            }
            if (doc.querySelector('parsererror')) return versions;

            doc.querySelectorAll('Version').forEach(function (v) {
                var label = v.getAttribute('Version') || v.getAttribute('VersionLabel') || v.getAttribute('version') || '';
                if (!label || !/\d/.test(label)) {
                    var verId = parseInt(v.getAttribute('VersionId') || v.getAttribute('versionid') || '0', 10);
                    if (verId) label = (verId / 512).toFixed(1);
                }
                var fieldEl = v.querySelector('Field[Name="' + fieldName + '"]') ||
                    v.querySelector('Field[name="' + fieldName + '"]') ||
                    v.querySelector('Field');
                var val = '';
                if (fieldEl) {
                    val = fieldEl.getAttribute('Value') || fieldEl.getAttribute('value') || smStripHtml(fieldEl.textContent);
                }
                if (label && /\d/.test(String(label))) {
                    versions.push({
                        versionLabel: String(label).replace(',', '.').trim(),
                        value: val,
                        fieldName: fieldName
                    });
                }
            });
            return versions;
        }

        function smFormatListGuid(guid) {
            if (!guid) return guid;
            var g = String(guid).trim();
            if (g.charAt(0) !== '{') g = '{' + g;
            if (g.charAt(g.length - 1) !== '}') g = g + '}';
            return g;
        }

        async function smSoapGetVersionCollection(listGuid, itemId, fieldName) {
            const envelope = '<?xml version="1.0" encoding="utf-8"?>' +
                '<soap:Envelope xmlns:xsi="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema-instance" xmlns:xsd="http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema" xmlns:soap="http://schemas.xmlsoap.org/soap/envelope/">' +
                '<soap:Body><GetVersionCollection xmlns="http://schemas.microsoft.com/sharepoint/soap/">' +
                '<strlistID>' + smFormatListGuid(listGuid) + '</strlistID>' +
                '<strlistItemID>' + itemId + '</strlistItemID>' +
                '<strFieldName>' + fieldName.replace(/&/g, '&amp;').replace(/</g, '&lt;') + '</strFieldName>' +
                '</GetVersionCollection></soap:Body></soap:Envelope>';

            const res = await fetch(SP_URL + '/_vti_bin/lists.asmx', {
                method: 'POST',
                credentials: 'include',
                headers: {
                    'Content-Type': 'text/xml; charset=utf-8',
                    'SOAPAction': 'http://schemas.microsoft.com/sharepoint/soap/GetVersionCollection'
                },
                body: envelope
            });
            if (!res.ok) return [];
            const text = await res.text();
            return smParseSoapVersionCollection(text, fieldName);
        }

        function smSoapValueAtVersion(hist, versionLabel) {
            if (!hist || !hist.length) return '';
            var target = parseFloat(versionLabel);
            for (var i = 0; i < hist.length; i++) {
                if (parseFloat(hist[i].versionLabel) === target) {
                    return smCleanSpValue(hist[i].value);
                }
            }
            return '';
        }

        function smResolveFieldValueAtVersion(fieldHistories, fieldKey, versionLabel, allLabels) {
            var exact = smSoapValueAtVersion(fieldHistories[fieldKey], versionLabel);
            if (exact) return exact;
            var target = parseFloat(versionLabel);
            var labels = allLabels.slice().sort(function (a, b) { return parseFloat(b) - parseFloat(a); });
            for (var i = 0; i < labels.length; i++) {
                if (parseFloat(labels[i]) > target) continue;
                var val = smSoapValueAtVersion(fieldHistories[fieldKey], labels[i]);
                if (val) return val;
            }
            return '';
        }

        function smChangesFromSoapHistories(fieldHistories, versionLabel, olderVersionLabel, allLabels) {
            const changes = [];
            const seen = {};
            Object.keys(fieldHistories).forEach(function (fieldKey) {
                var newerVal = smResolveFieldValueAtVersion(fieldHistories, fieldKey, versionLabel, allLabels);
                if (!olderVersionLabel) {
                    if (newerVal) {
                        var lbl = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[fieldKey] || smHistoryFieldLabel(fieldKey);
                        if (!seen[lbl]) {
                            seen[lbl] = true;
                            changes.push({ label: lbl, oldVal: '—', newVal: newerVal });
                        }
                    }
                    return;
                }
                var olderVal = smResolveFieldValueAtVersion(fieldHistories, fieldKey, olderVersionLabel, allLabels);
                if (newerVal !== olderVal) {
                    var label = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[fieldKey] || smHistoryFieldLabel(fieldKey);
                    if (!seen[label]) {
                        seen[label] = true;
                        changes.push({
                            label: label,
                            oldVal: olderVal || '—',
                            newVal: newerVal || '—'
                        });
                    }
                }
            });
            return changes;
        }

        async function smBuildHistoryChangesViaSoap(itemId, entries) {
            const listGuid = await smGetListGuid();
            const fieldKeys = Object.keys(SM_HISTORY_FIELDS);
            const fieldHistories = {};
            const allLabels = entries.map(function (e) { return e.versionLabel; });

            await Promise.all(fieldKeys.map(async function (fieldKey) {
                try {
                    const hist = await smSoapGetVersionCollection(listGuid, itemId, fieldKey);
                    if (hist.length) fieldHistories[fieldKey] = hist;
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn('[smSoapGetVersionCollection]', fieldKey, e);
                }
            }));

            if (!Object.keys(fieldHistories).length) {
                console.warn('[smBuildHistoryChangesViaSoap] No field histories returned from lists.asmx');
                return null;
            }
            console.log('[smBuildHistoryChangesViaSoap] Loaded', Object.keys(fieldHistories).length, 'field histories via SOAP');

            return entries.map(function (e, idx) {
                var olderLabel = idx < entries.length - 1 ? entries[idx + 1].versionLabel : null;
                var soapChanges = smChangesFromSoapHistories(fieldHistories, e.versionLabel, olderLabel, allLabels);
                var changes = soapChanges.length ? soapChanges : (e.changes || []);
                return Object.assign({}, e, { changes: changes });
            });
        }

        async function smFetchItemFieldsAtVersion(itemId, listGuid, versionNo, viewUrl) {
            const urls = [];
            if (viewUrl) urls.push(viewUrl);
            urls.push(
                SP_URL + '/_layouts/15/listform.aspx?PageType=3&ListId=' + encodeURIComponent(listGuid) +
                    '&ID=' + itemId + '&VersionNo=' + versionNo,
                SP_URL + '/Lists/' + encodeURIComponent(SP_LIST) + '/DispForm.aspx?ID=' + itemId + '&VersionNo=' + versionNo
            );
            for (var u = 0; u < urls.length; u++) {
                try {
                    const res = await fetch(urls[u], { credentials: 'include' });
                    if (!res.ok) continue;
                    const html = await res.text();
                    const fields = smParseDispFormFields(html);
                    if (Object.keys(fields).length) return fields;
                } catch (e) {
                    console.warn('[smFetchItemFieldsAtVersion]', urls[u], e);
                }
            }
            return {};
        }

        function smInitialVersionChanges(fields) {
            const changes = [];
            const seen = {};
            Object.keys(fields || {}).forEach(function (key) {
                if (!key || key.indexOf('__') === 0) return;
                const val = smCleanSpValue(fields[key]);
                if (!val) return;
                const label = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key] || smHistoryFieldLabel(key);
                if (seen[label]) return;
                seen[label] = true;
                changes.push({ label: label, oldVal: '—', newVal: val });
            });
            return changes;
        }

        async function smEnrichVersionEntriesByCompare(itemId, entries) {
            var soapEntries = await smBuildHistoryChangesViaSoap(itemId, entries);
            if (soapEntries && soapEntries.some(function (e) { return e.changes && e.changes.length; })) {
                return soapEntries;
            }

            const listGuid = await smGetListGuid();
            const snapshots = [];
            for (var i = 0; i < entries.length; i++) {
                var e = entries[i];
                var versionNo = e.versionNo || smVersionLabelToNo(e.versionLabel);
                snapshots.push(await smFetchItemFieldsAtVersion(itemId, listGuid, versionNo, e.viewUrl));
            }

            var hasSnapshotData = snapshots.some(function (s) { return Object.keys(s).length > 0; });
            if (!hasSnapshotData && soapEntries) return soapEntries;

            return entries.map(function (e, idx) {
                if (e.changes && e.changes.length) return e;
                var newer = snapshots[idx] || {};
                var older = idx < snapshots.length - 1 ? snapshots[idx + 1] : null;
                var changes = older ? smCompareVersionFields(newer, older) : smInitialVersionChanges(newer);
                return Object.assign({}, e, { changes: changes });
            });
        }

        function smParseVersionPropertiesRow(propsRow, changes) {
            smCollectVersionChanges(propsRow, changes, {});
        }

        function smParseVersionsPageHtmlFallback(doc) {
            const entries = [];
            const rows = doc.querySelectorAll('tr');
            for (let i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
                const row = rows[i];
                const cells = row.querySelectorAll(':scope > td');
                if (cells.length < 3) continue;
                const firstText = smStripHtml(cells[0].innerHTML).replace(/\s*View\s*$/i, '').trim();
                const verMatch = firstText.match(/^(\d+\.\d+)/);
                if (!verMatch || /^no\.?$/i.test(firstText)) continue;

                const changes = [];
                const nextRow = rows[i + 1];
                if (nextRow) {
                    smParseVersionPropertiesRow(nextRow, changes);
                    i++;
                }
                entries.push({
                    versionLabel: verMatch[1],
                    created: smStripHtml(cells[1].innerHTML),
                    editor: smStripHtml(cells[2].innerHTML),
                    changes: changes
                });
            }
            entries.sort(function (a, b) { return parseFloat(b.versionLabel) - parseFloat(a.versionLabel); });
            entries.forEach(function (e, idx) { e.isCurrent = idx === 0; });
            return entries;
        }

        async function smBuildItemHistoryFromVersionsPage(itemId) {
            const html = await smFetchVersionsPageHtml(itemId);
            let entries = smParseVersionsPageHtml(html);
            if (!entries.length) throw new Error('No version history found');
            entries = await smEnrichVersionEntriesByCompare(itemId, entries);
            return entries;
        }

        async function smFetchVersionFields(itemId, versionId) {
            const textUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items(" + itemId + ")/versions(" + versionId + ")/FieldValuesAsText";
            try {
                const res = await fetch(textUrl, {
                    headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });
                if (res.ok) {
                    const data = await res.json();
                    const parsed = smParseVersionFields(data);
                    if (parsed && Object.keys(parsed).length) return parsed;
                }
            } catch (e) {
                console.warn('[smFetchVersionFields] FieldValuesAsText failed', e);
            }

            const rawUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items(" + itemId + ")/versions(" + versionId + ")";
            const rawRes = await fetch(rawUrl, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });
            if (!rawRes.ok) return {};
            const rawData = await rawRes.json();
            return smParseVersionFields(rawData);
        }

        function smGetHistoryFieldVal(fields, internalKey) {
            if (!fields) return '';
            if (fields[internalKey] !== undefined && fields[internalKey] !== null) return fields[internalKey];
            var label = SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[internalKey];
            if (label && fields[label] !== undefined && fields[label] !== null) return fields[label];
            return '';
        }

        function smCompareVersionFields(newerFields, olderFields) {
            const changes = [];
            const checked = {};
            function pushChange(key) {
                if (checked[key] || !key || key.indexOf('__') === 0) return;
                checked[key] = true;
                const oldVal = smCleanSpValue((olderFields || {})[key]);
                const newVal = smCleanSpValue((newerFields || {})[key]);
                if (oldVal === newVal) return;
                changes.push({
                    label: SM_HISTORY_FIELDS[key] || smHistoryFieldLabel(key),
                    oldVal: oldVal || '—',
                    newVal: newVal || '—'
                });
            }
            Object.keys(SM_HISTORY_FIELDS).forEach(pushChange);
            Object.keys(newerFields || {}).forEach(pushChange);
            Object.keys(olderFields || {}).forEach(pushChange);
            return changes;
        }

        function smHistoryVersionLabel(version) {
            if (!version) return '';
            if (version.VersionLabel) return version.VersionLabel;
            if (version.VersionId) return (version.VersionId / 512).toFixed(1);
            return String(version.ID || '');
        }

        function smRenderItemHistoryTimeline(entries, container) {
            if (!entries.length) {
                container.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:48px 20px;color:var(--t3);">' +
                    '<i data-lucide="inbox" style="width:40px;height:40px;display:block;margin:0 auto 12px;"></i>' +
                    '<div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:700;">No version history</div>' +
                    '<div style="font-size:13px;margin-top:6px;">This item has not been modified since creation.</div></div>';
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
                return;
            }

            let html = '<div class="sm-history-timeline">';

            entries.forEach(function (entry, idx) {
                const hasChanges = entry.changes && entry.changes.length > 0;
                const versionText = entry.versionLabel || entry.versionId || ('v' + (idx + 1));
                html += '<div class="sm-history-card">';
                html += '<div class="sm-history-card-head">';
                html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;flex-wrap:wrap;">';
                html += '<span class="sm-history-version-badge">' + versionText + '</span>';
                html += '<div><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--t1);">' +
                    (entry.isCurrent ? 'Current version' : 'Previous version') + '</div>';
                html += '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--t3);margin-top:2px;">Modified by <strong style="color:var(--t2);">' +
                    (entry.editor || 'Unknown') + '</strong></div></div></div>';
                html += '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--t3);font-weight:600;white-space:nowrap;">' +
                    smHistoryFmtDate(entry.created) + '</div>';
                html += '</div>';

                if (hasChanges) {
                    const showValueOnly = entry.changes.every(function (ch) { return ch.oldVal === '—' || !ch.oldVal; });
                    html += '<table class="sm-history-changes-table"><thead><tr>';
                    if (showValueOnly) {
                        html += '<th style="width:40%;">Field</th><th style="width:60%;">Value</th>';
                    } else {
                        html += '<th style="width:28%;">Field</th><th style="width:36%;">Previous</th><th style="width:36%;">New value</th>';
                    }
                    html += '</tr></thead><tbody>';
                    entry.changes.forEach(function (ch) {
                        html += '<tr><td style="font-weight:700;color:var(--t1);">' + ch.label + '</td>';
                        if (showValueOnly) {
                            html += '<td><span class="sm-history-new">' + ch.newVal + '</span></td></tr>';
                        } else {
                            html += '<td><span class="sm-history-old">' + ch.oldVal + '</span></td>' +
                                '<td><span class="sm-history-new">' + ch.newVal + '</span></td></tr>';
                        }
                    });
                    html += '</tbody></table>';
                } else if (idx === entries.length - 1) {
                    html += '<div style="padding:14px 16px;font-size:13px;color:var(--t3);">Initial item creation — no field details captured.</div>';
                } else {
                    html += '<div style="padding:14px 16px;font-size:13px;color:var(--t3);">No tracked field changes in this version.</div>';
                }
                html += '</div>';
            });

            html += '</div>';
            container.innerHTML = html;
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        }

        async function smBuildItemHistoryEntries(itemId) {
            try {
                return await smBuildItemHistoryFromVersionsPage(itemId);
            } catch (pageErr) {
                console.warn('[smBuildItemHistoryEntries] Versions.aspx parse failed, trying REST', pageErr);
            }
            try {
                const versions = await smFetchItemVersions(itemId);
                if (!versions.length) return [];

                const fieldSets = await Promise.all(versions.map(function (v) {
                    return smFetchVersionFields(itemId, v.ID);
                }));

                return versions.map(function (v, idx) {
                    const fields = fieldSets[idx] || {};
                    const olderFields = idx < versions.length - 1 ? (fieldSets[idx + 1] || {}) : null;
                    const changes = olderFields ? smCompareVersionFields(fields, olderFields) : [];
                    let editor = smEditorFromFields(fields);
                    if (!editor && v.Editor && typeof v.Editor === 'object' && v.Editor.Title) editor = v.Editor.Title;
                    return {
                        versionId: v.ID,
                        versionLabel: smHistoryVersionLabel(v),
                        created: v.Created,
                        editor: editor,
                        changes: changes,
                        isCurrent: idx === 0
                    };
                });
            } catch (restErr) {
                throw new Error('Could not load version history from SharePoint');
            }
        }

        async function smGetListGuid() {
            if (window._SM_LIST_GUID) return window._SM_LIST_GUID;
            const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')?$select=Id";
            const res = await fetch(url, {
                headers: { 'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose' },
                credentials: 'include'
            });
            if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Could not resolve SharePoint list ID');
            const data = await res.json();
            window._SM_LIST_GUID = data.d.Id;
            return window._SM_LIST_GUID;
        }

        async function smShowItemHistory() {
            const account = EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA;
            const code = account && account.code;
            if (!code) { alert('No account selected'); return; }

            const modal = document.getElementById('editHistoryModal');
            const body = document.getElementById('editHistoryModalBody');
            const title = document.getElementById('editHistoryModalTitle');
            if (!modal || !body) return;

            title.textContent = code + (account.customer ? ' · ' + account.customer : '');
            body.innerHTML = '<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px;"><i data-lucide="loader" style="width:24px;height:24px;animation:spin 1s linear infinite;"></i><div style="margin-top:12px;font-size:13px;color:var(--t3);">Loading version history...</div><div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--t3);margin-top:6px;">Fetching each version snapshot from SharePoint…</div></div>';
            modal.style.display = 'flex';
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();

            try {
                let itemId = account.spItemId;
                if (!itemId) itemId = await smFetchListItemId(code);
                account.spItemId = itemId;

                const entries = await smBuildItemHistoryEntries(itemId);
                smRenderItemHistoryTimeline(entries, body);
            } catch (err) {
                console.error('[smShowItemHistory]', err);
                var openLink = '';
                try {
                    var itemId = account.spItemId;
                    if (!itemId) itemId = await smFetchListItemId(code);
                    var listGuid = await smGetListGuid();
                    openLink = SP_URL + '/_layouts/15/Versions.aspx?list=' + encodeURIComponent(listGuid) + '&ID=' + itemId;
                } catch (e) {}
                body.innerHTML = '<div style="color:#ef4444;padding:16px;line-height:1.5;">Error loading item history: ' + err.message +
                    '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--t3);margin-top:8px;">On-prem SharePoint may not expose the REST /versions API. Versioning must be enabled on the Service Manager Request list.</div>' +
                    (openLink ? '<div style="margin-top:12px;"><a href="' + openLink + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener" style="color:var(--accent);font-weight:600;">Open SharePoint Version History</a></div>' : '') +
                    '</div>';
            }
        }

        function smCloseItemHistory() {
            const modal = document.getElementById('editHistoryModal');
            if (modal) modal.style.display = 'none';
        }

        window.smShowItemHistory = smShowItemHistory;
        window.smCloseItemHistory = smCloseItemHistory;

        async function openEditRequest(accountCode) {
            try {
                document.querySelectorAll('.dashboard-section').forEach(function (s) { s.style.display = 'none'; });
                document.getElementById('editRequestView').style.display = 'block';
                var contentDiv = document.querySelector('.content');
                var portalShell = document.querySelector('.portal-shell');
                if (contentDiv) {
                    contentDiv.classList.remove('section-mode');
                    contentDiv.classList.add('edit-full-mode');
                }
                if (portalShell) portalShell.classList.add('edit-full-shell');
                // ✅ STEP 2: NOW reset the button (it exists now)
                const submitBtn = document.querySelector('#editReviewSection button[onclick="submitEditRequest()"]');
                if (submitBtn) {
                    submitBtn.disabled = false;
                    submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="check" style="width: 16px; height: 16px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;"></i>Submit Changes';
                }

                // ✅ STEP 3: Hide review section
                document.getElementById('editReviewSection').style.display = 'none';
                document.getElementById('editSubmitMessage').innerHTML = '';
                document.getElementById('editReviewContent').innerHTML = '';

                // ✅ STEP 4: Clear global variables
                window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA = null;
                EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA = null;

                // ✅ STEP 5: Reset dropdowns
                document.getElementById('editAM').selectedIndex = 0;
                document.getElementById('editAD').selectedIndex = 0;

                // ✅ STEP 6: Load fresh account data
                const account = ALL_DATA.find(a => a.code === accountCode);
                if (!account) {
                    alert('Account not found');
                    return;
                }

                EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA = account;
                window.EDIT_ACCOUNT_CODE = account.code;

                if (!SM_MAPPING_DATA.length) {
                    await fetchAccountMapping();
                }

                const histBtn = document.getElementById('editViewHistoryBtn');
                if (histBtn) histBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';

                // Display current info
                let html = '<div class="edit-section-block">';
                html += '<h3 class="table-title"><i data-lucide="building-2" style="width: 18px; height: 18px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;"></i>Account Information</h3>';
                html += '<div class="edit-info-grid">';
                const fields = [
                    ['Account Code', account.code],
                    ['Customer Name', account.customer],
                    ['Team', account.team],
                    ['Line Manager', account.lm],
                    ['Service Manager', account.sm],
                    ['Account Manager', account.am],
                    ['Account Director', account.ad]
                ];

                fields.forEach(function (pair) {
                    html += '<div class="edit-field-card">' +
                        '<div class="edit-field-label">' + pair[0] + '</div>' +
                        '<div class="edit-field-value">' + (pair[1] || '—') + '</div></div>';
                    if (pair[0] === 'Service Manager') {
                        html += smSecondarySmEditHtml();
                    }
                });

                html += '<div class="edit-field-card">' +
                    '<div class="edit-field-label">Account Type</div>' +
                    '<div class="edit-field-value">' + (account.accountType || '—') + '</div></div>';

                if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) {
                    html += '<div class="edit-field-card">' +
                        '<div class="edit-field-label">RNPS Eligibility</div>' +
                        '<select class="filter-select" id="editRnpsEligibility" style="font-size: 14px; padding: 10px; width: 100%;">' +
                        '<option value="">Select...</option>' +
                        '<option value="Yes"' + (account.rnpsEligibility === 'Yes' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Yes</option>' +
                        '<option value="No"' + (account.rnpsEligibility === 'No' ? ' selected' : '') + '>No</option>' +
                        '</select></div>';
                } else {
                    html += '<div class="edit-field-card">' +
                        '<div class="edit-field-label">RNPS Eligibility</div>' +
                        '<div class="edit-field-value">' + (account.rnpsEligibility || '—') + '</div></div>';
                }

                html += '</div></div>';

                html += '<div class="edit-section-block">';
                html += '<h3 class="table-title"><i data-lucide="bar-chart-3" style="width: 18px; height: 18px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;"></i>Monthly Revenue</h3>';

                const revenueMonths = getRevenueMonthsForEdit();

                html += '<h4>Past 3 Months (Read-Only)</h4>';
                html += '<div class="edit-revenue-grid">';

                revenueMonths.lastThree.forEach(function (month) {
                    const value = account.allMonths ? (account.allMonths[month.field] || 0) : 0;
                    const isLocked = !window.REVENUE_ENABLED;
                    html += '<div class="edit-revenue-card">' +
                        '<div class="edit-field-label">' + month.label + '</div>' +
                        '<input type="number" id="hist_' + month.field + '" value="' + value + '" ' + (isLocked ? 'disabled' : '') +
