                        ' style="width: 100%; padding: 10px; background: var(--bg-input); border: 1px solid var(--border-s); border-radius: 8px; font-size: 16px; font-weight: 700; color: var(--t1); cursor: ' + (isLocked ? 'not-allowed' : 'text') + ';">' +
                        '</div>';
                });
                html += '</div>';

                if (revenueMonths.editable && !window.REVENUE_ENABLED) {
                    const editMonth = revenueMonths.editable;
                    const currentValue = account.allMonths ? (account.allMonths[editMonth.field] || 0) : 0;
                    const isLocked = isMonthLocked(currentValue, editMonth);

                    html += '<h4 style="margin-top: 1.25rem;">' +
                        (isLocked ? 'Previous Month (Locked)' : 'Previous Month (You Can Submit Revenue)') +
                        '</h4>';

                    if (isLocked) {
                        html += '<div class="edit-revenue-card" style="border-color: rgba(16,185,129,.45); background: rgba(16,185,129,.08);">' +
                            '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:8px;">' +
                            '<i data-lucide="lock" style="width:20px;height:20px;color:var(--success);"></i>' +
                            '<div class="edit-field-label" style="color:var(--success);margin:0;">' + editMonth.label + ' — LOCKED</div></div>' +
                            '<div class="edit-field-value" style="font-size:1.25rem;color:var(--success);">' + formatCurrency(currentValue) + '</div>' +
                            '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--t3);margin-top:8px;">Revenue submitted and locked. Contact admin to modify.</div></div>';
                    } else {
                        html += '<div class="edit-revenue-card" style="border-color: var(--accent); background: rgba(168,85,247,.06); margin-top: .5rem;">' +
                            '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:12px;">' +
                            '<i data-lucide="edit-3" style="width:20px;height:20px;color:var(--accent);"></i>' +
                            '<div class="edit-field-label" style="color:var(--accent);margin:0;">' + editMonth.label + ' Revenue</div></div>' +
                            '<input type="number" step="0.01" id="editRevenue_' + editMonth.field + '" value="' + currentValue + '" ' +
                            'style="width:100%;padding:14px;background:var(--bg-input);border:2px solid var(--accent);border-radius:10px;font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:var(--accent);" placeholder="Enter revenue amount">' +
                            '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--t3);margin-top:8px;">Deadline: ' + getDeadlineText(editMonth) + ' | Once submitted, cannot be edited.</div></div>';
                    }
                } else if (!window.REVENUE_ENABLED) {
                    html += '<div class="edit-revenue-card" style="text-align:center;color:var(--danger);margin-top:1rem;">No editable month available (deadline passed).</div>';
                }

                html += '</div>';

                html += '<div class="edit-section-block">';
                html += '<h3 class="table-title"><i data-lucide="users" style="width: 18px; height: 18px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;"></i>POC Details</h3>';
                html += '<div class="filter-group" style="margin-bottom: 1rem; max-width: 360px;">' +
                    '<label class="filter-label">POC Category</label>' +
                    '<select class="filter-select" id="editPocCategory" onchange="renderEditPocFields()" style="font-size: 14px; padding: 10px;">' +
                    '<option value="primary" selected>Primary POC Details</option>' +
                    '<option value="secondary">Secondary POC Details</option>' +
                    '<option value="technical">Technical POC Details</option>' +
                    '</select></div>' +
                    '<div id="editPocFields"></div></div>';

                document.getElementById('editCurrentInfo').innerHTML = html;
                renderEditPocFields();

                if (account.secondarySm) {
                    const mappedExisting = SM_MAPPING_DATA.find(function(a) {
                        return smNormalizePersonName(a.name) === smNormalizePersonName(account.secondarySm);
                    });
                    smSelectSecondarySm(
                        mappedExisting ? mappedExisting.name : account.secondarySm,
                        mappedExisting ? mappedExisting.team : ''
                    );
                } else {
                    smClearSecondarySm();
                }

                // Populate AM/AD dropdowns
                const allAMs = [...new Set(ALL_DATA.map(a => a.am))].filter(Boolean).sort();
                const allADs = [...new Set(ALL_DATA.map(a => a.ad))].filter(Boolean).sort();

                const amSelect = document.getElementById('editAM');
                amSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">Select Account Manager</option>';
                allAMs.forEach(am => {
                    const opt = document.createElement('option');
                    opt.value = am;
                    opt.textContent = am;
                    if (am === account.am) opt.selected = true;
                    amSelect.appendChild(opt);
                });

                const adSelect = document.getElementById('editAD');
                adSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">Select Account Director</option>';
                allADs.forEach(ad => {
                    const opt = document.createElement('option');
                    opt.value = ad;
                    opt.textContent = ad;
                    if (ad === account.ad) opt.selected = true;
                    adSelect.appendChild(opt);
                });

                // Initialize Lucide icons
                if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                    lucide.createIcons();
                }

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Error:', err);
                alert('Error opening edit view: ' + err.message);
            }
        }

        /**
         * Helper: Get deadline text for display
         */
        function getDeadlineText(monthInfo) {
            const deadlineMonth = monthInfo.month + 1;
            const deadlineYear = monthInfo.year;
            const lastDay = new Date(deadlineYear, deadlineMonth + 1, 0);

            const monthNames = ['Jan', 'Feb', 'Mar', 'Apr', 'May', 'Jun', 'Jul', 'Aug', 'Sep', 'Oct', 'Nov', 'Dec'];
            return `${monthNames[lastDay.getMonth()]} ${lastDay.getDate()}, ${deadlineYear}`;
        }
        async function populateEditDropdowns(account) {
            // Get all unique AMs and ADs
            const allAMs = [...new Set(ALL_DATA.map(a => a.am))].filter(Boolean).sort();
            const allADs = [...new Set(ALL_DATA.map(a => a.ad))].filter(Boolean).sort();

            const amSelect = document.getElementById('editAM');
            amSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">Select Account Manager</option>';
            allAMs.forEach(am => {
                const opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = am;
                opt.textContent = am;
                if (am === account.am) opt.selected = true;
                amSelect.appendChild(opt);
            });

            const adSelect = document.getElementById('editAD');
            adSelect.innerHTML = '<option value="">Select Account Director</option>';
            allADs.forEach(ad => {
                const opt = document.createElement('option');
                opt.value = ad;
                opt.textContent = ad;
                if (ad === account.ad) opt.selected = true;
                adSelect.appendChild(opt);
            });
        }

        function renderEditPocFields() {
            const account = EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA;
            if (!account) return;
            const cat = (document.getElementById('editPocCategory') || {}).value || 'primary';
            const wrap = document.getElementById('editPocFields');
            if (!wrap) return;

            const configs = {
                primary: {
                    title: 'Primary POC Details',
                    readOnly: true,
                    fields: [
                        ['POC Name', account.pocName || '—'],
                        ['POC Email', account.pocEmail || '—'],
                        ['POC Contact', account.pocPhone || '—']
                    ]
                },
                secondary: {
                    title: 'Secondary POC Details',
                    readOnly: false,
                    prefix: 'secondary',
                    fields: [
                        ['Secondary POC Name', account.secondaryPocName || ''],
                        ['Secondary POC Email', account.secondaryPocEmail || ''],
                        ['Secondary POC Contact', account.secondaryPocPhone || '']
                    ]
                },
                technical: {
                    title: 'Technical POC Details',
                    readOnly: false,
                    prefix: 'technical',
                    fields: [
                        ['Technical POC Name', account.technicalPocName || ''],
                        ['Technical POC Email', account.technicalPocEmail || ''],
                        ['Technical POC Contact', account.technicalPocPhone || '']
                    ]
                }
            };
            const cfg = configs[cat] || configs.primary;
            let html = '<div class="edit-revenue-card" style="margin-top:.5rem;">';
            html += '<div class="edit-field-label" style="color:var(--accent);margin-bottom:14px;">' + cfg.title + (cfg.readOnly ? ' <span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--t3);font-weight:600;">(Read-only)</span>' : ' <span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--success);font-weight:600;">(Editable)</span>') + '</div>';
            html += '<div class="edit-info-grid" style="grid-template-columns:repeat(3,minmax(0,1fr));">';

            if (cfg.readOnly) {
                cfg.fields.forEach(function (pair) {
                    html += '<div class="edit-field-card"><div class="edit-field-label">' + pair[0] + '</div><div class="edit-field-value">' + (pair[1] || '—') + '</div></div>';
                });
            } else {
                const ids = ['Name', 'Email', 'Contact'];
                cfg.fields.forEach(function (pair, idx) {
                    const inputId = 'edit' + cfg.prefix.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + cfg.prefix.slice(1) + ids[idx];
                    const inputType = idx === 1 ? 'email' : 'text';
                    html += '<div class="filter-group"><label class="filter-label">' + pair[0] + '</label><input type="' + inputType + '" class="filter-select" id="' + inputId + '" value="' + String(pair[1] || '').replace(/"/g, '&quot;') + '" style="cursor:text;font-size:14px;padding:12px 16px;"></div>';
                });
            }
            html += '</div></div>';
            wrap.innerHTML = html;
        }

        function getEditPocChanges() {
            const changes = [];
            if (!EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA) return changes;
            const pairs = [
                ['secondary', 'Secondary POC Name', 'secondaryPocName', 'editSecondaryName'],
                ['secondary', 'Secondary POC Email', 'secondaryPocEmail', 'editSecondaryEmail'],
                ['secondary', 'Secondary POC Contact', 'secondaryPocPhone', 'editSecondaryContact'],
                ['technical', 'Technical POC Name', 'technicalPocName', 'editTechnicalName'],
                ['technical', 'Technical POC Email', 'technicalPocEmail', 'editTechnicalEmail'],
                ['technical', 'Technical POC Contact', 'technicalPocPhone', 'editTechnicalContact']
            ];
            pairs.forEach(function (p) {
                const el = document.getElementById(p[3]);
                if (!el) return;
                const oldVal = EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA[p[2]] || '';
                const newVal = el.value.trim();
                if (newVal !== oldVal) changes.push({ label: p[1], oldVal: oldVal || '—', newVal: newVal || '—', field: p[2] });
            });
            return changes;
        }

        function backFromEditRequest() {
            document.getElementById('editRequestView').style.display = 'none';
            var dashView = document.getElementById('dashboard-view');
            if (dashView) dashView.style.display = 'block';
            var contentDiv = document.querySelector('.content');
            var portalShell = document.querySelector('.portal-shell');
            if (contentDiv) {
                contentDiv.classList.remove('section-mode');
                contentDiv.classList.remove('edit-full-mode');
            }
            if (portalShell) portalShell.classList.remove('edit-full-shell');
            const histBtn = document.getElementById('editViewHistoryBtn');
            if (histBtn) histBtn.style.display = 'none';
            window.EDIT_ACCOUNT_CODE = null;
        }


        function reviewEditRequest() {
            const newAM = document.getElementById('editAM').value;
            const newAD = document.getElementById('editAD').value;
            const newSecondarySm = smNormalizePersonName((document.getElementById('editSecondarySM') || {}).value);
            const oldSecondarySm = smNormalizePersonName(EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.secondarySm);

            if (!newAM || !newAD) {
                alert('Please fill in all required fields');
                return;
            }
            // Collect past 3 months if revenue enabled
            const lastThree = getLastThreeCompletedMonths();
            window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS = [];
            if (window.REVENUE_ENABLED) {
                lastThree.forEach(month => {
                    const inputEl = document.getElementById('hist_' + month.field);
                    if (inputEl) {
                        window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS.push({
                            field: month.field,
                            value: parseFloat(inputEl.value) || 0
                        });
                    }
                });
            }

            // rest of reviewEditRequest continues here...
            const revenueMonths = getRevenueMonthsForEdit();
            let newRevenue = null;
            let revenueField = null;

            if (revenueMonths.editable) {
                const editMonth = revenueMonths.editable;
                const inputId = 'editRevenue_' + editMonth.field;
                const inputEl = document.getElementById(inputId);
                if (inputEl) {
                    newRevenue = parseFloat(inputEl.value);
                    revenueField = editMonth.field;
                    if (isNaN(newRevenue) || newRevenue < 0) {
                        alert('Please enter a valid revenue amount (0 or greater)');
                        return;
                    }
                }
            }

            const amChanged = newAM !== EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.am;
            const adChanged = newAD !== EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.ad;
            const secondarySmChanged = newSecondarySm !== oldSecondarySm;
            const revenueChanged = newRevenue !== null && newRevenue !== (EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.allMonths[revenueField] || 0);
            let newRnpsEligibility = EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.rnpsEligibility || '';
            let rnpsChanged = false;
            if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) {
                const rnpsEl = document.getElementById('editRnpsEligibility');
                newRnpsEligibility = rnpsEl ? rnpsEl.value : (EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.rnpsEligibility || '');
                rnpsChanged = newRnpsEligibility !== (EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.rnpsEligibility || '');
            }

            const pocChanges = getEditPocChanges();
            const pocChanged = pocChanges.length > 0;

            if (!amChanged && !adChanged && !secondarySmChanged && !revenueChanged && !rnpsChanged && !pocChanged && window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS.length === 0) {
                alert('No changes detected');
                return;
            }

            window.EDIT_SECONDARY_SM = newSecondarySm;

            let html = '<div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: 1fr 1fr 1fr; gap: 16px;">';
            const changes = [
                ['Account Code', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.code, EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.code],
                ['Customer', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.customer, EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.customer],
                ['Team', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.team, EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.team],
                ['Line Manager', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.lm, EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.lm],
                ['Service Manager', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.sm, EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.sm],
                ['Secondary SM', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.secondarySm || '—', newSecondarySm || '—'],
                ['Account Manager', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.am, newAM],
                ['Account Director', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.ad, newAD],
                ['Account Type', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.accountType || '—', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.accountType || '—'],
                ['RNPS Eligibility', EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.rnpsEligibility || '—', newRnpsEligibility || '—']
            ];

            if (revenueChanged) {
                const monthLabel = revenueMonths.editable.label;
                const oldValue = EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.allMonths[revenueField] || 0;
                changes.push([`${monthLabel} Revenue`, formatCurrency(oldValue), formatCurrency(newRevenue)]);
            }
            if (window.REVENUE_ENABLED && window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS && window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS.length > 0) {
                window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS.forEach(m => {
                    const oldValue = EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.allMonths[m.field] || 0;
                    if (m.value !== oldValue) {
                        const monthLabel = m.field.replace('_x002d_', '-').replace('_', ' ');
                        changes.push([monthLabel + ' Revenue', formatCurrency(oldValue), formatCurrency(m.value)]);
                    }
                });
            }
            pocChanges.forEach(function (pc) {
                changes.push([pc.label, pc.oldVal, pc.newVal]);
            });
            window.EDIT_POC_CHANGES = pocChanges;
            changes.forEach(([label, oldVal, newVal]) => {
                const hasChanged = oldVal !== newVal;
                html += `<div style="padding: 12px; background: ${hasChanged ? 'rgba(16, 185, 129, 0.15)' : 'rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.1)'}; border-radius: 8px; border: ${hasChanged ? '2px solid var(--success)' : 'none'};">
            <div style="font-size: 11px; color: var(--text-secondary); margin-bottom: 4px; font-weight: 600;">${label}</div>
            <div style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: 600;">${hasChanged ? `${oldVal} <i data-lucide="arrow-right" style="width: 14px; height: 14px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin: 0 4px;"></i> ${newVal}` : newVal}</div>
        </div>`;
            });

            html += '</div>';
            window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA = {
                field: revenueField,
                value: newRevenue
            };
            document.getElementById('editReviewContent').innerHTML = html;
            document.getElementById('editReviewSection').style.display = 'block';
            document.getElementById('editSubmitMessage').innerHTML = '';
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        }

        async function submitEditRequest() {
            const submitBtn = event.target;
            submitBtn.disabled = true;
            submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="loader" style="width: 16px; height: 16px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px; animation: spin 1s linear infinite;"></i>Submitting...';

            try {
                const newAM = document.getElementById('editAM').value;
                const newAD = document.getElementById('editAD').value;
                const newSecondarySm = smNormalizePersonName((document.getElementById('editSecondarySM') || {}).value);
                const oldSecondarySm = smNormalizePersonName(EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.secondarySm);

                // Find item ID
                const searchUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                    "$select=ID&$filter=Title eq '" + EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA.code + "'&$top=1";

                const searchRes = await fetch(searchUrl, {
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });

                if (!searchRes.ok) throw new Error('Cannot find account');
                const searchData = await searchRes.json();
                if (searchData.d.results.length === 0) throw new Error('Account not found');

                const itemId = searchData.d.results[0].ID;

                // Get user IDs
                const amId = await getUserId(newAM);
                const adId = await getUserId(newAD);
                const secondarySmChanged = newSecondarySm !== oldSecondarySm;
                let secondarySmId = null;
                if (secondarySmChanged && newSecondarySm) {
                    secondarySmId = await smResolvePersonId(newSecondarySm);
                    if (!secondarySmId) throw new Error('Could not resolve Secondary SM user: ' + newSecondarySm);
                }

                // Get form digest
                const digestRes = await fetch(SP_URL + "/_api/contextinfo", {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });
                if (!digestRes.ok) throw new Error('Failed to get form digest');
                const digestData = await digestRes.json();
                const digest = digestData.d.GetContextWebInformation.FormDigestValue;

                // Build update data
                const updateUrl = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items(" + itemId + ")";
                const updateData = {
                    __metadata: {
                        type: 'SP.Data.Service_x0020_Manager_x0020_RequestListItem'
                    },
                    Account_x0020_ManagerId: amId,
                    Account_x0020_DirectorId: adId
                };
                if (secondarySmChanged) {
                    const replacingExisting = !!oldSecondarySm && !!newSecondarySm;
                    if (replacingExisting) {
                        // SharePoint on-prem person fields often fail on direct swap — clear first, then set new
                        await smPatchListItem(itemId, digest, { Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_MaId: null });
                        updateData.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_MaId = secondarySmId;
                    } else {
                        updateData.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_MaId = newSecondarySm ? secondarySmId : null;
                    }
                }

                if (window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA && window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA.field) {
                    updateData[window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA.field] = window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA.value;
                }

                if (USER_CONTEXT.isAdmin) {
                    const rnpsEl = document.getElementById('editRnpsEligibility');
                    if (rnpsEl) updateData.RNPS_Eligibility = rnpsEl.value;
                }

                // Save all 3 months if revenue enabled
                if (window.REVENUE_ENABLED && window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS && window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS.length > 0) {
                    window.EDIT_ALL_MONTHS.forEach(m => {
                        updateData[m.field] = m.value;
                    });
                }

                var spPocMap = {
                    secondaryPocName: 'Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Name',
                    secondaryPocEmail: 'Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Email',
                    secondaryPocPhone: 'Secondary_x0020_POC_x0020_Contac',
                    technicalPocName: 'Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Name',
                    technicalPocEmail: 'Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Email',
                    technicalPocPhone: 'Technical_x0020_POC_x0020_Contac'
                };
                (window.EDIT_POC_CHANGES || []).forEach(function (pc) {
                    if (spPocMap[pc.field]) updateData[spPocMap[pc.field]] = pc.newVal === '—' ? '' : pc.newVal;
                });

                const updateRes = await fetch(updateUrl, {
                    method: 'POST',
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose',
                        'Content-Type': 'application/json;odata=verbose',
                        'X-RequestDigest': digest,
                        'IF-MATCH': '*',
                        'X-HTTP-Method': 'MERGE'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include',
                    body: JSON.stringify(updateData)
                });

                if (!updateRes.ok) {
                    const errorText = await updateRes.text();
                    throw new Error('Update failed: ' + errorText);
                }

                document.getElementById('editSubmitMessage').innerHTML = '<span style="color: var(--success);">✅ Account updated successfully!</span>';

                // Clear stored revenue data
                window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA = null;
                EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA = null;
                setTimeout(() => {
                    // RESET EVERYTHING
                    document.getElementById('editReviewSection').style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('editSubmitMessage').innerHTML = '';
                    window.EDIT_REVENUE_DATA = null;
                    EDIT_ACCOUNT_DATA = null;

                    // Reset dropdowns to placeholder
                    document.getElementById('editAM').selectedIndex = 0;
                    document.getElementById('editAD').selectedIndex = 0;
                    smClearSecondarySm();

                    // Clear current info display
                    document.getElementById('editCurrentInfo').innerHTML = '';

                    backFromEditRequest();
                    init();
                }, 2000);

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Error:', err);
                document.getElementById('editSubmitMessage').innerHTML = '<span style="color: var(--danger);">Error: ' + err.message + '</span>';
                submitBtn.disabled = false;
                submitBtn.innerHTML = '<i data-lucide="check" style="width: 16px; height: 16px; display: inline-block; vertical-align: middle; margin-right: 6px;"></i>Submit Changes';
                lucide.createIcons();
            }
        }
        // ========================================
        // ACCOUNT SEARCH FUNCTIONS
        // ========================================

        function showAccountSearch() {
            const landing = document.getElementById('landingPage');
            if (landing) {
                landing.style.display = 'none';
                landing.style.visibility = 'hidden';
                landing.style.position = 'absolute';
                landing.style.zIndex = '-1';
            }
            const dc = document.getElementById('dashboardContent');
            if (dc) dc.style.display = 'none';

            document.getElementById('accountSearchView').style.display = 'block';
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);

            // Sync theme selector with current theme
            const currentTheme = document.body.getAttribute('data-theme');
            const searchSelector = document.getElementById('searchColorSchemeSelector');
            const searchIcon = document.getElementById('searchThemeIcon');

            if (searchSelector) {
                if (currentTheme === 'duralux' || currentTheme === 'duralux-dark') {
                    searchSelector.value = 'duralux';
                } else {
                    searchSelector.value = 'magenta';
                }
            }

            if (searchIcon) {
                if (currentTheme === 'dark' || currentTheme === 'duralux-dark') {
                    searchIcon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'sun');
                } else {
                    searchIcon.setAttribute('data-lucide', 'moon');
                }
            }

            // Initialize Lucide icons
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                lucide.createIcons();
            }
        }

        // ─── COMING SOON VIEWS ──────────────────────────────────────────────
        var ALL_VIEW_IDS = ['dashboardContent', 'landingPage', 'customerServiceView',
            'reviewRequestView', 'transferRequestView', 'sdReviewTransferView',
            'amAdDashboard', 'amTransferRequestsView',
            'createRequestView', 'accountSearchView', 'comingSoonView', 'portalAnalyticsView',
            'editRequestView', 'executiveHubView', 'contactUsView', 'newsletterView'
        ];

        window.showPortalAnalytics = function() {
            ALL_VIEW_IDS.forEach(function(vid) {
                var el = document.getElementById(vid);
                if (el) {
                    el.style.display = 'none';
                    el.style.position = 'absolute';
                    el.style.zIndex = '-1';
                }
            });
            var view = document.getElementById('portalAnalyticsView');
            if (view) {
                view.style.position = '';
                view.style.zIndex = '';
                view.style.display = 'block';
            }
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
            if (typeof analyticsLoadDashboard === 'function') analyticsLoadDashboard();
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        };

        window.showPortalAnalyticsBack = function() {
            var view = document.getElementById('portalAnalyticsView');
            if (view) {
                view.style.display = 'none';
                view.style.position = 'absolute';
                view.style.zIndex = '-1';
            }
            var dc = document.getElementById('dashboardContent');
            if (dc) {
                dc.style.position = '';
                dc.style.zIndex = '';
                dc.style.display = 'block';
            }
            if (typeof switchDashboardSection === 'function') switchDashboardSection('dashboard-view');
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
        };

        window.showComingSoon = function(id, title, icon) {
            if (typeof analyticsTrackPage === 'function') analyticsTrackPage(title);
            ALL_VIEW_IDS.forEach(function(vid) {
                var el = document.getElementById(vid);
                if (el) {
                    el.style.display = 'none';
                    el.style.position = 'absolute';
                    el.style.zIndex = '-1';
                }
            });

            // Update the single shared view
            var view = document.getElementById('comingSoonView');
            document.getElementById('comingSoonTitle').textContent = title;
            document.getElementById('comingSoonHeading').textContent = title;
            document.getElementById('comingSoonIcon').setAttribute('data-lucide', icon);
            document.getElementById('comingSoonBigIcon').setAttribute('data-lucide', icon);

            view.style.position = '';
            view.style.zIndex = '';
            view.style.display = 'block';
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        };

        window.showComingSoonBack = function() {
            var view = document.getElementById('comingSoonView');
            if (view) {
                view.style.display = 'none';
                view.style.position = 'absolute';
                view.style.zIndex = '-1';
            }
            var dc = document.getElementById('dashboardContent');
            if (dc) {
                dc.style.position = '';
                dc.style.zIndex = '';
                dc.style.display = 'block';
            }
            if (typeof switchDashboardSection === 'function') switchDashboardSection('dashboard-view');
            window.scrollTo(0, 0);
            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') lucide.createIcons();
        };

        function backToLanding() {
            document.getElementById('accountSearchView').style.display = 'none';
            const landing = document.getElementById('landingPage');
            if (landing) {
                landing.style.position = '';
                landing.style.visibility = '';
                landing.style.zIndex = '';
                landing.style.display = 'grid';
            }

            // Clear search results
            document.getElementById('searchAccountCode').value = '';
            document.getElementById('accountDetailsSection').style.display = 'none';
            document.getElementById('relatedAccountsSection').style.display = 'none';

            if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                lucide.createIcons();
            }
        }

        async function searchAccount() {
            const accountCode = document.getElementById('searchAccountCode').value.trim();

            if (!accountCode) {
                alert('Please enter an account code');
                return;
            }

            try {
                // Fetch account from SharePoint
                const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                    "$select=Title,Parent_x0020_Code,Customer_x0020_Name,Team," +
                    "Line_x0020_Manager/Title,Service_x0020_Manager/Title," +
                    "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma/Title," +
                    "Account_x0020_Manager/Title,Account_x0020_Director/Title," +
                    "Service_x0020_Director/Title,Jan_x002d_26&" +
                    "$expand=Line_x0020_Manager,Service_x0020_Manager," +
                    "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma,Account_x0020_Manager," +
                    "Account_x0020_Director,Service_x0020_Director&" +
                    "$filter=Title eq '" + accountCode + "'&" +
                    "$top=1";

                const res = await fetch(url, {
                    headers: {
                        'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                    },
                    credentials: 'include'
                });

                if (!res.ok) throw new Error('Failed to search account');

                const data = await res.json();

                if (data.d.results.length === 0) {
                    // Show error message below search box
                    document.getElementById('searchErrorMessage').style.display = 'block';
                    document.getElementById('accountDetailsSection').style.display = 'none';
                    document.getElementById('relatedAccountsSection').style.display = 'none';

                    // Re-initialize Lucide icons
                    if (typeof lucide !== 'undefined') {
                        lucide.createIcons();
                    }
                    return;
                }

                // Hide error message if account found
                document.getElementById('searchErrorMessage').style.display = 'none';

                const account = data.d.results[0];
                displayAccountDetails(account);
                await loadRelatedAccounts(account);

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Search error:', err);
                alert('Error searching account: ' + err.message);
            }
        }

        function displayAccountDetails(account) {
            const isGroup = (account.Title === account.Parent_x0020_Code) || !account.Parent_x0020_Code;

            let html = '<div style="display: grid; grid-template-columns: repeat(3, 1fr); gap: 16px;">';

            const fields = [
                ['Account Code', account.Title],
                ['Parent Code', account.Parent_x0020_Code || account.Title],
                ['Account Type', isGroup ?
                    '<span style="color: var(--success); font-weight: 700; font-size: 16px;">🟢 Group Account</span>' :
                    '<span style="color: var(--accent); font-weight: 700; font-size: 16px;">🔵 Child Account</span>'
                ],
                ['Line Manager', account.Line_x0020_Manager?.Title || 'N/A'],
                ['Service Manager', account.Service_x0020_Manager?.Title || 'N/A'],
                ['Secondary SM', account.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma?.Title || 'N/A'],
                ['Account Manager', account.Account_x0020_Manager?.Title || 'N/A'],
                ['Account Director', account.Account_x0020_Director?.Title || 'N/A'],
                ['Service Director', account.Service_x0020_Director?.Title || 'N/A']
            ];

            fields.forEach(([label, value]) => {
                html += `
            <div style="padding: 12px; background: rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.1); border-radius: 8px;">
                <div style="font-size: 11px; color: var(--text-secondary); margin-bottom: 4px; font-weight: 600;">${label}</div>
                <div style="font-size: 14px; font-weight: 600;">${value}</div>
            </div>
        `;
            });

            html += '</div>';

            document.getElementById('accountDetailsContent').innerHTML = html;
            document.getElementById('accountDetailsSection').style.display = 'block';
        }

        let relatedAccountsGridApi = null;

        async function loadRelatedAccounts(account) {
            const isGroup = (account.Title === account.Parent_x0020_Code) || !account.Parent_x0020_Code;

            try {
                let relatedAccounts = [];
                let titleText = '';

                if (isGroup) {
                    // Show children
                    titleText = 'Child Accounts';
                    const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                        "$select=Title,Parent_x0020_Code,Customer_x0020_Name,Team," +
                        "Line_x0020_Manager/Title,Service_x0020_Manager/Title," +
                        "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma/Title," +
                        "Account_x0020_Manager/Title,Account_x0020_Director/Title," +
                        "Service_x0020_Director/Title,Jan_x002d_26&" +
                        "$expand=Line_x0020_Manager,Service_x0020_Manager," +
                        "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma,Account_x0020_Manager," +
                        "Account_x0020_Director,Service_x0020_Director&" +
                        "$filter=Parent_x0020_Code eq '" + account.Title + "' and Title ne '" + account.Title + "'&" +
                        "$top=500";

                    const res = await fetch(url, {
                        headers: {
                            'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                        },
                        credentials: 'include'
                    });

                    if (res.ok) {
                        const data = await res.json();
                        relatedAccounts = data.d.results;
                    }
                } else {
                    // Show parent
                    titleText = 'Parent/Group Account';
                    const url = SP_URL + "/_api/web/lists/getbytitle('" + SP_LIST + "')/items?" +
                        "$select=Title,Parent_x0020_Code,Customer_x0020_Name,Team," +
                        "Line_x0020_Manager/Title,Service_x0020_Manager/Title," +
                        "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma/Title," +
                        "Account_x0020_Manager/Title,Account_x0020_Director/Title," +
                        "Service_x0020_Director/Title,Jan_x002d_26&" +
                        "$expand=Line_x0020_Manager,Service_x0020_Manager," +
                        "Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma,Account_x0020_Manager," +
                        "Account_x0020_Director,Service_x0020_Director&" +
                        "$filter=Title eq '" + account.Parent_x0020_Code + "'&" +
                        "$top=1";

                    const res = await fetch(url, {
                        headers: {
                            'Accept': 'application/json;odata=verbose'
                        },
                        credentials: 'include'
                    });

                    if (res.ok) {
                        const data = await res.json();
                        relatedAccounts = data.d.results;
                    }
                }

                document.getElementById('relatedAccountsTitle').textContent = titleText;
                renderRelatedAccountsGrid(relatedAccounts, isGroup);
                document.getElementById('relatedAccountsSection').style.display = 'block';

            } catch (err) {
                console.error('Error loading related accounts:', err);
            }
        }

        function renderRelatedAccountsGrid(accounts, isGroup) {
            const gridDiv = document.getElementById('relatedAccountsGrid');

            const columnDefs = [{
                    field: 'Title',
                    headerName: 'Account Code',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 180,
                    pinned: 'left',
                    cellStyle: {
                        fontWeight: '700'
                    }
                },
                {
                    field: 'Parent_x0020_Code',
                    headerName: 'Parent Code',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 180,
                    cellRenderer: params => {
                        const isParentRow = params.value === params.data.Title;
                        return isParentRow ?
                            `<span style="color: var(--success); font-weight: 700;">${params.value}</span>` :
                            params.value;
                    }
                },
                {
                    field: 'accountType',
                    headerName: 'Account Type',
                    filter: 'agSetColumnFilter',
                    width: 140,
                    valueGetter: params => {
                        return params.data.Title === params.data.Parent_x0020_Code ? 'Group' : 'Child';
                    },
                    cellRenderer: params => {
                        const badge = params.value === 'Group' ? 'badge-success' : 'badge-warning';
                        return `<span class="status-badge ${badge}">${params.value}</span>`;
                    }
                },
                {
                    field: 'Customer_x0020_Name',
                    headerName: 'Customer',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 220
                },
                {
                    field: 'Team',
                    headerName: 'Team',
                    filter: 'agSetColumnFilter',
                    width: 120
                },
                {
                    field: 'Line_x0020_Manager.Title',
                    headerName: 'Line Manager',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 160,
                    valueGetter: params => params.data.Line_x0020_Manager?.Title || ''
                },
                {
                    field: 'Service_x0020_Manager.Title',
                    headerName: 'Service Manager',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 160,
                    valueGetter: params => params.data.Service_x0020_Manager?.Title || ''
                },
                {
                    field: 'Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma.Title',
                    headerName: 'Secondary SM',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 160,
                    valueGetter: params => params.data.Secondary_x0020_Service_x0020_Ma?.Title || 'N/A'
                },
                {
                    field: 'Account_x0020_Manager.Title',
                    headerName: 'Account Manager',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 160,
                    valueGetter: params => params.data.Account_x0020_Manager?.Title || ''
                },
                {
                    field: 'Account_x0020_Director.Title',
                    headerName: 'Account Director',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 160,
                    valueGetter: params => params.data.Account_x0020_Director?.Title || ''
                },
                {
                    field: 'Service_x0020_Director.Title',
                    headerName: 'Service Director',
                    filter: 'agTextColumnFilter',
                    width: 160,
                    valueGetter: params => params.data.Service_x0020_Director?.Title || ''
                }
            ];

            const gridOptions = {
                columnDefs: columnDefs,
                rowData: accounts,
                defaultColDef: {
                    sortable: true,
                    filter: true,
                    resizable: true,
                    minWidth: 100
                },
                rowHeight: 50,
                headerHeight: 52,
                animateRows: true,
                enableCellTextSelection: true,
                pagination: true,
                paginationPageSize: 50,
                paginationPageSizeSelector: [25, 50, 100],
                onGridReady: params => {
                    relatedAccountsGridApi = params.api;
                },
                getRowStyle: params => {
                    // Alternate row colors with theme support
                    const isDark = document.body.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'dark' ||
                        document.body.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'duralux-dark';

                    if (params.node.rowIndex % 2 === 0) {
                        return {
                            background: isDark ? 'rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.08)' : 'rgba(168, 85, 247, 0.05)'
                        };
                    }
                    return null;
                }
            };

            if (relatedAccountsGridApi) {
                relatedAccountsGridApi.destroy();
            }

            gridDiv.innerHTML = '';
            agGrid.createGrid(gridDiv, gridOptions);
        }

        function searchRelatedAccounts(searchText) {
            if (!relatedAccountsGridApi) return;
            relatedAccountsGridApi.setGridOption('quickFilterText', searchText);
        }
